niyatikṛtaniyamarahitāṃ hlādaikamayīmananyaparatantrām । navarasarucirāṃ nirmitimādadhatī bhāratī kaverjayati ।। niyatiśaktyā niyatarūpā sukhaduḥkhamohasvabhāvā paramāṇvādyupādānakarmādisahakārikāraṇaparatantrā ṣaḍrasā na ca hṛdyaiva taiḥ, tādṛśī brahmaṇo nirmitirnirmāṇam । etadvilakṣaṇā tu kavivāṅnirmitiḥ । ata eva jayati । jayatyarthena ca namaskāra ākṣipyate iti tāṃ pratyasmi praṇata iti labhyate ।। kāvyaṃ yaśase arthakṛte vyavahāravide śivetarakṣataye ।
sadyaḥ paranirvṛtaye kāntāsaṃmitatayopadeśayuje ।। kālidāsādīnāmiva yaśaḥ śrīharṣāderdhāvakādīnāmiva dhanam rājādigatocitācāraparijñānam ādityādermayūrādīnāmivānarthanivāraṇam । sakalaprayojanamaulibhūtaṃ samanantarameva rasāsvādana-samudbhūtaṃ vigalitavedyāntaramānandam prabhusaṃmitaśabdapradhānavedādiśāstrebhyaḥ śabdārthayorguṇabhāvena rasāṅgabhūtavyāpārapravaṇatayā vilakṣaṇaṃ yat kāvyaṃ lokottaravarṇanānipuṇakavikarma tat kānteva sarasatāpādanenābhimukhīkṛtya rāmādivadvartitavyaṃ na rāvaṇādivadityupadeśaṃ ca yathāyogaṃ kaveḥ sahṛdayasya ca karotīti sarvathā tatra yatanīyam ।। śaktirnipuṇatā lokaśāstrakāvyādyavekṣaṇāt ।
kāvyajñaśikṣayābhyāsa iti hetustadudbhave ।। śaktiḥ kavitvabījarūpaḥ saṃskāraviśeṣaḥ yāṃ vinā kāvyaṃ na prasaret prasṛtaṃ vā upahasanīyaṃ syāt । lokasya sthāvarajaṅgamātmakalokavṛttasya । śāstrāṇāṃ chandovyākaraṇābhidhānakośakalācaturvargagajaturagakhaḍgādilakṣaṇagranthānām । kāvyānāṃ ca mahākavisaṃbandhinām । ādigrahaṇāditihāsānāṃ ca vimarśanādvyutpattiḥ । kāvyaṃ kartuṃ vicārayituṃ ca ye jānanti tadupadeśena karaṇe yojane ca paunaḥpunyena pravṛttiriti । trayaḥ samuditāḥ na tu vyastāḥ tasya kāvyasyodbhave nirmāṇe samullāse ca heturna tu hetavaḥ ।। tadadoṣau śabdārthau saguṇāvanalaṅkṛtī punaḥ kvāpi । doṣaguṇālaṅkārāḥ vakṣyante । kvāpītyanenaitadāha yat sarvatra
sālaṅkārau kvacittu sphuṭālaṅkāravirahe api na kāvyatvahāniḥ । conmīlitamālatīsurabhayaḥ prauḍhāḥ kadambānilāḥ । revārodhasi vetasītarutale cetaḥ samutkaṇṭhate ।।} atra sphuṭo na kaścidalaṅkāraḥ । rasasya ca prādhānyānnālaṅkāratā ।
idamuttamamatiśayini vyaṅgye vācyāddhvanirbudhaiḥ kathitaḥ ।। idamiti kāvyam । budhairvaiyākaraṇaiḥ pradhānabhūtasphoṭarūpavyaṅgyavyañjakasya śabdasya dhvanir iti vyavahāraḥ kṛtaḥ । tatastanmatānusāribhiranyairapi nyagbhāvitavācyavyaṅgyavyañjanakṣamasya śabdārthayugalasya । netre dūramanañjane pulakitā tanvī tavayaṃ tanuḥ । vāpīṃ snātumito gatāsi na punastasyādhamasyāntikam ।।}
atra tadantikameva rantuṃ gatāsīti prādhānyenādhamapadena vyajyate ।। atādṛśi guṇībhūtavyaṅgyaṃ vyaṅgye tu madhyamam । atādṛśi vācyādanatiśāyini । yathā {grāmataruṇaṃ taruṇyā navavañjulamañjarīsanāthakaram ।
paśyantyā bhavati muhurnitarāṃ malinā mukhacchāyā ।।} tadapekṣayā vācyasyaiva camatkāritvāt ।। śabdacitraṃ vācyacitramavyaṅgyaṃ tvavaraṃ smṛtam ।। citramiti guṇālaṅkārayuktam । avyaṅgyamiti sphuṭapratīyamānārtharahitam ।
avaram adhamam । yathā mūrchanmohamaharṣiharṣavihitasnānāhnikāhnāya vaḥ । drohodrekamahormimeduramadā mandākinī mandatām ।।} {vinirgataṃ mānadamātmamandirād bhavatyupaśrutya yadṛcchayāpi yam ।
sasaṃbhramendrradrutapātitārgalā nimīlitākṣīva bhiyāmarāvatī ।।} prathama ullāsaḥ ।। syādvācako lākṣaṇikaḥ śabdo atra vyañjakastridhā । atreti kāvye । eṣāṃ svarūpaṃ vakṣyate ।।
vācyalakṣyavyaṅgyāḥ ।। tātparyārtho api keṣucit ।। ākāṅkṣāyogyatāsaṃnidhivaśādvakṣyamāṇasvarūpāṇāṃ padārthānāṃ samanvaye tātparyārtho viśeṣavapurapadārtho api vākyaārthaḥ samullasatītyabhihitānvayavādināṃ matam ।। vācya eva vākyārtha ityanvitābhidhānavādinaḥ ।।
sarveṣāṃ prāyaśo arthānāṃ vyañjakatvamapīṣyate । {māe gharovaaraṇaṃ ajja hu ṇatthi tti sāhiaṃ tumae । tā bhaṇa kiṃ karaṇijjaṃ emea ṇa vāsaro ṭhāi ।।} [mātaḥ gṛhopakaraṇaṃ adya khalu nāstīti sādhitaṃ tvayā ।
tadbhaṇa kiṃ karaṇīyaṃ evameva na vāsaraḥ sthīyī ।।] atra svairavihārārthinīti vyajyate । {sāhentī sahi suhaaṃ khaṇe khaṇe dummiāsi majjhakae । sabbhāvaṇehakaraṇijjasarisaaṃ dāva viraiaṃ tumae ।।}
[sādhayantī sakhi subhagaṃ kṣaṇekṣaṇe dūnā'si matkṛte । sadbhāvasnehakaraṇīyasadṛśaṃ tāvat viracitaṃ tvayā ।।] atra matpriyaṃ ramayantyā tvayā śatrutvamācaritamiti lakṣyam । tena ca kāmukaviṣayaṃ sāparādhatvaprakāśanaṃ vyaṅgyam । vyaṅgyasya yathā {ua ṇiccalaṇippandā bhisiṇīpattammi rehai valāā ।
ṇimmalamaragaabhāaṇapariṭṭiā saṃkhasuttivva ।।} [paśya niścalaniṣpandā visinīptre rājate balākā । nirmalamarakatabhājanaparisthitā śaṅkhaśuktiriva ।।] atra niṣpandatvena āśvastatvam । tena ca janarahitatvam । ataḥ saṃketasthānametaditi kayācit kañcitpratyucyate । athavā mithyā vadasi na tvamatrāgatobhūriti vyajyate ।।
vācakādīnāṃ krameṇa svarūpamāha । sākṣātsaṃketitaṃ yo arthamabhidhatte sa vācakaḥ ।। ihāgṛhītasaṃketasya śabdasyārthapratīterabhāvātsaṃketasahāya eva śabdo arthaviśeṣaṃ pratipādayatīti yasya yatrāvyavadhānena saṃketo gṛhyate sa tasya vācakaḥ ।। saṅketitaścaturbhedo jātyādirjātireva vā ।
gauḥ śuklaścalo ḍittha ityādīnāṃ viṣayavibhāgo na prāpnotīti ca । tadupādhāveva saṃketaḥ । upādhiśca dvividhaḥ vastudharmo vaktṛyadṛcchāsaṃniveśitaśca । vastudharmo api dvividhaḥ siddhaḥ sādhyaśca । siddho api dvividhaḥ padārthasya prāṇaprado viśeṣādhānahetuśca । uktaṃ hi vākyapadīye {na hi gauḥ svarūpeṇa gaurnāpyagauḥ । gotvābhisaṃvandhātu gauḥ} iti । dvitīyo guṇaḥ । śuklādinā hi labdhasattākaṃ vastu viśiṣyate । sādhyaḥ pūrvāparībhūtāvayavaḥ kriyārūpaḥ ।
ḍitthādiśabdānāmantyabuddhinirgrāhyaṃ saṃhṛtakramaṃ svarūpaṃ vaktrā tadṛcchayā ḍitthādiṣvartheṣūpādhitvena saṃniveśyata iti so ayaṃ saṃjñārūpo yadṛcchātmaka iti । {gauḥśuklaścalo ḍittha ityādau catuṣṭayī śabdānāṃ pravṛttiḥ} iti mahābhāṣyakāraḥ । paramāṇvādīnāṃ tu guṇamadhyapāṭhāt pāribhāṣikaṃ guṇatvam । guṇakriyāyadṛcchānāṃ vastuta ekarūpāṇām apyāśrayabhedād bheda iva lakṣyate । yathaikasya mukhasya khaḍgamukuratailādyālambanabhedāt । himapayaḥśaṅkhādyāśrayeṣu paramārthato bhinneṣu śuklādiṣu yadvaśena śuklaḥ śukla ityādyabhinnābhidhānapratyayotpattistat śuklatvādi sāmānyam । guḍataṇḍulādipākādiṣvevameva pākatvādi । bālavṛddhaśukādyudīriteṣu ḍitthādiśabdeṣu ca pratikṣaṇaṃ bhidyamāneṣu ḍitthādya'rtheṣu vā ḍitthatvādyastīti sarveṣāṃ śabdānāṃ jātireva pravṛttinimittamityanye । tadvān apoho vā śabdārthaḥ kaiściduktaṃ iti granthagauravabhayāt prakṛtānupayogācca na darśitam ।।
sa mukhyo arthastatra mukhyo vyāpāro asyābhidhocyate ।। sa iti sākṣātsaṃketitaḥ ।। mukhyārthabādhe tadyoge rūḍhito atha prayojanāt । anyo artho lakṣyate yatsā lakṣaṇāropitā kriyā ।।
lakṣaṇā ।। svāsiddhaye parākṣepaḥ parārthaṃ svasamarpaṇam । upādānaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cetyuktā śuddhaiva sā dvidhā ।। {kuntāḥ praviśanti} {yaṣṭayaḥ praviśanti} ityādau kuntādibhirātmanaḥ praveśasiddhyarthaṃ svasaṃyoginaḥ puruṣā ākṣipyante । tata upādānene ayaṃ lakṣaṇā ।
{viśeṣyaṃ nābhidhā gacchet kṣīṇaśaktirviśeṣaṇe} iti nyāyādityupādānalakṣaṇā tu nodāhartavyā । na hyatra prayojanamasti na vā rūḍhiriyam । vyaktyavinābhāvitvāttu jātyā vyaktirākṣipyate । yathā kriyatāmityatra kartā । praviśa piṇḍīmityādau gṛhaṃ bhakṣayetyādi ca । {pīno devadatto divā na bhuṅkte} ityatra ca rātribhojanaṃ na lakṣyate śrutārthāpatterarthāpattervā tasya viṣayatvāt । {gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣaḥ} ityatra taṭasya ghoṣādhikaraṇatvasiddhaye gaṅgāśabdaḥ svārthamarpayati ityevamādau lakṣaṇenaiṣā lakṣaṇā । ubhayarūpā ceyaṃ śuddhā । upacāreṇāmiśritatvāt ।
anayorlakṣyasya lakṣakasya ca na bhedarūpaṃ tāṭasthyam । taṭādīnāṃ gaṅgādiśabdaiḥ pratipādane tattvapratipattau hi pratipipādayiṣitaprayojanasaṃpratyayaḥ । gaṅgāsaṃbandhamātrapratītau tu gaṅgātaṭe ghoṣa iti mukhyaśabdābhidhānāllakṣaṇāyāḥ ko bhedaḥ ।। sāropānyā tu yatroktau viṣayī viṣayastathā । āropyamāṇaḥ āropaviṣayaśca yatrānapahnutabhedau sāmānādhikaraṇyena nirdiśyete sā lakṣaṇā sāropā ।। viṣyayyantaḥkṛte anyasmin sā syātsādhyavasānikā ।।
viṣayiṇāropyamāṇenāntaḥkṛte nigīrṇe anyasminnāropaviṣaye sati sādhyavasānā syāt ।। bhedāvimau ca sādṛśyātsambandhāntaratastathā । imāvāropādhyavasānarūpau sādṛśyahetū bhedau {gaurvāhīkaḥ} ityatra {gaurayam} ityatra ca । atra hi svārthasahacāriṇo guṇā jāḍyamāndyādayo lakṣyamāṇā api gośabdasya parārthābhidhāne pravṛttinimittatvamupayāntiṃ iti kecit । svārthasahacāriguṇābhedena padārthagatā guṇā eva lakṣyante na
parārtho abhidhīyate ityanye । sādhāraṇaguṇāśrayatvena parārtha eva lakṣyate ityapare । {abhidheyāvinābhūtapratītirlakṣaṇocyate । lakṣyamāṇaguṇairyogādvṛtteriṣṭā tu gauṇatāṃ} iti । avinābhāvo atra saṃbandhamātraṃ na tu nāntarīyakatvam । tattve hi {mañcāḥ krośanti} ityādau na lakṣaṇā syāt ।
avinābhāve cākṣepeṇaiva siddherlakṣaṇāyā nopayoga ityuktam । {āyurdhṛtam} {āyurevedam} ityādau ca sādṛśyādanyat kāryakāraṇabhāvādi saṃbandhāntaram । evamādau ca kāryakāraṇabhāvādilakṣaṇapūrve āropādhyavasāne । atra gauṇabhedayorbhede api tādrūpyapratītiḥ sarvathaivābhedāvagamaśca prayojanam । śuddhabhedayostvanyavailakṣaṇyenāvyabhicāreṇa ca kāryakāritvādi । kvacit tādarthyādupacāraḥ । yathā indrārthā sthūṇā indraḥ । kvacit svasvāmibhāvāt । yathā rājakīyaḥ puruṣo rājā । kvacit avayavāvayavibhāvāt । yathā agrahasta ityatrāgramātre avayave hastaḥ । kvacit tātkarmyāt । yathā atakṣā takṣā ।।
lakṣaṇā tena ṣaḍvidhā ।। ādyabhedābhyāṃ saha ।। vyaṅgyena rahitā rūḍhau sahitā tu prayojane । prayojanaṃ hi vyañjanavyāpāragamyameva ।।
tacceti vyaṅgyam । gūḍhaṃ yathā samucchalitavibhramā gatirapāstasaṃsthā matiḥ । batenduvadanātanau taruṇimodgamo modate ।।} {śrīparicayājjaḍā api bhavantyabhijñā vidagdhacaritānām ।
upadiśati kāminīnāṃ yauvanamada eva lalitāni ।।} atropadiśatīti ।। tadeṣā kathitā tridhā ।। avyaṅgyā gūḍhavyaṅgyā agūḍhavyaṅgyā ca ।।
śabda iti saṃbadhyate ।। tatra vyāpāro vyañjanātmakaḥ । yasya pratītimādhātuṃ lakṣaṇā samupāsyate ।। phale śabdaikagamye atra vyañjanānnāparā kriyā ।
prayojanapratipipādayiṣayā yatra lakṣaṇayā śabdaprayogastatra nānyatastatpratītirapi tu tasmādeva śabdāt । na cātra vyañjanādṛte anyo vyāpāraḥ ।। gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau ye pāvanatvādayo dharmāstaṭādau pratīyante na tatra gaṅgādiśabdāḥ saṃketitāḥ ।। hetvabhāvānna lakṣaṇā ।।
mukhyārthabādhāditrayaṃ hetuḥ ।। lakṣyaṃ na mukhyaṃ nāpyatra bādho yogaḥ phalena no । na prayojanametasmin na ca śabdaḥ skhaladgatiḥ ।। yathā gaṅgāśabdaḥ srotasi sabādha iti taṭaṃ lakṣayati tadvat yadi taṭe api sabādhaḥ syāt tat prayojanaṃ lakṣayet ।
na ca taṭaṃ mukhyo arthaḥ । na ca gaṅgāśabdārthasya taṭasya pāvanatvādyairlakṣaṇīyaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ । nāpi prayojane lakṣye kiñcit prayojanam । nāpi gaṅgāśabdastaṭamiva prayojanaṃ pratipādayitumasamarthaḥ ।। evamapyanavasthā syād yā mūlakṣayakāriṇī । evamapi prayojanaṃ cellakṣyate tat prayojanāntareṇeti tadapi prayojanāntareṇeti prakṛtāpratītikṛt anavasthā bhavet ।। nanu pāvanatvādidharmayuktameva taṭaṃ lakṣyate । {gaṅgāyāstaṭe ghoṣaḥ} ityato adhikasyārthasya pratītiśca prayojanamiti viśiṣṭe lakṣaṇā tatkiṃ vyañjanayetyāha
prayojanena sahitaṃ lakṣaṇīyaṃ na yujyate ।। jñānasya viṣayo hyanyaḥ phalamanyadudāhṛtam । pratyakṣādernīlādirviṣayaḥ phalaṃ tu prakṭatā saṃvittirvā ।। vyākhyātam ।।
viśeṣāḥ syustu lakṣite ।। taṭādau viśeṣāḥ pāvanatvādayaste cābhidhātātparyalakṣaṇābhyo vyāpārāntareṇa gamyāḥ । tacca vyañjanadhvananadyotanādiśabdavācyamavaśyameṣitavyam ।। evaṃ lakṣaṇāmūlaṃ vyañjakatvamuktam ।। abhidhāmūlaṃ tvāha anekārthasya śabdasya vācakatve niyantrite ।
saṃyogādyairavācyārthadhīkṛdvyāpṛtirañjanam ।। {saṃyogo viprayogaśca sāhacaryaṃ virodhitā । arthaḥ prakaraṇaṃ liṅgaṃ śabdasyānyasya saṃnidhiḥ ।। sāmarthyamaucitī deśaḥ kālo vyaktiḥ svarādayaḥ ।
śabdārthasyānavacchede viśeṣasmṛtihetavaḥ ।।} saśaṅkhacakro hariḥ aśaṅkhacakro harirityucyate । rāmalakṣmaṇāviti dāśarathau । rāmārjunagatistayoriti bhārgavakārtavīryayoḥ । sthāṇuṃ bhaja bhavacchide, iti hare । sarvaṃ jānāti deva iti yuṣmadarthe । kupito makaradhvaja iti kāme । devasya purārāteriti śaṃbhau । madhunā mattaḥ kokila iti vasante । pātu vo dayitāmukhamiti sāṃmukhye । bhātyatra parameśvara iti rājadhānīrūpāt deśādrājani । citrabhānurvibhātīti dine ravau rātrau vahnau । mitraṃ bhātīti suhṛdi mitro bhātīti ravau । indraśatrurityādau vede eva na kāvye svaro viṣeṣapratītikṛt ।
{eddahamettatthaṇiā eddahamettehi acchivattehiṃ । eddahamettāvatthā eddahamettehiṃ diaehiṃ ।।} [etāvanmātrastankā etāvanmātrābhyāmakṣipatrābhyām । etāvanmātrāvasthā etāvanmātrairdivasaiḥ ।।]
ityādāvabhinayādayaḥ । itthaṃ saṃyogādibhirarthāntarābhidhāyakatve nivārite apyanekārthasya śabdasya yat kvacidarthāntarapratipādanaṃ tatra nābhidhā niyamanāttasyāḥ । na ca lakṣaṇā mukhyārthabādhādyabhāvāt । api tvañjanaṃ vyañjanameva vyāpāraḥ । yathā vaṃśonnateḥkṛtaśilīmukhavigrahasya । dānāmbusekasubhagaḥ satataṃ karobhūt ।।}
।। yatso arthāntarayuk tathā । artho api vyañjakastatra sahakāritayā mataḥ ।। tatheti vyañjakaḥ ।।
iti kāvyaprakāśe śabdārthasvarūpanirṇayo nāma dvitīya ullāsaḥ ।। arthāḥ vācyalakṣyavyaṅgyāḥ । teṣāṃ vācakalākṣaṇikavyañjakānām ।। arhtavyañjakatocyate । vaktṛboddhavyakākūnāṃ vākyavācyānyasannidheḥ ।।
prastāvadeśakālādervaiśiṣṭyāt pratibhājuṣām । yo arthasyānyārthadhīheturvyāpāro vyaktireva sā ।। boddhavyaḥ pratipādyaḥ । kākurdhvanervikāraḥ । prastāvaḥ prakaraṇam । arthasya vācyalakṣyavyaṅgyātmanaḥ ।
krameṇodāharaṇāni । {aipihulaṃ jalakuṃbhaṃ ghettūṇa samāgadahmi sahi turiaṃ । samaseasalilaṇīsāsaṇīsahā vīsamāmi khaṇaṃ ।।} [atipṛthulaṃ jalakumbhaṃ gṛhītvā samāgatāsmi sakhi tvaritam ।
śramasvedasalilaniḥśvāsaniḥsahā viśrāmyāmi kṣaṇam ।।] atra cauryaratahopanaṃ gamyate । {oṇṇiddaṃ dobballaṃ cintā alasattaṇaṃ saṇīsasiaṃ । maha mandabhāiṇīe keraṃ sahi tuha vi ahaha parihavai ।।}
[aunnidryaṃ daurbalyaṃ cintālasatvaṃ saniścasitam । mama mandabhāginyāḥ krṭe sakhi tvāmapyahaha paribhavati ।।] atra dūtyāstatkāmukopabhogo vyajyate । vane vyādhaiḥ sārdhaṃ suciramuṣitaṃ valkaladharaiḥ ।
guruḥ khedaṃ khinne mayi bhajati nādyāpi kuruṣu ।।} atra mayi na yogyaḥ khedaḥ kuruṣu tu yogya iti kākvā prakāśyate । na ca vācyasiddhyaṅgamatra kākuriti guṇībhūtavyaṅgyatvaṃ śaṅgyam । praśnamātreṇāpi kākorviśrānteḥ ।
{taiā maha gaṇḍatthalaṇimiaṃ diṭṭhiṃ ṇa ṇesi aṇṇatto । eṇhiṃ saccea ahaṃ te a kavālā ṇa sā diṭṭhī ।।} [tadā mama gaṇḍasthalanimagnāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ nānaiṣīratnyatra । idānīṃ saivāhaṃ tau ca kapolau na ca sā dṛṣṭiḥ ।।]
atra matsakhīṃ kapolapratibimbitāṃ paśyataste dṛṣṭiranyaivābhūt calitāyāṃ tu tasyāmanyaiva jātetyaho pracchannakāmukatvaṃ te iti vyajyate । kuñjotkarṣāṅkuritaramaṇīvibhramo narmadāyāḥ । yeṣāmagre sarati kalitākāṇḍakopo manobhūḥ ।।} atra ratārthaṃ praviśeti vyaṅgyam ।
{ṇollei aṇollamaṇā attā maṃ gharabharammi saalammi । khaṇamettaṃ jai saṃjhāi hoi ṇa va hoi vīsāmo ।।} [nudatyanārdramanāḥ śvaśrūrmāṃ gṛhabhare sakale । kṣaṇamātraṃ yadi saṃdhyāyāṃ bhavati na vā bhavati viśrāmaḥ ।।]
atra saṃdhyā saṃketakāla iti taṭasthaṃ prati kayāciddyotyate । {suvvai samāgamissadi tujjha pio añjaṃ paharametteṇa । eme a kitti ciṭṭhasi tā sahi sañjesu karaṇijjaṃ ।।} [śrūyate samāgamiṣyati tava priyo adya praharamātreṇa ।
evameva kimiti tiṣṭhasi tat sakhi sajjaya karaṇīyam ।।] atropapatiṃ pratyabhisartuṃ prastutā na yuktamiti kayācinnivāryate । {anyatra yūyaṃ kusumāvacāyaṃ kurudhvamatrāsmi karomi sakhyaḥ । nāhaṃ hi dūraṃ bhramituṃ samarthā prasīdatāyaṃ racitoñjalirvaḥ ।।}
atra vivikto ayaṃ deśa iti pracchannakāmukastvayābhisāryatāmiti āśvastāṃ prati kayācinnivedyate । {guruaṇaparavasa pia kiṃ bhaṇāmi tui mandabhāiṇī ahaaṃ । ajja pavāsaṃ vaccasi vacca saaṃ jevva suṇasi karaṇijjaṃ ।।} [gurujanaparavaśa priya kiṃ bhaṇāmi tava mandabhāginī ahakam ।
adya pravāsaṃ vrajasi vraja svayameva śroṣyasi karaṇīyam ।।] tava tu na jānāmi gatimiti vyajyate ।। ādigrahaṇācceṣṭādeḥ । tatra ceṣṭāyā yathā prollāsyoruyugaṃ parasparasamāsaktaṃ samāsāditam ।
vācastatra nivāritaṃ prasaraṇaṃ saṃkocite dorlate ।।} atra ceṣṭayā pracchannakāntaviṣaya ākūtaviśeṣo dhvanyate । nirākāṅkṣapratipattaye prāptāvasaratayā ca punaḥ punarudāhriyate । vaktrādīnāṃ mithaḥsaṃyoge dvikādibhedena । anena krameṇa lakṣyavyaṅgyayośca vyañjakatvamudāhāryam ।।
śabdapramāṇavedyo artho vyanaktyarthāntaraṃ yataḥ । arthasya vyañjakatve tacchabdasya sahakāritā ।। śabdeti । nahi pramāṇāntaravedyo artho vyañjakaḥ ।। iti śrīkāvyaprakāśe arthavyañjakatānirṇayo nāma tṛtīya ullāsaḥ ।।
avivakṣitavācyo yastatra vācyaṃ bhaveddhvanau । arthāntare saṅkramitamatyantaṃ vā tiraskṛtam ।। lakṣaṇāmūlagūḍhavyaṅgyaprādhānye satyeva avivakṣitaṃ vācyaṃ yatra sa adhvanau'; ityanuvādāt dhvaniriti jñeyaḥ । tatra ca vācyaṃ kvacidanupayujyamānatvādarthāntare pariṇamitam । yathā
{tvāmasmi vacmi viduṣāṃ samavāyo atra tiṣṭhati । ātmīyāṃ matimāsthāya sthitimatra vidhehi tat ।।} atra vacanādi upadeśādirūpatayā pariṇamati । kvacidanupapadyamānatayā atyantaṃ tiraskṛtam । yathā
{upakṛtaṃ bahu tatra kimucyate sujanatā prathitā bhavatā param । vidadhadīdṛśameva sadā sakhe sukhitamāssva tataḥ śaradāṃ śatam ।।} etad apakāriṇaṃ prati viparītalakṣaṇayā kaścidvakti ।। vivakṣitaṃ cānyaparaṃ vācyaṃ yatrāparastu saḥ ।
anyaparaṃ vyaṅgyaniṣṭham । eṣa ca ko apyalakṣyakramavyaṅgyo lakṣyavyaṅgyakramaḥ paraḥ ।। alakṣyeti । na khalu vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicāriṇa eva rasaḥ । api tu rasastaiḥ ityasti kramaḥ । sa tu lāghavānna lakṣyate ।। rasabhāvatadābhāvabhāvaśāntyādirakramaḥ ।
bhinno rasādyalaṅkārādalaṅkāryatayā sthitaḥ ।। ādigrahaṇād bhāvodayabhāvasaṃdhibhāvaśabalatvāni । pradhānatayā yatra sthito rasādistatrālaṅkāryaḥ yathodāhariṣyate । anyatra tu pradhāne vākyārthe yatrāṅgabhūto rasādistatra guṇībhūtavyaṅgye rasavatpreyaūrjasvisamāhitādayo alaṅkārāḥ । te ca guṇībhūtavyaṅgyābhidhāne udāhariṣyante ।। kāraṇānyatha kāryāṇi sahakārīṇi yāni ca ।
ratyādeḥ sthāyino loke tāni cennāṭyakāvyayoḥ ।। vibhāvā anubhāvāstat kathyante vyabhicāriṇaḥ । vyaktaḥ sa tairvibhāvādyaiḥ sthāyī bhāvo rasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। etadvivṛṇvate {vibhāvairlalanodyānādibhirālambanoddīpanakāraṇaiḥ ratyādiko bhāvo janitaḥ anubhāvaiḥ kaṭākṣabhujākṣepaprabhṛtibhiḥ kāryaiḥ pratītiyogyaḥ kṛtaḥ vyabhicāribhirnirvedādibhiḥ sahakāribhirupacito mukhyayā vṛttyā rāmādāvanukārye tadrūpasaṃdhānānnartake api pratīyamāno rasaḥ} iti bhaṭṭalollaṭaprabhṛtayaḥ ।
{seyaṃ mamāṅgeṣu sudhārasacchaṭā supūrakarpūraśalākikā dṛśoḥ । manorathaśrīrmanasaḥ śarīriṇī prāṇeśvarī locanagocaraṃ gatā ।।} {daivādahamadya tayā capalāyatanetrayā viyuktaśca । aciralavilolajaladaḥ kālaḥ samupāgataścāyam ।।}
ityādikāvyānusaṃdhānabalācchikṣābhyāsanirvartitasvakāryaprakaṭanena ca naṭenaiva prakāśitaiḥ kāraṇakāryasahakāribhiḥ kṛtrimairapi tathānabhimanyamānairvibhāvādiśabdavyapadeśyaiḥ {saṃyogāt}, gamyagamakabhāvarūpāt anumīyamāno api vastusaudaryabalādrasanīyatvenānyānumīyamānavilakṣaṇaḥ sthāyitvena saṃbhāvyamāno ratyādirbhāvastatrāsannapi sāmājikānāṃ vāsanayā carvyamāṇo rasa iti śrīśaṅkukaḥ । na tāṭasthyena nātmagatatvena rasaḥ pratīyate notpadyate nābhivyajyate api tu kāvye nāṭye cābhidhāto dvitīyena vibhāvādisādhāraṇīkaraṇātmanā bhāvakatvavyāpāreṇa bhāvyamānaḥ sthāyī sattvodrekaprakāśānandamayasaṃvidviśrāntisatattvena bhogena bhujyate iti bhaṭṭanāyakaḥ । sarvamiva tirodadhat brahmāsvādamivānubhāvayan alaukikacamatkārakārī śṛṅgārādiko rasaḥ । vibhāvādivināṃśe api tasya saṃbhavaprasaṅgāt । nāpi jñāpyaḥ siddhasya tasyāsaṃbhavāt । api tu vibhāvādibhirvyañjitaścarvaṇīyaḥ । kārakajñāpakābhyāmanyat kva dṛṣṭamiti cet na kvaciddṛṣṭamityalaukikasiddherbhūṣaṇametanna dūṣaṇam । carvaṇāniṣpattyā tasya niṣpattirupacariteti kāryo apyucyatām ।
laukikapratyakṣādipramāṇatāṭasthyāvabodhaśālimitayogijñānavedyāntarasaṃsparśarahitasvātmamātraparyavasitaparimitetarayogisaṃvedanavilakṣaṇalokottarasvasaṃvedanagocara iti pratyeyo apyabhidhīyatām । tadgrāhakaṃ ca na nirvikalpakaṃ vibhāvādiparāmarśapradhānatvāt । nāpi savikalpakaṃ carvyamāṇasyālaukikānandamayasya svasaṃvedanasiddhatvāt । ubhayābhāvasvarūpasya cobhayātmakatvamapi pūrvavallokottaratāmeva gamayati na tu virodhamiti śrīmadācāryābhinavaguptapādāḥ ।। cintādayo vyabhicāriṇaḥ śṛṅgārasyaeva vīrakaruṇabhayānakānām iti pṛthaganaikāntikatvāt sūtre militā nirdiṣṭāḥ । madhukarakokilakūjitairdiśāṃ śrīḥ ।
praṇatipare dayite prasīda mugdhe ।।} kathamapi parivāraprārthanābhiḥ kriyāsu । abhinavakaridantacchedakāntaḥ kapolaḥ ।।} saṃśliṣyatyaruṇaṃ gṛhītavasane kiñcāñcitabhrūlatam ।
cakṣurjātamaho prapañcacaturaṃ jātāgasi preyasi ।।} yadyapi vibhāvānāmanubhāvānāmautsukyavrīḍāharṣakopāsūyāprasādānāṃ ca vyabhicāriṇāṃ kevalānāmatra sthitiḥ, tathāpyeteṣāmasādhāraṇatvamityanyatamadvayākṣepakatve sati nānaikāntikatvamiti ।। sṛṅgārahāsyakaruṇaraudravīrabhayānakāḥ । bībhatsādbhutasaṃjñau cetyaṣṭau nāṭye rasāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
tatra śṛṅgārasya dvau bhedau । saṃbhogo vipralambhaśca । tatrādyaḥ parasparāvalokanāliṅganādharapānaparicumbanādyanantatvādaparicchedya eka eva gaṇyate । yathā nidrāvyājamupāgatasya suciraṃ nirvarṇya patyurmukham । lajjānamramukhī priyeṇa hasatā bālā ciraṃ cumbitā ।।}
lakṣmīmityabhidhāyini priyatame tadvīṭikāsaṃspṛśi । niryātaḥ śanakairalīkavacanopanyāsamālījanaḥ ।।} aparastu abhilāṣaviraherṣyāpravāsaśāpahetuka iti pañcavidhaḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam tāstā mugdhadṛśo nisargamadhurāśceṣṭā bhaveyurmayi ।
āśaṃsāparikalpitāsvapi bhavatyānandasāndro layaḥ ।।} yo māṃ necchati nāgataśca hahahā ko ayaṃ vidheḥprakramaḥ । bālā vṛttavivartanavyatikarā nāpnoti nidrāṃ niśi ।।} eṣā virahotkaṇṭhitā ।
no jānāti savibhramāṅgavalanāvakroktisaṃsūcanam । bālā kevalameva roditi luṭhallolālakairaśrubhiḥ ।।} dhṛtyā na kṣaṇamāsitaṃ vyavasitaṃ cittena gantuṃ puraḥ । gantavye sati jīvita priyasuhṛtsārthaḥ kimu tyajyate ।।}
mātmānaṃ te caraṇapatitaṃ yāvadicchāmi kartum । krūrastasminnapi na sahate saṃgamaṃ nau kṛtāntaḥ ।।} mantrābhasāṃ pratipadaṃ pṛṣataiḥ pavitre । hāhā hato ahamiti roditi viṣṇuśarmā ।।}
dhik prāṇān patito aśanirhutavahaste aṅgeṣu dagdhe dṛśau । ścitrasthānapi rodayanti śatadhā kurvanti bhittīrapi ।।} manujapaśubhirnirmaryādairbhavadbhirudāyudhaiḥ । mayamaha[ma]sṛṅmedomāṃsaiḥ karomi diśāṃ balim ।।}
yuṣmaddeheṣu lajjāṃ dadhati paramamī sāyakā niṣpatantaḥ । kiñcidbhrūbhaṅgalīlāniyamitajaladhiṃ rāmamanveṣayāmi ।।} paścārdhena praviṣṭaḥ śarapatanabhayādbhūyasā pūrvakāyam । paśyodagraplutatvādviyati bahutaraṃ stokamurvyāṃ prayāti ।।}
nyaṃsasphikpṛṣṭhapiṇḍyādyavayavasulabhānyugrapūtīni jagdhvā । daṅkasthādasthisaṃsthaṃ sthapuṭagatamapi kravyamavyagramatti ।।} {citraṃ mahāneṣa batāvatāraḥ kva kāntireṣābhinavaiva bhaṅgiḥ । lokottaraṃ dhairyamaho prabhāvaḥ kāpyākṛtirnūtana eṣa sargaḥ ।।}
ratirhāsaśca śokaśca krodhotsāhau bhayaṃ tathā । jugupsā vismayaśceti sthāyibhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। spaṣṭam ।। nirvedaglāniśaṅkākhyāstathāsūyā madaśramāḥ ।
ālasyaṃ caiva dainyaṃ ca cintā mohaḥ smṛtirdhṛtiḥ ।। vrīḍā capalatā harṣa āvego jaḍatā tathā । garvo viṣāda autsukyaṃ nidrāpasmāra eva ca ।। suptaṃ prabodhomarṣaścāpyavahitthamathogratā ।
matirvyādhistathonmādastathā maraṇameva ca ।। trāsaścaiva vitarkaśca vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ । triṃstriśadamī bhāvāḥ samākhyātāstu nāmataḥ ।। nirvedasyāmaṅgalaprāyasya prathamamanupādeyatve apyupādānaṃ vyabhicāritve api sthāyitābhidhānārtham । tena
nirvedasthāyibhāvo asti śānto api navamo rasaḥ । maṇau vā loṣṭe vā balavati ripau vā suhṛdi vā । kvacitpuṇyāraṇye śiva śiva śiveti pralapataḥ ।।} ratirdevādiviṣayā vyabhicārī tathāñjitaḥ ।।
ādiśabdānmunigurunṛpaputrādiviṣayā । kāntāviṣayā tu vyaktā śṛṅgāraḥ । {kaṇṭhakoṇaviniviṣṭamīśa te kālakūṭamapi me mahāmṛtam । apyupāttamamṛtaṃ bhavadvapurbhedavṛtti yadi me na rocate ।।} {haratyaghaṃ saṃprati hetureṣyataḥ śubhasya pūrvācaritaiḥ kṛtaṃ śubhaiḥ ।
śarīrabhājāṃ bhavadīyadarśanaṃ vyanakti kālatritaye api yogyatām ।।} evamanyadapyudāhāryam । añjitavyabhicārī yathā mā māṃ saṃspṛśa pāṇineti rudatī gantuṃ pravṛttā puraḥ । bhrātastāvadahaṃ śaṭhena vidhinā nidrādaridrīkṛtaḥ ।।}
atra vidhiṃ pratyasūyā । tadābhāsā anaucityapravarttitāḥ । tadābhāsā rasābhāsā bhāvābhāsāśca । tatra rasābhāso yathā vilebhe kaḥ prāṇān raṇamakhamukhe yaṃ mṛgayase ।
tapaḥśrīḥ kasyaiṣā madananagari dhyāyasi tu yam ।।} atrānekakāmukaviṣayamabhilāpaṃ tasyāḥ stuma ityādyanugataṃ bahuvyāpāropādānaṃ vyanakti । bhāvābhāso yathā sā smerayauvanataraṅgitavibhramāṅgī । tatsvīkṛtivyatikare ka ivābhyupāyaḥ ।।}
atra cintā anaucityapravartitā । evamanye apyudāhāryāḥ ।। bhāvasya śāntirudayaḥ sandhiḥ śabalatā tathā ।। kiṃ vakṣaścaraṇānativyatikaravyājena gopāyyate । sāśliṣṭā rabhasena tatsukhavaśāttanvyā ca tadvismṛtam ।।}
atra kopasya । sadyo mānaparigrahaglapitayā cāṭūni kurvannapi । mā bhūtsupta ivetyamandavalitagrīvaṃ punarvīkṣitaḥ ।।} atrautsukyasya ।
satsaṃgapriyatā ca vīrarabhasotphālaśca māṃ karṣataḥ । ānandī haricandanenduśiśirasnigdho ruṇaddhyanyataḥ ।।} atrāvegaharṣayoḥ । doṣāṇāṃ praśamāya na śrutamaho kope api kāntaṃ mukham ।
cetaḥ svāsthyamupaihi kaḥ khalu yuvā dhanyo adharaṃ dhāsyati ।।} atra vitarkautsukyamatismaraṇaśaṅkādainyadhṛticintānāṃ śabalatā । bhāvasthitistūktā udāhṛtā ca ।। mukhye rase api te aṅgitvaṃ prāpnuvanti kadācana ।
te bhāvaśāntyādayaḥ । aṅgitvaṃ rājānugatavivāhapravṛttabhṛtyavat ।। anusvānābhasaṃlakṣyakramavyaṅgyasthitistu yaḥ ।। śabdārthobhayaśaktyutthastridhā sa kathito dhvaniḥ । ubhayaśaktimūlānuraṇanarūpavyaṅgyaśceti trividhaḥ ।।
alaṅkāro atha vastveva śabdādyatrāvabhāsate ।। pradhānatvena sa jñeyaḥ śabdaśaktyudbhavo dvidhā । vastveti, analaṅkāraṃ vastumātram । ādyo yathā devena yena jaraṭhorjitagarjitena ।
dhārājalaistrijagati jvalitaḥ pratāpaḥ ।।} atra vākyasyāsaṃbaddhārthābhidhāyakatvaṃ mā prasāṅkṣīditi prākaraṇikāprākaraṇikayorupamānopameyabhāvaḥ kalpanīya ityatropamālaṅkāro vyaṅgyaḥ । {tigmarucirapratāpo vidhuraniśākṛdvibho madhuralīlaḥ । matimānatattvavṛttiḥpratipadapakṣāgraṇīrvibhāti bhavān ।।}
atraikaikasya padasya dvipadatve virodhābhāsaḥ । {amitaḥ samitaḥ prāptairutkarṣairharṣada prabho । ahitaḥ sahitaḥ sādhuyaśobhirasatāmasi ।।} atrāpi virodhābhāsaḥ ।
{nirupādānasaṃbhāramabhittāveva tanvate । jagaccitraṃ namastasmai kalāślādhyāya śūline ।।} atra vyatirekaḥ । alaṅkāryasyāpi brāhmaṇaśramaṇanyāyenālaṅkāratā । vastumātraṃ yathā
{panthia ṇa ettha sattharamaitthi maṇaṃ pattharatthale gāme । uṇṇaapaoharaṃ pekhkhiūṇa jai vasasi tā vasasu ।।} [pathika nātra srastaramasti manāk prastarasthale grāme । unnatapayodharaṃ praksya yadi vasasi tadā vasa ।।]
atra yadyupabhogakṣamosi tadā āssvetiṃ vyajyate । {śaniraśaniśca tamuccairnihanti kupyasi narendra yasmai tvam । yatra prasīdasi punaḥ sa bhātyudāronudāraśca ।।} aviruddhāvapi tvadanuvartanārthamekaṃ kārya kuruta iti dhvanyate ।
arthaśaktyudbhavo apyartho vyañjakaḥ saṃbhavī svataḥ ।। prauḍhoktimātrātsiddho vā kavestenombhitasya vā । vastu vālaṅkṛtirvety ṣaḍbhedo asau vyanakti yat ।। vastvalaṅkāramathavā tenāyaṃ dvādaśātmakaḥ ।
svataḥsaṃbhavī na kevalaṃ bhaṇitamātraniṣpanno yāvadbahirapyaucityena saṃbhāvyamānaḥ । kavinā pratibhāmātreṇa bahirasannapi nirmitaḥ kavinibaddhena vaktreti vā dvividhopara iti trividhaḥ । vastu vālaṅkāro vāsāviti ṣoḍhā vyañjakaḥ । tasya vastu vālaṅkāro vā vyaṅgya iti dvādaśabhedo arthaśaktyudbhavo dhvaniḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam {alasaśiromaṇi dhuttāṇaṃ aggimo putti dhaṇasamiddhimao । ia bhaṇieṇa ṇaaṅgī papphullaviloaṇā jāā ।।} [alasaśiromaṇirdhūrtānāmagrimaḥ putri dhanasamṛddhimayaḥ ।
iti bhaṇitenanatāṅgī praphullavilocanā jātā ।।] atra mamaivopabhogya iti vastunā vastu vyajyate । viśrabdhacāṭukaśatāni ratāntareṣu । sakhyaḥ śapāmi yadi kiñcidapi smarāmi ।।}
atra tvamadhanyā ahaṃ tu dhanyeti vyatirekālaṅkāraḥ । saṃkrāntinighnaghanaśoṇitaśoṇaśociḥ । kālīkaṭākṣa iva yasya kare kṛpāṇaḥ ।।} atropamālaṅkāreṇa sakalaripubalakṣayaḥ kṣaṇāt kariṣyate iti vastu ।
{gāḍhakāntadaśanakṣatavyathāsaṃkaṭādarivadhūjanasya yaḥ । oṣṭhavidrumadalānyamocayannirdaśan yudhi ruṣā nijādharam ।।} atra virodhālaṅkāreṇādharanirdaśanasamakālameva śatravo vyāpāditā iti tulyayogitā mama kṣatyāpyanyasya kṣatirnivartatāmiti tadbuddhirutprekṣyate ityutprekṣā ca । eṣūdāharaṇeṣu svataḥsaṃbhavī vyañjakaḥ ।
śrutvā kīrtiṃ vibudharamaṇīgīyamānāṃ yadīyām । diṅmātaṅgāḥ śravaṇapuline hastamāvartayanti ।।} atra vastunā yeṣāmapyarthādhigamo nāsti teṣāmapyevamādibuddhijananena camatkāraṃ karoti tvatkīrtiriti vastu dhvanyate । {kesesu balāmoḍia teṇa a samarammi jaasirī gahiā ।
jaha kandarāṃhi vihurā tassa daḍhaṃ kaṇṭhaammi saṃṭhaviā ।।} [keśeṣu balātkāreṇa tena ca samare jayaśrīrgṛhītā । yathā kandarābhirvidhurāstasya dṛḍhaṃ kaṇṭhe saṃsthāpitā ।।] atra keśagrahaṇāvalokanoddīpitamadanā iva kandarāstadvidhurān kaṇṭhe gṛhṇanti ityutprekṣā । ekatra saṃgrāme vijayadarśanāttasyārayaḥ palāyya guhāsu tiṣṭhantīti kāvyaheturalaṅkāraḥ । na palāyya gatāstadvairiṇo api tu tataḥ parābhavaṃ saṃbhāvya tān kandarā na tyajantītyapahnutiśca ।
{gāḍhāliṅgaṇarahasujja-ammi da-i-e lahu samosara-i । māṇaṃsiṇīṇa māṇo pīlaṇabhī-a vva hi-a-āhiṃ ।।} [gāḍhāliṅganarabhasodyate dayite laghu samapasarati । manasvinyāḥ mānaḥ pīḍanabhīta iva hṛdayāt ।।]
atrotprekṣayā pratyāliṅganādi tatra vijṛmbhate iti vastu । {jā ṭheraṃvva hasantī ka-iva-aṇaṃburuhavaddhaviṇivesā । dāve-i bhu-aṇamaṇḍalamaṇṇaṃ vi-a ja-a-i sā vāṇī ।।} [yā sthaviramiva hasantī kavivadanāmburuhabaddhaviniveśā ।
darśayati bhuvanamaṇḍalamanyadiva jayati sā vāṇī ।।] atrotprekṣayā camatkāraikakāraṇaṃ navaṃ navaṃ jagat ajaḍāsanasthā nirmimīte iti vyatirekaḥ । eṣu kaviprauḍhoktimātraniṣpanno vyañjakaḥ । phārupphullaphaṇāvalīkavalaṇe pattā dariddattaṇaṃ । jādā jhatti sisuttaṇe vi bahalā tāruṇṇapuṇṇā vi-a ।।}
sphārotphullaphaṇāvalīkavalane prāptā daridratvam । jātā jhaṭiti śiśutve api bahalāstāruṇyapūrṇā iva ।।] atra niḥśvāsaiḥ prāptaiśvaryā vāyavaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na kurvantīti vastunā vastu vyajyate । {sahi vira-i-ūṇa māṇassa majjha dhīrattaṇeṇa āsāsaṃ ।
pi-adaṃsaṇavihaṅkhalelakkhaṇammi sahasatti teṇa osari-aṃ ।।} [sakhi viracayya mānasya mama dhīratvenāśvāsam । priyadarśanaviśṛṅkhalakṣaṇe sahaseti tenāpasṛtam ।।] atra vastunākṛte api prārthane prasanneti vibhāvanā priyadarśanasya saubhāgyabalaṃ dhairyeṇa soḍhuṃ na śakyate ityutprekṣā vā ।
{ollollakara-ara-akhkha-ehi tuha lo-aṇesu maha diṇṇaṃ । rattaṃsu-aṃ pasā-o koveṇa puṇo ime ṇa akkami-ā ।।} [ārdrārdrakarajaradanakṣataistava locanayormama dattam । raktāṃśukaṃ prasādaḥ kopena punarime nākrānte ।।]
atra kimiti locane kupite vahasi iti uttarālaṅkāreṇa na kevalamārdranakhakṣatāni gopāyasi yāvatteṣāmahaṃ prasādapātraṃ jāteti vastu । {mahilāsahassabhari-e tuha hi-a-e suha-a sā amā-antī । aṇudiṇamaṇaṇṇakammā aṅgaṃ taṇu-aṃ vi taṇu-e-i ।।} [mahilāsahasrabharite tava hṛdaye subhaga sā amāntī ।
anudinamananyakarmā aṅgaṃ tanukamapi tanayati ।।] atra hetvalaṅkāreṇa tanostanūkaraṇepi tava hṛdaye na vartate iti viśeṣoktiḥ । eṣu kavinibaddhavaktṛprauḍhoktimātraniṣpannaśarīro vyañjakaḥ । evaṃ dvādaśa bhedāḥ ।। {atandracandrābharaṇā samuddīpitamanmathā । tārakātaralā śyāmā sānandaṃ na karoti kam ।।}
atropamā vyaṅgyā ।। bhedā aṣṭādaśāsya tat ।। asyeti dhvaneḥ ।। nanu rasādīnāṃ bahubhedatvena kathamaṣṭādaśetyata āha ।
rasādīnāmanantatvādbheda eko hi gaṇyate । anantatvāditi । tathāhi nava rasāḥ । tatra śṛṅgārasya dvau bhedau । saṃbhogo vipralambhaśca । saṃbhogasyāpi parasparāvalokanāliṅganaparicumbanādikusumoccayajalakelisūryāstamayacandrodayaṣaḍṛtuvarṇanādayo bahavo bhedāḥ । vipralambhasyābhilāṣādaya uktāḥ । tayorapi vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārivaicitryam । tatrāpi nāyakayoruttamamadhyamādhamaprakṛtitvam । tatrāpi deśakālāvasthādibhedā ityekasyaiva rasasyānantyam । kā gaṇanā tvanyeṣāṃ । kramatvaṃ tu sāmānyamāśritya rasādidhvanibheda eka eva gaṇyate ।। dvyuttha iti śabdārthobhayaśaktimūlaḥ ।।
apiśabdādvākyepi । ekāvayavasthitena bhūṣaṇena kāminīva padadyotyena vyaṅgyena vākyavyaṅgyāpi bhāratī bhāsate । tatra padaprakāśyatve krameṇodāharaṇāni {yasya mitrāṇi mitrāṇi śatravaḥ śatravastathā । anukampyonukampyaśca sa jātaḥ sa ca jīvati ।। } atra dvitīyamitrādiśabdā āśvastatvaniyantraṇīyatvasnehapātratvādisaṃkramitavācyāḥ ।
{khalavavahārā dīsanti dāruṇā jahavi tahavi dhīrāṇaṃ । hiaavaassavahumaā ṇa hu vavasāā vimujjhanti ।। } [khalavyavahārāḥ dṛśyante dāruṇāḥ yadyapi tathāpi dhīrāṇām । hṛdayavayasyabahumatāḥ na khalu vyavasāyāḥ vimuhyanti ।।]
atra vimuhyantīti । {lāvaṇyaṃ tadasau kāntistadrūpaṃ sa vacaḥkramaḥ । tadā sudhāspadamabhūdadhunā tu jvaro mahān ।।} atra tadādipadairanubhavaikagocarā arthāḥ prakāśyante । yathā vā
mānaṃ dhatsva dhṛtiṃ badhāna ṛjutāṃ dūre kuru preyasi । nīcaiḥśaṃsa hṛdi sthito hi nanu me prāṇeśvaraḥ śroṣyati ।। } atra bhītānaneti । etena hi nīcaiḥśaṃsanavidhānasya yuktatā gamyate । bhāvādīnāṃ padaprakāśyatve adhikaṃ na vaicitryamiti na tadudāhriyate । {rudhiravisaraprasādhitakaravālakarālarucirabhujaparighaḥ ।
jhaṭiti bhrukuṭiviṭaṅkitalalāṭapaṭṭo vibhāsi nṛpa bhīma ।। } atra bhīṣaṇīyasya bhīmasena upamānam । {bhuktimuktikṛdekāntasamādeśanatatparaḥ । kasya nānandanisyandaṃ vidadhāti sadāgamaḥ ।। }
kācit saṃketadāyinamevaṃ mukhyayā vṛttyā śaṃsati । yāto astācalamaulimambaramaṇirvisrabdhamatrāgatiḥ । netradvandvamamīlanavyatikaraṃ śaknoti tenāsitum ।। } atra vastunā kṛtapuruṣaparicayā klāntāsīti vastu adhunāpadadyotyaṃ vyajyate ।
{tadprāptimahāduḥkhavilīnāśeṣapātakā । taccintāvipulāhlādakṣīṇapuṇyacayā tathā ।। cintayantī jagatsūtiṃ parabrahmasvarūpiṇam । nirucchvāsatayā muktiṃ gatānyā gopakanyakā ।। }
atra janmasahastairupabhoktavyāni duṣkṛtasukṛtaphalāni viyogaduḥkhacintanāhlādābhyāmanubhūtānītyuktam । evaṃ cāśeṣacayapadadyotye atiśayoktī । {kṣaṇadāsāvakṣaṇadā vanamavanaṃ vyasanamavyasanam । bata vīra tava dviṣatāṃ parāṅmukhe tvayi parāṃṅmukhaṃ sarvam ।। }
atra śabdaśaktimūlavirodhāṅgenārthāntaranyāsena {vidhirapi tvāmanuvartate} iti sarvapadadyotyaṃ vastu । {tuha vallahassa gosammi āsi aharo milāṇakamaladalo । i-a ṇavavahu-ā so-ūṇa kuṇa-i va-aṇaṃ mahisaṃmuhaṃ ।। } [tava vallabhasya prabhāta āsīdadharo mlānakamaladalam ।
iti navavadhūḥ śrutvā karoti vadanaṃ mahīsaṃmukham ।।] atra rūpakeṇa tvayāsya muhurmuhuḥ paricumbanaṃ tathā kṛtaṃ yena mlānatvamiti milāṇādipadadyotyaṃ kāvyaliṅgam । eṣu svataḥ- saṃbhavī vyañjakaḥ । {rā-īsu candadhavalāsu lali-amapphāli-ūṇa jo cāvaṃ । ekacchattaṃ vi-a kuṇa-i bhu-aṇarajjaṃ vijaṃbhanto ।। }
[rātrīṣu candradhavalāsu lalitamāsphālya yaścāpam । ekacchatramiva karoti bhuvanarājyaṃ vijṛmbhamāṇaḥ ।।] atra vastunā yeṣāṃ kāmināmasau rājā smarastebhyo na kaścidapi tadādeśaparāṅmukha iti jāgradbhirupabhogaparaireva tairniśātivāhyate iti bhuaṇarajjapadadyotyaṃ vastu prakāśyate । dṛśi sudṛśaḥ svabalaṃ vayasyarāle ।
vyatikarametya samunmiṣantyavasthāḥ ।। } atra vastunā yugapadavasthāḥ prasparaviruddhā api prabhavantīti vyatikarapadadyotyo virodhaḥ । {vārijjanto vi puṇo saṃdāvakadatthi-eṇa hi-a-eṇa । thaṇaharava-asma-eṇa visuddhajā-ī ṇa cala-i se hāro ।। }
[vāryamāṇo api punaḥ saṃtāpakadarthitena hṛdayena । stanabharavayasyena viśuddhajātirna calatyasyā hāraḥ ।।] atra viśuddhajātitvalakṣaṇahetvalaṅkāreṇa hāro anavarataṃ kampamāna evāste iti ṇa cala-i-padadyotyaṃ vastu । {so muddhasāmalaṅgo dhammillo kali-alaliaṇi-adeho ।
tī-e khandhāhi balaṃ gahi-a saṃro sura-asaṃgare ja-a-i ।। } [sa mugdhaśyāmalāṅgaḥ dhammillaḥ kalitalalitanijadehaḥ । tasyāḥ skandhādbalaṃ gṛhītvā smaraḥ suratasaṃgare jayati ।।] atra rūpakeṇa muhurmuhurākarṣaṇena tathā keśapāśaḥ skandhayoḥ prāpto yathā rativiratāvapyanivṛttābhilāṣaḥ kāmko abhūditi khandha-padadyotyā vibhāvanā ।। eṣu kaviprauḍhoktimātraniṣpannaśarīraḥ ।।
{ṇavapuṇṇimāmi-aṅkassa suha-a ko taṃ si bhaṇasu maha saccaṃ । kā sohaggasamaggā pa-osara-aṇivva tuha ajja ।। } [navapūrṇimāmṛgāṅkasya subhaga kastvamasi bhaṇa mama satyam । kā saubhāgyasamagrā pradoṣarajanīva tavādya ।।]
atra vastunā mayīvānyasyāmapi prathamamanuraktastvaṃ na tata iti ṇavetyādi - pa-osetyādipadadyotyaṃ vastu vyajyate ।। {sahi ṇavaṇihuvaṇasamarammi aṅkavālīsahī-e ṇiviḍā-e । hāro ṇivāri-o vi-a uccheranto tado kahaṃ rami-aṃ ।। } [sakhi navanidhuvanasamare aṅkapālīsakhyā nibiḍayā ।
hāro nivārita evocchriyamāṇastataḥ kathaṃ ramitam ।।] atra vastunā hāracchedānantaramanyadeva ratamavaśyamabhūt tatkathaya kīdṛgiti vyatirekaḥ kahaṃpadagamyaḥ ।। {pravisaṃtī gharavāraṃ vivali-ava-aṇā vilo-i-ūṇa pahaṃ । khandhe ghettūṇa ghaḍaṃ hā hā ṇaṭṭhotti ru-asi sahi kinti ।।}
[praviśantī gṛhadvāraṃ vivalitavadanā vilokya panthānam । skandhe gṛhītvā ghaṭaṃ hā hā naṣṭa iti rodiṣi sakhi kimiti ।।] atra hetvalaṅkāreṇa saṃketaniketanaṃ gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā yadi tatra gantumicchasi tadā aparaṃ ghaṭaṃ gṛhītvā gaccheti vastu kinti-pada-dyotyam । yathā vā {vihalaṅkhalaṃ tumaṃ sahi daṭṭhūṇa kuḍeṇa taralataradiṭṭhiṃ ।
vārapphaṃsamiseṇa a appā guru-otti pāḍi-a vihiṇṇo ।। } [viśṛṅkhalāṃ tvāṃ sakhi dṛṣṭvā kuṭena taralataradṛṣṭim । dvārasparśamiṣeṇa cātmā guruka iti pātayitvā vibhinnaḥ ।।] atra nadīkūle latāgahane kṛtasaṃketamaprāptaṃ gṛhapraveśāvasare paścādāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā punarnadīgamanāya dvāropaghātavyājena buddhipūrvaṃ vyākulatayā tvayā ghaṭaḥ sphoṭita iti mayā cintitaṃ tatkimiti nāśvasiṣi tatsamīhitasiddhaye vraja ahaṃ te śvaśrūnikaṭe sarvaṃ samarthayiṣye iti dvārasparśanavyājenetyapahnutyā vastu ।
{johṇā-iṃ mahuraseṇa a vi-iṇṇatāruṇcchu-amaṇā sā । vuḍḍhāvi ṇavoḍhavvi-a paravahu-ā ahaha hara-ituha hi-a-aṃ ।। } [jyotsnayā madhurasena ca vitīrṇatāruṇyotsukamanāḥ sā । vṛddhāpi navoḍheva paravadhūrahaha harati tava hṛdayam ।।]
atra kāvyaliṅgena vṛddhāṃ paravadhūṃ tvamasmānujjhitvābhilaṣasīti tvadīyamācaritaṃ vaktuṃ na śaktyamityākṣepaḥ paravahūpadaprakāśyaḥ । eṣu kavinibaddhavaktṛprauḍhoktimātraniṣpannaśarīraḥ ।। vākyaprakāśye tu pūrvamudāhṛtam ।। pañcatriṃśadbhedāḥ ।।
prabandhe apyarthaśaktibhūḥ ।। yathā gṛdhragomāyusaṃvādādau । {alaṃ sthitvā śmaśāne asmin gṛdhragomāyusaṃkule । kaṅkālabahale ghore sarvaprāṇibhayaṅkare ।।}
{na ceha jīvitaḥ kaścit kāladharmamupāgataḥ । priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyaḥ prāṇināṃ gatirīdṛśī ।।} iti divā prabhavato gṛdhrasya puruṣavisarjanaparamidaṃ vacanam ।। {ādityo ayaṃ sthito mūḍhāḥ snehaṃ kuruta sāṃpratam ।
bahuvighno muhūrto ayaṃ jīvedapi kadācana ।।} {amuṃ kanakavarṇābhaṃ bālamaprāptayauvanam । gṛdhravākyātkathaṃ mūḍhāstyajadhvamaviśaṅkitāḥ ।।} iti niśi vijṛmbhamāṇasya gomāyorjanavyāvartananiṣṭhaṃ ca vacanamiti prabandha eva prathate ।।
anye tvekādaśa bhedā granthavistarabhayānnodāhṛtāḥ svayaṃ tu lakṣaṇatonusartavyāḥ ।। apiśabdātpadavākyayoḥ ।। padaikadeśaracanāvarṇeṣvapi rasādayaḥ । {ra-ikelihi-aṇivasaṇakarakisala-aruddhaṇa-aṇaju-alassa ।
ruddhassa ta-i-aṇa-aṇaṃ pavva-īparicuṃbi-aṃ ja-a-i ।।} [ratikelibṛtanivasanakarakisalayaruddhanayanayugalasya । rudrasya tṛtīyanayanaṃ pārvatīparicumbitañjayati ।।] atha jayatīti na tu śobhate ityādi । samāne api hi sthaganavyāpāre lokottareṇaiva vyāpāreṇāsya pidhānamiti
tadevotkṛṣṭam । yathā vā dvitrāṇyeva padāni vāsabhavanādyāvanna yātyunmanāḥ । dhāvitveva kṛtapraṇāmakamaho premṇo vicitrā gatiḥ ।।} atra padānīti na tu dvārāṇīti ।।
diśi diśi pavamāno vīrudhāṃ lāsakaśca । puri puri vinivṛttā māninīmānacarcā ।।} atra kiratīti kiraṇasya sādhyamānatvaṃ nivṛtteti nivartanasya siddhatvaṃ tiṅā supā ca tatrāpi ktapratyayenātītatvaṃ dyotyate । yathā vā nirāhārāḥ sakhyaḥ satataruditocchūnanayanāḥ ।
tavāvasthā ceyaṃ visṛja kaṭhine mānamadhhunā ।।} bhūmāviti na hi buddhipūrvakamaparaṃ kiñcillikhatīti tiṅsubvibhaktīnāṃ vyaṅgyam । {gāmāruhamhi hāme vasāmi ṇa-araṭṭhi-iṃ ṇa jāṇāmi । ṇā-ari-āṇaṃ pa-iṇo haremi jā homi sā homi ।।}
[grāmaruhāsmi grāme vasāmi nagarasthitiṃ na jānāmi । nāgarikāṇāṃ patīn harāmi yā bhavāmi sā bhavāmi ।।] atra nāgarikāṇāmiti ṣaṣṭhyāḥ । ramaṇīyaḥ kṣatriyakumāra āsīt iti kālasya । eṣā hi bhagnamaheśvarakārmukaṃ dāśarathiṃ pratikupitasya bhārgavasyokti । vacanasya yathā ।
{tāṇaṃ guṇaggaaṇāṇaṃ tāṇukkaṇṭhāṇaṃ tassa pemmassa । tāṇaṃ bhaṇi-āṇaṃ suṃdara erisi-aṃ jā-amavasāṇaṃ ।।} [teṣāṃ guṇagrahaṇānāṃ tāsāmutkaṇṭhānāṃ tasya premnaḥ । tāsāṃ bhaṇitīnāṃ sundara īdṛśaṃ jātamavasānam ।।]
atra guṇagrahaṇādīnāṃ bahutvaṃ premṇaścaikatvaṃ dyotyate ।। premāṇaṃ mahimānameṇayanāmālokya kiṃ nṛtyasi । eṣā kaṇṭhataṭe kṛtā khalu śilā saṃsāravārāṃnidhau ।।} atra prahāsaḥ ।
prāyaḥ kevalanītirītiśaraṇaiḥ kāryaṃ kimurvīśvaraiḥ । te syurnaiva bhavādṛśāstrijagati dvitrāḥ pavitrāḥ param ।।} atra parākramasya prādhānyamavagamyate । {pradhanādhvani dhīradhanurdhvanibhṛti vidhurairayodhi tava divasam ।
divasena tu narapa bhavānayuddha vidhisiddhasādhuvādapadam ।।} atra divasenetyapavargatṛtīyā phalaprāptiṃ dyotayati । dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā bhavanavalabhītuṅgavātāyanasthā । gāḍhotkaṇṭhālulitalulitairaṅgakaistāmyatīti ।।}
atrānukampāvṛtteḥ karūpataddhitasya । punarjanmanyasminnanubhavapathaṃ yo na gatavān । vikāraḥ ko apyantarjaḍayati ca tāpaṃ ca kurute ।।} atra praśabdasyopasargasya ।
kimanyadevaṃ nihatāśca no dviṣaḥ । na yāvadāyātyudayādrimaulitām ।।} atra tulyayogitādyotakasya [ca] iti nipātasya । masmadbhāgyaviparyayādyadi paraṃ devo na jānāti tam ।
śreṇībhūtaviśālatālavivarodgīrṇaiḥsvaraiḥsaptabhiḥ ।।} atrāsāviti bhuvaneṣviti guṇairiti sarvanāmaprātipadikavacanānāṃ na tvaditi na maditi api asmadityasya sarvākṣepiṇaḥ bhāgyaviparyayādityanyathāsaṃpattimukhena na tvabhāvamukhenābhidhānasya । {taruṇimani kalayati kalāmanumadanadhanurbhruvoḥ paṭhatyagre । adhivasati sakalalalanāmaulimiyaṃ cakitaṃhariṇacalanayanā ।।}
atra imanijavyayībhāvakarmabhūtādhārāṇāṃ svarūpasya taruṇatve, iti dhanuṣaḥ samīpe, iti maulau vasatīti tvādibhistulye, eṣāṃ vācakatve, asti kaścit svarūpasya viśeṣo yaścamatkārakārī sa eva vyañjakatvaṃ prāpnoti । evamanyeṣāmapi boddhavyam । varṇaracanānāṃ vyañjakatvaṃ guṇasvarūpanirūpaṇe udāhariṣyate apiśabdāt prabandheṣu nāṭakādiṣu । evaṃ rasādīnāṃ pūrvagaṇitabhedābhyāṃ saha ṣaḍ bhedāḥ ।
vyākhyātāḥ ।। teṣāṃ cānyonyayojane ।। saṃkareṇa trirūpeṇa saṃsṛṣṭyā caikarūpayā । na kevalaṃ śuddhā evaikapañcāśadbhedā bhavanti । yāvatteṣāṃ svaprabhedairekapañcāśatā saṃśayāspadatvenānugrāhakatayaikavyañjakānupraveśena ceti trividhena saṃkareṇa parasparanirapekṣarūpayaikaprakārayā saṃsṛṣṭyā ceti catur[bhir]guṇane ।
śareṣuyugakhendavaḥ ।। tatra diṅmātramudāhṇiyate । {kkhaṇapāhuṇi-ā de-ara jā-ā-e suha-a kiṃpi de bhaṇi-ā । ru-a-i paḍoharavalahīgharammi aṇuṇiñja-u varā-ī ।।}
[kṣaṇaprāghuṇikā devara jāyayā subhaga kimapi te bhaṇitā । roditi gṛhapaścādbhāgavalanbhīgṛhe anunīyatāṃ varākī ।।] atrānunayaḥ kimupabhogalakṣaṇe arthāntare saṃkramitaḥ kimanuraṇananyāyenopabhoge eva vyaṅgye vyañjakaḥ iti saṃdehaḥ । vātāḥ śīkariṇaḥ payodasuhṛdāmānandakekāḥ kalāḥ ।
vaidehī tu kathaṃ bhaviṣyati ha hā hā devi dhīrā bhava ।।} atra lipteti payodasuhṛdāmiti ca atyantatiraskṛtavācyayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । tābhyāṃ saha rāmo asmītyarthāntarasaṃkramitavācyasyānugrāhakabhāvena rāmapadalakṣaṇaikavyañjakānupraveśena cārthāntarasaṃkramitavācyarasadhvanyoḥ saṃkaraḥ । evamanyadapyudāhāryam ।। iti kāvyaprakāśe dhvaninirṇayo nāma caturtha ullāsaḥ ।। evaṃ dhvanau nirṇīte guṇībhūtavyaṅgyaprabhedānāha ।
agūḍhamaparasyāṅgaṃ vācyasiddhyaṅgamasphuṭam । sandigdhatulyaprādhānye kākvākṣiptamasundaram ।। vyaṅgyamevaṃ guṇībhūtavyaṅgyasyāṣṭau bhidāḥ smṛtāḥ । kāminīkucakalaśavat gūḍhaṃ camatkaroti । agūḍhaṃ tu sphuṭatayā vācyāyamānamiti guṇībhūtameva । agūḍhaṃ yathā
sūcīvyadhavyatikareṇa yunakti karṇau । jīvanna saṃprati bhavāmi kimāvahāmi ।।} atra jīvannityarthāntarasaṃkramitavācyasya । gāyanti mañju madhupā gṛhadīrghikāsu ।
puṣpacchadābhamudayācalacumbi bimbam ।।} atra cumbanasyātyantatiraskṛtavācyasya । gāḍhaṃ vakṣasi tāḍite hanumatā droṇādriratrāhṛtaḥ । kenāpyatra mṛgākṣi rākṣasapateḥ kṛttā ca kaṇṭhāṭavī ।। }
atra kenāpyatretyarthaśaktimūlānuraṇanarūpasya । {tasyāpyatra} iti yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ । aparasya rasādervācyasya vā aṅgaṃ rasādi anuraṇanarūpaṃ vā । yathā {ayaṃ sa raśanotkarṣī pīnastanavimardanaḥ । nābhyūrujaghanasparśī nīvīvisraṃsanaḥ karaḥ ।।}
atra śṛṅgāraḥ karuṇasya । vyaktiḥ pādanakhadyutirgiribhuvaḥ sā vaḥ sadā trāyatām । kāntiḥ kokanadānukārasarasā sadyaḥ samutsāryate ।।} atra bhāvasya rasaḥ ।
stānetānapi bibhratī kimapi na klāntāsi tubhyaṃ namaḥ । stāvadbibhradimāṃ smṛtastava bhujo vācastato mudritāḥ ।।} atra bhūviṣayo ratyākhyo bhāvo rājaviṣayasya ratibhāvasya । śliṣyanti praṇamanti lānti paritaścumbanti te sainikāḥ ।
vidhvastā vipadokhilāstaditi taiḥ pratyarthibhiḥ stūyase ।।} atra bhāvasya rasābhāsabhāvābhāsau prathamārdhadvitīyārdhadyotyau । {aviralakaravālakampanairbhrukuṭītarjanagarjanairmuhuḥ । dadṛśe tava vairiṇāṃ madaḥ sa gataḥ kvāpi tavekṣaṇe kṣaṇāt ।।}
atra bhāvasya bhāvapraśamaḥ । kartuṃ suhṛdbhirapi vairiṇi te pravṛtte । kenāpi tatra viṣamāmakarodavasthām ।।} atra trāsodayaḥ ।
kathānāṃ viśrambheṣvatha ca rasikaḥ śailaduhituḥ । tvarāśaithilyābhyāṃ yugapadabhiyuktaḥ smaraharaḥ ।।} atrāvegadhairyayoḥ saṃdhiḥ ।। hastālambaṃ vitara ha ha hā vyutkramaḥ kvāsi yāsi ।
kanyā kañcit phalakisalayānyādadānābhidhatte ।।} atra śaṅkāsūyādhṛtismṛtiśramadainyavibodhautsukyānāṃ śabalatā । ete ca rasavadādyalaṅkārāḥ । yadyapi bhāvodayabhāvasaṃdhibhāvaśabalatvāni nālaṅkāratayā uktāni tathāpi kaścit brūyādityevamuktam । yadyapi sa nāsti kaścidviṣayaḥ yatra dhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyayoḥ svaprabhedādibhiḥ saha saṃkaraḥ saṃsṛṣṭirvā nāsti tathāpi prādhānyena vyapadeśā bhavantīti kvacitkenacidvyavahāraḥ । vaco vaidehīti pratipadamudaśru pralapitam । mayāptaṃ rāmatvaṃ kuśalavasutā na tvadhigatā ।।}
vācyāṅgatāṃ nītaḥ । mambhojinīṃ kvacidapi kṣapitatriyāmaḥ । tanvaṅgi pādapatanena sahasraraśmiḥ ।। } atra nāyakavṛttānto arthaśaktimūlo vasturūpo nirapekṣaravikamalinīvṛttāntādhyāropeṇaiva sthitaḥ ।।
{bhramimaratimalasahṛdayatāṃ pralayaṃ mūrchā tamaḥ śarīrasādam । maraṇaṃ jaladabhujagajaṃ prasahya kurute viṣaṃ viyoginīnām ।।} atra hālāhalaṃ vyaṅgyaṃ bhujagarūpasya vācyasya siddhikṛt । yathā vā kiṃ tvevaṃ vijanasthayorhatajanaḥsaṃbhāvayatyanyathā ।
āśliṣyan pulakotkarāñcitatanurgopīṃ hariḥ pātu vaḥ ।। } atrācyutādipadavyaṅgyamāmantraṇetyādivācyasya । etaccaikatra ekavaktṛgatatvena aparatra bhinnavaktṛgatatvenetyanayorbhedaḥ ।। {adṛṣṭe darśanotkaṇṭhā dṛṣṭe vicchedabhīrutā । nādṛṣṭena na dṛṣṭena bhavatā labhyate sukham ।। }
atrādṛṣṭo yathā na bhavasi viyogabhayaṃ ca yathā notpadyate tathā kuryā iti kliṣṭam ।। {harastu kiñcitparivṛttadhairyaścandrodayārambha ivāmburāśiḥ । umāmukhe bimbaphalādharoṣṭhe vyāpārayāmāsa vilocanāni ।। } atra paricumbitumaicchaditi kiṃ pratīyamānaṃ kiṃ vā vilocanavyāpāraṇaṃ vācyaṃ pradhānamiti saṃdehaḥ ।।
{brāhmaṇātikramatyāgo bhavatāmeva bhūtaye । jāmadagnyastathā mitramanyathā durmanāyate ।। } atra jāmadagnyaḥ sarveṣāṃ kṣatriyāṇāmiva rakṣasāṃ kṣaṇāt kṣayaṃ kariṣyatīti vyaṅgyasya vācyasya ca samaṃ prādhānyam ।। duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ na pbāmyurastaḥ ।।
saṃdhiṃ karotu bhavatāṃ nṛpatiḥ paṇena ।। } atra mathnāmyevetyādi vyaṅgyaṃ vācyaniṣedhasahabhāvena sthitam ।। {vāṇīrakuñjuḍḍīṇasa-uṇikolāhalaṃ suṇantī-e । gharakammavāvaḍā-e bahu-e sī-anti aṅgā-iṃ ।। }
[vānīrakuñjoḍḍīnaśakunikolāhalaṃ śṛṇvantyāḥ । gṛhakarmavyāpṛtāyā vadhvāḥ sīdantyaṅgāni ।।] atra dattasaṃketaḥ kaścillatāgahanaṃ praviṣṭa iti vyaṅgyāt sīdantyaṅgānīti vācyaṃ sacamatkāram ।। eṣāṃ bhedā yathāyogaṃ veditavyāśca pūrvavat ।।
{vyajyante vastumātreṇa yadālaṅkṛtayastadā । dhruvaṃ dhvanyaṅgatā tāsāṃ kāvyavṛttestadāśrayāt ।।} iti dhvanikāroktadiśā vastumātreṇa yatrālaṅkāro vyajyate na tatra guṇībhūtavyaṅgyatvam । sālaṅkārairdhvanestaiśca yogaḥ saṃsṛṣṭisaṅkaraiḥ ।
sālaṅkārairiti tairevālaṅkāraiḥ alaṅkārayuktaiśca taiḥ । taduktaṃ dhvanikṛtā {sa guṇībhūtavyaṅgyaiḥ sālaṅkāraiḥ saha prabhedaiḥ svaiḥ । saṃkarasaṃsṛṣṭibhyāṃ punarapyuddyotate bahudhā ।।} iti ।
anyonyayogādevaṃ syādbhedasaṃkhyātibhūyasī ।। evamanena prakāreṇa avāntarabhedagaṇanetiprabhūtatarā gaṇanā । tathāhiśṛṅgasyaiva bhedaprabhedagaṇanāyāmānantyam । kā gaṇanā tu sarveṣām । saṃkalanena punarasya dhvanestrayo bhedāḥ । vyaṅgyasya trirūpatvāt । tathāhikiñcidvācyatāṃ sahate kiñcittvanyathā । tatra vācyatāsaham avicitraṃ vicitraṃ ceti । avicitraṃ vastumātraṃ vicitraṃ tvalaṅkārarūpam । yadyapi prādhānyena tadalaṅkāryaṃ tathāpi brāhmaṇaśramaṇanyāyena tathocyate । rasādilakṣaṇastvarthaḥ svapne api na vācyaḥ । sa hi rasādiśabdena śṛṅgārādiśabdena vābhidhīyeta । na cābhidhīyate tatprayoge api vibhāvādyaprayoge tasyāpratipattestadaprayoge api vibhāvādiprayoge tasya pratipatteścetyanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vibhāvādyabhidhānadvāreṇaiva pratīyate iti niścīyate ।
tenāsau vyaṅgya eva । mukhyārthabādhādyabhāvānna punarlakṣaṇīyaḥ । arthāntarasaṃkramitātyantatiraskṛtavācyayorvastumātrarūpaṃ vyaṅgyaṃ vinā lakṣaṇaiva na bhavatīti prāk pratipāditam । śabdaśaktimūle tu abhidhāyā niyantraṇenānabhidheyasyārthāntarasya tena sahopamādera[raṃ]laṅkārasya ca nirvivādaṃ vyaṅgatvam । kā vārt[t]ā vyaṅgyasyābhidheyatāyām । {śabdavṛddhābhidheyāṃśca pratyakṣeṇātra paśyati । śrotuśca pratipannatvamanumānena ceṣṭayā ।।
anyathānupapattyā tu bodhecchaktiṃ dvayātmikām । arthāpattyāvabodheta saṃbandhaṃ tripramāṇakam ।।} iti pratipāditadiśā devadatta gāmānaya ityādyuttamavṛddhavākyaprayogāddeśāntaraṃ sāsnādimantamarthaṃ madhyamavṛddhe nayati sati anenāsmādvākyādevaṃvidho arthaḥ pratipannaḥ iti tacceṣṭayānumāya tayorakhaṇḍavākyavākyārthayorarthāpattyā vācyavācakabhāvalakṣaṇaṃ saṃbandhamavadhārya bālastatra vyutpadyate । parataḥ caitra gāmānaya devadatta aśvamānaya devadatta gāṃ naya ityādivākyaprayoge tasya tasya śabdasya taṃ tamarthamavadhārayatīti anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ pravṛttinivṛttikāri vākyameva prayogayogyamiti vākyasthitānāmeva padānāmanvitaiḥ padā[r]thairanvitānāmeva saṃketo gṛhyate iti viśiṣṭā eva padārthā vākyārthāḥ ।
na tu padārthānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyam । yadyapi vākyāntaraprayujyamānānyapi pratyabhijñāpratyayena tānyevaitāni padāni niścīyanta iti padārthāntaramātreṇānvitaḥ padārthaḥ saṃketagocaraḥ । tathāpi sāmānyāvacchādito viśeṣarūpa evāsau pratipadyate vyatiṣaktānāṃ padārthānāṃ tathābhūtatvādityanvitābhidhānavādinaḥ । teṣāmapi mate sāmānyaviśeṣarūpaḥ padārhaḥ saṃketaviṣaya ityativiśeṣabhūto vākyārthāntargatosaṃketitatvādavācya eva yatra padārthaḥ pratipadyate tatra dūre arthāntarabhūtasya niḥśeṣacyutetyādau vidhyādeścarcā ।
ananvito artho abhihitānvaye padārthāntaramātreṇānvitastvanvitābhidhāne anvitaviśeṣastvavācya eva ityubhayanaye apyapadārtha eva vākyārthaḥ । yadapyucyate naimittikānusāreṇa nimittāni kalpyante iti । tatra nimittatvaṃ kārakatvaṃ jñāpakatvaṃ vā śabdasya । prakāśakatvānna kārakatvam । jñāpakatvaṃ tu ajñātasya katham । jñātatvañca saṃketenaiva sa cānvitamātre evaṃ ca nimittasya niyatanimittatvaṃ yāvanna niścitaṃ tāvannaimittikasya pratītireva katham iti anaimittikānusāreṇa nimittāni kalpyante a; ityavicāritābhidhānam ।
ye tvabhidadhati so ayamiṣoriva dīrghadīrghataro vyāpāraḥ iti yatparaḥ śabdaḥ sa śabdārthaḥ iti vidhirevātra vācya iti । te apyatātparyajñāstātparyavācoyukterdevānāṃpriyāḥ । tathāhi {bhūtavyasamuccāraṇe bhūtaṃ bhavyāyopadiśyate} iti kārakapadārthāḥ kriyābhisaṇbandhāt sādhyāmānatāṃ prāpnuvanti । tataścādagdhadahananyāyena yāvadaprāptaṃ tāvadvidhīyate । yathā ṛtvikpracaraṇe pramāṇāntarāt siddhe {lohitoṣṇīṣā ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti} ityatra lohitoṣṇīṣatvamātraṃ vidheyaṃ havanasyānyataḥ siddheḥ {dadhnā juhoti} ityādau dadhyādeḥ karaṇatvamātraṃ vidheyam ।। kvacidubhayavidhiḥ kvacittrividhirapi yathā {raktaṃ paṭaṃ vayaḥ} ityādau ekavidhirdvividhistrividhirvā । tataśca {yadeva vidheyaṃ tatraiva tātparyam} ityupāttasyava śabdasyārthe tātparya na tu pratītamātre evaṃ hi {pūrvo dhāvati} ityādāvaparādyathapi kvacittātparyaṃ syāt । yattu {viṣaṃ bhakṣaya mā cānya gṛhe bhuṅkthāḥ} ityatra {etadgṛhe na bhoktavyam} ityatra tātparyamiti sa eva vākyārtha iti, ucyate tatra cakāra ekavākyatāsūcanārthaḥ na cākhyātavākyayor dvayoraṅgāṅgibhāva iti viṣabhakṣaṇavākyasya suhṛdvākyatvenāṅgatā kalpanīyeti {viṣabhakṣaṇādapi duṣṭametadgṛhe bhojanamiti sarvathā māsya gṛhe bhuṅkthāḥ} iti, upāttaśabdārthe eva tātparyam ।
yadi śabdaśruterantaraṃ yāvānartho labhyate tāvati śabdasyābhidhaiva vyāpāraḥ tataḥ kathaṃ abrāhmaṇa putraste jātaḥ brāhmaṇa kanyā te garbhiṇī'; ityādau harṣaśokādīnāmapi na vācyatvam । kasmācca lakṣaṇā lakṣaṇīye apyarthe dīrghadīrghatarābhidhāvyaāpāreṇaiva pratītisiddheḥ । kimiti ca śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ pūrvapūrvabalīyastvam ityanvitābhidhānavāde api vidherapi siddhaṃ vyaṅgyatvam ।। kiṃ ca {kuru rucim} iti padayorvaiparītye kāvyāntarvartini kathaṃ duṣṭatvam । na hmatrāsabhyo arthaḥ padārthāntarairanvitaḥ ityanabhidheya eveti evamādi aparityājyaṃ syāt । vibhāgakaraṇamanupapannaṃ syāt । na cānupapannaṃ sarvasyaiva vibhaktatayā pratibhāsāt । vācyavācakabhāvavyatirekeṇa vyaṅgyavyañjakatāśrayaṇe tu vyaṅgyasya bahuvidhatvāt kvacideva kasyacidevaucityenopapadyata eva vibhāgavyavasthā ।। {dvayaṃ gataṃ saṃprati śocanīyatāṃ samāgamaprārthanayā kapālinaḥ ।}
ityādau pinākyādipadavailakṣaṇyena kimiti kapālyādipadānāṃ kāvyānuguṇatvam । api ca vācyo arthaḥ sarvān pratipattṝn prati ekarūpa eveti niyato asau । na hi {gatostamarkaḥ} ityādau vācyo arthaḥ kvacidanyathā bhavati । pratīyamānastu tattatprakaraṇavaktṛpratipattrādiviśeṣasahāyatayā nānātvaṃ bhajate । tathā ca {gato astamarkaḥ} ityataḥ sapatnaṃ pratyavaskandanāvasara iti abhisaraṇamupakramyatāmiti prāptaprāyaste preyāniti karmakaraṇānnivartāmaha iti sāṃdhyo vidhirupakramyatāmiti dūraṃ mā gā iti surabhayo gṛhaṃ praveśyantāmiti saṃtāpodhunā na bhavatīti vikreyavastūni saṃhriyantāmiti nāgatodyāpi preyānityādiranavadhirvyaṅgyo arthaḥ tatra tatra pratibhāti । {mātsaryamutsārya vicārya kāryamāryāḥ samaryādamudāharantu ।
sevyānitambāḥ kimubhūdharāṇāmutasmarasmeravilāsinīnām ।।} dalanagalitamūrdhnā vidviṣāṃ svīkṛtā śrīḥ । tridivamapagatāṅgairvallabhā kīrtirebhiḥ ।।} ityādau nindāstutivapuṣā svarūpasya ।
{kassa va ṇa ho-i roso daṭṭhūṇa pi-ā-i savvaṇaṃ aharaṃ । sabhamarapaḍamagdhā-iṇi vāri-avāme sahasu eṇhiṃ ।।} [kasya vā na bhavati roṣo dṛṣṭvā priyāyā savraṇamaṣaram । sabhramarapadmāghrāyiṇi vāritavāse sahasvedānīm ।।]
ityādau sakhītatkāntādigatatvena viṣayasya ca bhede api yadyekatvam tat kvacidapi nīlapītādau bhedo na syāt । uktaṃ hi {ayameva hi bhedo bhedaheturvā yadviruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ kāraṇabhedaśca} iti । vācakānāmarthāpekṣā vyañjakānāṃ tu na tadapekṣatvamiti na vācakatvameva vyañjakatvam । kiṃ ca {vāṇīrakuḍaṅgu} ityādau pratīyamānamarthamabhivyajya vācyaṃ svarūpa eva yatra viśrāmyati tatra guṇībhūtavyaṅgyetātparybhūto apyarthaḥ svaśabdānabhidheyaḥ pratītipathamavataran kasya vyāpārasya viṣayatāmavalambatāmiti ।
premṇaḥ priye nocitam} iti {rāmo asau bhuvaneṣu vikramaguṇaiḥ prāptaḥ prasiddhiṃ parām} ityādau lakṣaṇīyo apyartho nānātvaṃ bhajate viśeṣavyapadeśahetuśca bhavati । tadavagamaśca śabdārthāyattaḥ prakaraṇādisavyapekṣaśca iti ko ayaṃ nūtanaḥ pratīyamāno nāma । ucyate lakṣaṇīyasyārthasya nānātve api anekārthaśabdābhidheyavanniyatatvameva । na khalu mukhyenārthenāniyatasaṃbandho lakṣayituṃ śakyate । pratīyamānastu prakaraṇādiviśeṣavaśena niyata saṃbandhaḥ aniyatasaṃbandhaḥ saṃbaddhasaṃbandhaśca dyotyate । {attā ettha ṇimajja-i ettha ahaṃ di-aha-e palo-ehi ।
mā pahi-a ratti-andha-a sejjā-e maha ṇimajjahisi ।।} [śvaśrūtatra nimajjati atrāhaṃ divasake pralokaya । mā pathika rātryandhaka śayyāyāmāvayornimaṅkṣyasi ।।] ityādu vivakṣitānyaparavācye dhvanau mukhyārthabādhaḥ । tatkathamatra lakṣaṇā । lakṣaṇāyāmapi vyañjanamavaśyamāśrayitavyamiti pratipāditam ।
yathā ca samayasavyapekṣā abhidhā tathā mukhyārthabādhāditrayasamayaviśeṣasavyapekṣā lakṣaṇā । ata evābhidhāpucchabhūtā setyāhuḥ । na ca lakṣaṇātmakameva dhvananaṃ tadanugamena tasya darśanāt । na ca tadanugatameva abhidhāvalambanenāpi tasya bhāvāt । na cobhayānusāryeva avācakavarṇānusāreṇāpi tasya dṛṣṭeḥ । na ca śabdānusāryeva aśabdātmakanetratribhāgāvalokanādigatatvenāpi tasya prasiddheḥ iti abhidhātātparyalakṣaṇātmakavyāpāratrayātivartī dhvananādiparyāyo vyāpāronapahnavanīya eva ।। tatra {attā ettha} ityādau niyatasaṃbandhaḥ {kasya va ṇa ho-i roso} ityādau, aniyatasaṃbandhaḥ । {viparī-ara-e lacchī bamhaṃ daṭaṭhūṇa ṇāhikamalaṭṭhaṃ ।
hariṇo dāhiṇaṇa-aṇaṃ rasā-ulā jhatti ḍhakke-i ।।} [viparītarate lakṣmīrvrahmāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā nābhikamalastham । harerdakṣiṇanayanaṃ rasākulā jhaṭiti sthagayati ।।] ityādau saṃbaddhasaṃbandhaḥ । atra hi haripadena dakṣiṇanayanasya sūryātmakatā vyajyate tannimīlanena sūryāstamayaḥ । tena padmasya saṃkocaḥ । tato brahmaṇaḥ sthaganam । tatra sati go apyāṅgasyādarśanena aniryantraṇaṃ nidhuvanavilasitamiti ।
{akhaṇḍabuddhinirgrāhyo vākyārtha eva vācyaḥ vākyameva ca vācakam} ।। iti ye apyāhuḥ tairapyavidyāpadapatitaiḥ padapadārthakalpanā kartavyaiveti tatpakṣe apyavaśyamuktodāharaṇādau vidhyādirvyaṅgya eva । nanu vācyādasaṃbaddhaṃ tāvanna pratīyate yataḥ kutaścit yasya kasyacidarthasya pratīteḥ prasaṅgāt । evaṃ ca saṃbandhāt vyaṅgyavyañjakabhāvopratibandhevaśyaṃ na bhavatīti vyāptatvena niyatadharminiṣṭhatvena ca trirūpālliṅgālliṅgijñānamanumānaṃ yat tadrūpaḥ paryavasyati । tathāhi {bhama dhammi-a vīsaddho so suṇa-o ajja māri-o teṇa ।
golāṇa-ikacchakuḍaṅgavāsiṇā dari-asīheṇa ।।} [bhrama dhārmika viśrabdhaḥ sa śūnako adya māritastena । godānadīkacchakuñjavāsinā dṛptasiṃhena ।।] atra gṛhe śvanivṛttyā bhramaṇaṃ vihitaṃ godāvarītīre siṃhopalabdherabhramaṇamanumāpayati । yat yata bhīrubhramaṇaṃ tattadbhayakāraṇanivṛttyupalabdhipūrvakaṃ godāvarītīre ca siṃhopalabdhiriti vyāpakaviruddhopalabdhiḥ ।
siṃhasadbhāvaḥ pratyakṣādanumānādvā na niścitaḥ । na ca vacanasya prāmāṇyamasti । arthenāpratibandhādityaasiddhaśca tatkathamevaṃvidhāddheyoḥ sādhyasiddhiḥ । tathā {niḥśeṣacyuta- } ityādau gamakatayā yāni candanacyavanādīnyupāttāni tāni kāraṇāntarato api bhavanti । ataścātraiva snānakāryatvenoktānīti nopabhoge eva pratibaddhānītyanaikāntikāni । vyaktivādinā cādhamapadasahāyānāmeṣāṃ vyañjakatvamuktam । na cātrādhamatvaṃ pramāṇapratipannamiti kathamanumānam । evaṃvidhādarthādevaṃvidho artha upapattyanapekṣatve api prakāśate iti vyaktivādinaḥ punastat adūṣaṇam ।।
iti kāvyaprakāśe dhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyasaṃkīrṇabhedanirṇayo nāma pañcama ullāsaḥ ।। śabdārthacitraṃ yatpūrvaṃ kāvyadvayamudāhṛtam । guṇaprādhānyatastatra sthitiścitrārthaśabdayoḥ ।। na tu śabdacitre arthasyācitratvamarthacitre vā śabdasya । tathā coktam
{rūpakādiralaṅkārastasyānyairbahudhoditaḥ । na kāntamapi nirbhūṣaṃ vibhāti vanitānanam ।। rūpakādimalaṅkāraṃ bāhyamācakṣate pare । supāṃ tiṅāṃ ca vyutpattiṃ vācāṃ vāñchantyalaṅkṛtim ।।
tadetadāhuḥ sauśabdyaṃ nārthavyutpattirīdṛśī । śabdābhidheyālaṅkārabhedādiṣṭaṃ dvayaṃ tu naḥ ।।} iti ।। stadanu virahottāmyattanvīkapolataladyutiḥ ।
sarasabisinīkandacchedacchavirmṛgalāñchanaḥ ।।} kṣobhāya pakṣmaladṛśāmalakāḥ khalāśca । ye kālatāṃ kuṭilatāmiva na tyajanti ।।} yadyapi sarvatra kāvyentataḥ vibhāvādirūpatayaiva paryavasānaṃ tathāpi sphuṭasya rasasyānupalambhādavyaṅgyametatkāvyadvayamuktam । atra ca śabdārthālaṅkārabhedādbahavo bhedāḥ te cālaṅkāranirṇaye nirṇeṣyante ।।
iti kāvyaprakāśe śabdārthacitranirūpaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭha ullāsaḥ ।। mukhyārthahatirdoṣo rasaśca mukhyastadāśrayādvācyaḥ । ubhayopayoginaḥ syuḥ śabdādyāstena teṣvapi saḥ ।। hatirapakarṣaḥ । śabdādyāḥ ityādyagrahaṇādvarṇaracane ।
duṣṭaṃ padaṃ śrutikaṭu cyutasaṃskṛtyaprayuktamasamartham । nihatārthamanucitārthaṃ nirarthakamavācakaṃ tridhāślīlam ।। sandigdhamapratītaṃ grāmyaṃ neyārthamatha bhavet kliṣṭam । avimṛṣṭavidheyāṃśaṃ viruddhamatikṛtsamāsagatameva ।।
{śrutikaṭu} paruṣavarṇarūpaṃ duṣṭam । yathā {anaṅgamangalagṛhāpāṅgabhaṅgitaraṅgitaiḥ । āliṅgitaḥ sa tanvaṅgyā kārtārthyaṃ labhate kadā ।।} atra kārtārthyamiti ।।
prāntaṃ hanta pulindasundarakarasparśakṣamaṃ labhyate । dīnaṃ tvāmanunāthate kucayugaṃ patrāvṛtaṃ mā kṛthāḥ ।।} atrānunāthate iti । {sarpiṣo nāthate} ityādāvāśiṣyeva nāthaterātmanepadaṃ vihitam । {āśiṣi nāthaḥ} iti । atra tu yācanamarthaḥ । tasmāt {anunāthati stanayugam} iti paṭhanīyam ।
{aprayuktaṃ} tathā āmnātamapi kavibhirnādṛtam । yathā {yathāyaṃ dāruṇācāraḥ sarvadaiva vibhāvyate । tathā manye daivato asya piśāco rākṣaso atha vā ।।} atra daivataśabdo {daivatāni puṃsi vā} iti puṃsyāmnāto api na kenacitprayujyate ।।
{asamarthaṃ} yattadarthaṃ paṭhyate na ca tatrāsya śaktiḥ । yathā {tīrthāntareṣu snānena samupārjitasatkṛtiḥ । surasrotasvinīmeṣa hanti saṃprati sādaram ।।} atra hantīti gamanārtham ।।
{nihatārthaṃ} yadubhayārthamaprasiddhe arthe prayuktam । yathā {yāvakarasārdrapādaprahāraśoṇitakacena dayitena । mugdhā sādhvasataralā vilokya paricumbitā sahasā ।।} atra śoṇitaśabdasya rudhiralakṣaṇenārthenojjvalīkṛtatvarūpo artho vyavadhīyate ।।
{tapasvibhiryā sucireṇa labhyate prayatnataḥ sattribhiriṣyate ca yā । prayānti tāmāśu gatiṃ yaśasvino raṇāśvamedhepaśutāmupāgatāḥ ।।} atra paśupadaṃ kātaratāmabhivyanaktītyanucitārtham ।। {nirarthakaṃ} pādapūraṇamātraprayojanaṃ cādipadam । yathā
{utphullakamalakesaraparāgagauradyute mama hi gauri । abhivāñchitaṃ prasiddhyatu bhagavati yuṣmatprasādena ।।} atra hiśabdaḥ ।। {avandhyakopasya vihanturāpadāṃ bhavanti vaśyāḥ svayameva dehinaḥ ।
amarṣaśūnyena janasya jantunā na jātahārdena na vidviṣādaraḥ ।।} atra jantupadamadātaryarthe vivakṣitaṃ tatra ca nābhidhāyakam । yathā vā tadvicchedarujāndhakāritamidaṃ dagdhaṃ dinaṃ kalpitam । tādṛgyāmavatīmayo bhavati me no jīvalokodhunā ।।}
atra dinamiti prakāśamayamityarthe vācakam । pratyagrālaktakābhāprasarakisakayo mañjumañjīrabhṛṅga । saṃbhūtāmbhojaśobhāṃ vidadhadabhibavo daṇḍapādo bhavānyāḥ ।।} atra dadhadityarthe vidadhaditi ।।
{aślīlam} traidheti vrīḍājugupsāmaṅgalavyañjakatvāt । yathā {sādhanaṃ sumahadyasya yannānyasya vilokyate । tasya dhīśālinaḥ ko anyaḥ sahatārālitāṃ bhruvam ।। } kaścvitkesaradūṣitekṣaṇa iva vyāmīlya netre sthitaḥ ।
bhrāntyā dhūrtatayātha vānatimṛtetenāniśañcumbitā ।। } ghanarucirakalāpo niḥsapatno adya jātaḥ । sati kusumasanāthe kaṃ haredeṣa barhī ।। } eṣu sādhanavāyuvināśaśabdāḥ vrīḍādivyañjakāḥ ।।
{āliṅgitastatrabhavān saṃparāye jayaśriyā । āśīḥparaṃparāṃ vandyāṃ karṇe kṛtvā kṛpāṃ kuru ।।} atra vandyāṃ kiṃ haṭhahṛtamahilāyāṃ kiṃ vā namasyāmiti saṃdehaḥ ।। {apratītaṃ} yatkevale śāstre prasiddham । yathā
{samyagjñānamahājyotirdalitāśayatājuṣaḥ । vidhīyamānamapyetanna bhavetkarmabandhanam ।।} {grāmyaṃ} yatkevale loke sthitam । yathā {rākāvibhāvarīkāntasaṃkrāntadyuti te mukham ।
tapanīyaśilāśobhā kaṭiśca harate manaḥ ।।} atra kaṭiriti ।। {nirūḍhā lakṣaṇāḥ kāścit sāmarthyāt abhidhānavat । kriyante sāṃprataṃ kāścit kāścinnaiva tvaśaktitaḥ ।।}
yanniṣiddhaṃ lākṣaṇikam । yathā {śaratkālasamullāsipūrṇimāśarvarīpriyam । karoti te mukhaṃ tanvi capeṭāpātanātithim ।।} atra capeṭāpātanena nirjitatvaṃ lakṣyate ।
atha samāsagatameva duṣṭamiti saṃbandhaḥ, anyat kevalaṃ samāsagataṃ ca ।। {kliṣṭaṃ} yataḥ arthapratipattirvyavahitā । yathā {atrilocanasaṃbhūtajyotirudgamabhāsibhiḥ । sadṛśaṃ śobhatetyarthaṃ bhūpāla tava ceṣṭitam ।।}
atrātrilocanasaṃbhūtasya candrasya jyotirudgamena bhāsibhiḥ kumudairityarthaḥ ।। {avimṛṣṭavidheyāṃśam} avimṛṣṭaḥ prādhānyenānirdiṣṭo vidheyāṃśo yatra tat । yathā dhauteśāṅghriprasādopanatajayajagajjātamithyāmahimnām । doṣṇāṃ caiṣāṃ kimetat phalamiha nagarīrakṣaṇe yat prayāsaḥ ।।}
atra mithyāmahimatvaṃ nānuvādyam api tu vidheyam । yathā vā {srastāṃ nitambādavaropayantī punaḥ punaḥ kesaradāmakāñcīm । nyāsīkṛtāṃ sthānavidā smareṇa dvitīyamaurvīmiva kārmukasya ।।} atra dvitīyatvamātramutprekṣyam । maurvīṃ dvitīyāmiti yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ । yathā vā
{vapurvirūpākṣamalakṣyajanmatā digambaratvena niveditaṃ vasu । vareṣu yadbālamṛgākṣi mṛgyate tadasti kiṃ vyastamapi trilocane ।।} atra {alakṣitā janiḥ} iti vācyam । yathā vā saṃdānanaikasadanaṃ kṣaṇamapyamuktā ।
tāntiṃ tanoti tava saṃprati dhigdhigasmān ।।} atra {na muktā} iti saṃnaddho ayaṃ vidheyaḥ । yathā suradhanuridaṃ dūrākṛṣṭaṃ na tasya śarāsanam । kanakanikaṣasnigdhā vidyut priyā na mamorvaśī ।।}
ityatra । na tvamuktatānuvādenānyadatra kiñcidvihitam । yathā {jugopātmānamatrasto bheje dharmamanāturaḥ । agṛdhnurādade so arthānasaktaḥ sukhamanvabhūt ।।} ityatra atrastatvādyanuvādenātmano gopanādi ।।
{sudhākarakarākāraviśāradaviceṣṭitaḥ । akāryamitrameko asau tasya kiṃ varṇayāmahe ।।} atra {kāryaṃ vinā mitram} iti vivakṣitam {akārye mitram iti} tu pratītiḥ । yathā vā {cirakālapariprāptalocanānandadāyinaḥ ।
kāntā kāntasya sahasā vidadhāti galagraham ।।} atra {kaṇṭhagraham} iti vācyam । yathā vā tena vyārujatā dhanurbhagavato devādbhavānīpateḥ । skandaḥ skanda iva priyo ahamatha vā śiṣyaḥ kathaṃ vismṛtaḥ ।।}
atra bhavānīpatisabdo bhavānyāḥ patyantare pratītiṃ karoti । yathā vā {gorapi yadvāhanatāṃ prāptavataḥ so api girisutāsiṃhaḥ । savidhe nirahaṅkāraḥ pāyādvaḥ so ambikāramaṇaḥ ।।} atrāmbikāramaṇa iti viruddhāṃ dhiyamutpādayati ।।
{sā dūre ca sudhāsāndrataraṅgitavilocanā । bahirnirhrādanārho ayaṃ kālaśca samupāgataḥ ।।} evamanyadapi jñeyam ।। apāsya cyutasaṃskāramasamarthaṃ nirarthakam ।
vākye api doṣāḥ santyete padasyāṃśe api kecana ।। kecana na punaḥ sarve । krameṇodāharaṇam {so adhyauṣṭa vedāṃstridaśānayaṣṭa pitṛnatārpsītsamamaṃsta bandhūn । vyajeṣṭa ṣaḍavargamaraṃsta nītau samūlaghātaṃ nyavadhīdarīṃśca ।।}
{sa rātu vo duścyavano bhāvukānāṃ paraṃparām । aneḍamūkatādyaiśca dyatu doṣairasaṃmatān ।।} atra duścyavana indraḥ aneḍamūko mūkabadhiraḥ ।। {sāyakasahāyabāhormakaradhvajaniyamitakṣamādhipateḥ ।
abjarucibhāsvaraste bhātitarāmavanipa ślokaḥ ।।} atra sāyakādayaḥ śabdaḥ khaḍgābdhibhūcandrayaśaḥparyāyāḥ śarādyarthatayā prasiddhaḥ ।। yaśo gāyantyete diśi diśi ca nagnāstava vibho । tathāpi tvatkīrtirbhramati vigatācchādanamiha ।।}
atra kuvindādiśabdo arthāntaraṃ pratipādayannupaślokyamānasya tiraskāraṃ vyanaktītyanucitārthaḥ । {prābhrabhrāḍviṣṇudhāmāpya viṣamāśvaḥ karotyayam । nidrāṃ sahasraparṇānāṃ palāyanaparāyaṇām ।।} atra prābhrabhrāḍviṣṇudhāmacviṣamāśvanidrāparṇaśabdāḥ prakuṣṭajaladagaganasaptāśvasaṃkocadalānāmavācakāḥ ।।
{bhūpaterupasarpantī kampanā vāmalocanā । tattatpraharaṇotsāhavatī mohanamādadhau ।।} atropasarpaṇapraharaṇamohanaśabdā vrīḍādāyitvādaślīlāḥ । {tenyairvāntaṃ samaśnanti parotsargaṃ ca bhuñjate ।
itarārthagrahe yeṣāṃ kavīnāṃ syātpravartanam ।।} atra vāntotsargapravartanaśabdā jugupsādāyinaḥ । {pitṛvasatimahaṃ vrajāmi tāṃ saha parivārajanena yatra me । bhavati sapadi pāvakānvaye hṛdayamaśeṣitaśokaśalyakam ।।}
atra pitṛgṛhamityādau vivakṣite śmaśānādipratītāvamaṅgalārthatvam । {surālayollāsaparaḥ prāptaparyāptakampanaḥ । mārgaṇapravaṇo bhāsvadbhūtireṣa vilokyatām ।।} atra kiṃ surādiśabdā devasenāśaravibhūtyarthāḥ kiṃ madirādyarthāḥ iti saṃdehaḥ ।।
{tasyādhimātropāyasya tīvrasaṃvegatājuṣaḥ । dṛḍhabhūmiḥ priyaprāptau yatnaḥ sa phalitaḥ sakhe ।।} atrādhimātropāyādayaḥ śabdā yogaśāstramātraprayuktatvādapratītāḥ ।। {tāmbūlabhṛtagalloyaṃ bhallaṃ jalpati mānuṣaḥ ।
karoti khādanaṃ pādaṃ sadaiva tu yathā tathā ।।} atra gallādayaḥ śabdāḥ grāmyāḥ ।। {vastravaidūryacaraṇaiḥ kṣatasattvarajaḥparā । niṣkampā racitā netrayuddhaṃ vedaya sāṃpratam ।।}
atrāmbararatnapādaiḥ kṣatatamā acalā bhūḥ kṛtā netradvandvaṃ bodhayeti neyārthatā ।। {dhammillasya na kasya prekṣya nikāmaṃ kuraṅgaśāvākṣyāḥ । rajyatyapūrvabandhavyutpattermānasaṃ śobhām ।।} atra dhammillasya śobhāṃ prekṣya kasya mānasaṃ na rajyatīti saṃbandhe kliṣṭatvam ।।
so apyatraiva nihanti rākṣasakulaṃ jīvatyaho rāvaṇaḥ । svargagāmaṭikāviluṇṭhanavṛthocchūnaiḥ kimebhirbhujaiḥ ।।} atra aayameva nyakkāraḥ'; iti vācyam । ucchūnatvamātraṃ cānuvādyam, na vṛthātvaviśeṣitam । atra ca śabdaracanā viparītā kṛteti vākyasyaiva doṣo na vākyārthasya । yathā vā {apāṅgasaṃsargi taraṅgitaṃ dṛśorbhruvorarālāntavilāsi vellitam ।
visāri romāñcanakañcukaṃ tanostanoti yo asau subhage tavāgataḥ ।।} atra yo asāviti padadvayamanuvādyamātrapratītikṛt । tathāhi prakrāntaprasiddhānubhūtārthaviṣayastacchabdo yacchabdopādānaṃ nāpekṣate । {kātaryaṃ kevalā nītiḥ śauryaṃ śvāpadaceṣṭitam ।
ataḥ siddhiṃ sametābhyāmubhābhyāmanviyeṣa saḥ ।।} {dvayaṃ gataṃ saṃprati śocanīyatāṃ samāgamaprārthanayā kapālinaḥ । kalā ca sā kāntimatī kalāvatastvamasya lokasya ca netrakaumudī ।।} te locane pratidiśaṃ vidhure kṣipantī ।
dhūmāndhitena dahanena na vīkṣitāsi ।।} yacchabdastūttaravākyānugatatvenopāttaḥ sāmarthyātpūrvavākyānugatasya tacchabdasyopādānaṃ nāpekṣate । yathā {sādhu candramasi puṣkaraiḥ kṛtaṃ mīlitaṃ yadabhirāmatādhike । udyatā jayani kāminīmukhe tena sāhasamanuṣṭhitaṃ punaḥ ।।}
prāgupāttastu yacchabdastacchabdopādānaṃ vinā sākāṅkṣaḥ । yathā atraiva śloke ādyapādayorvyatyāse । dvayorupādāne tu nirākāṅkṣatvaṃ prasiddham । anupādāne api sāmarthyātkutraciddvayamapi gamyate । yathā jānanti te kimapi tān prati naiṣa yatnaḥ । kālo hyayaṃ niravadhirvipulā ca pṛthvī ।।} atra ya utpatsyate taṃ pratīti । evaṃ ca tacchabdānupādāne atra sākāṅkṣatvam । na cāsāviti
tacchabdārthamāha । {asau maruccumbitacārukesaraḥ prasannatārādhipamaṇḍalāgraṇīḥ । viyuktarāmāturadṛṣṭivīkṣito vasantakālo hanumānivāgataḥ ।।} atra hi na tacchabdārthapratītiḥ ।
{karabālakarāladoḥ sahāyo yudhi yosau vijayārjunaikamallaḥ । yadi bhūpatinā sa tatra kārye viniyujyeta tataḥ kṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ syāt ।।} atra sa ityasyānarthakyaṃ syāt । {yovikalpamidamarthamaṇḍalaṃ paśyatīśa nikhilaṃ bhavadvapuḥ ।
ātmapakṣaparipūrite jagatyasya nityasukhinaḥ kuto bhayam ।।} itīdaṃśabdavadadaḥśabdastacchabdārthamabhidhatte iti ucyate । tarhyatraiva vākyāntare upādānamarhati na tatraiva । yacchabdasya hi nikaṭe sthitaḥ prasiddhiṃ parāmṛśati । yathā {yattadūrjitamatyugraṃ kṣātraṃ tejosya bhūpateḥ । dīvyatākṣaistadānena nūnaṃ tadapiṃ hāritam ।।}
ityatra tacchabdaḥ । dhuryāṃ lakṣmīmatha mayi bhṛśaṃ dhehi deva prasīda । bhadraṃ bhadraṃ vitara bhagavan bhūyase maṅgalāya ।।} atra yadyadityuktvā tanme ityuktam । ucyate yadyaditi yena kenacidrūpeṇa sthitaṃ sarvātmakaṃ vastvākṣiptaṃ tathābhūtameva tacchabdena parāmṛśyate ।
mātrā strīlaghutāṃ gatā kimatha vā mātaiva madhyamā । rmātā tātakalatramityanucitaṃ manye vidhātrā kṛtaṃ ।।} atrāryasyeti tātasyeti ca vācyam । na tvanayoḥ samāse guṇībhāvaḥ kāryaḥ । evaṃ samāsāntare apyudāhāryam ।। {śritakṣamā raktabhuvaḥ śivāliṅgitamūrtayaḥ ।
vigrahakṣapaṇenādya śerate te gatāsukhāḥ ।।} atra kṣamādiguṇayuktāḥ sukhamāsate iti vivakṣite hatā iti viruddhā pratītiḥ ।। pariṇativirasatvātsaṃgamenāṅganāyāḥ । stadapi na hariṇākṣīṃ vismaratyantarātmā ।।}
atra tvāditi । yathā vā {tadgaccha siddhyai kuru devakāryamartho ayamarthāntaralabhya eva । apekṣate pratyayamaṅgalabdhyai bījāṅkuraḥ prāgudayādivāmbhaḥ ।।} atra ddhyai vdhyai, iti kaṭu ।।
{yaścāpsarovibhramamaṇḍanānāṃ saṃpādayitrīṃ śikharairbibharti । balāhakacchedavibhaktarāgāmkālasaṃdhyāmiva dhātumattām ।।} atra mattāśabdaḥ kṣībārthe nihatārthaḥ ।। protsarpaddhirahānalena ca tataḥ saṃtāpitānāṃ dṛśām ।
bhallīnāmiva pānakarma kurute kāmaṃ kuraṅgekṣaṇā ।।} atra dṛśāmiti bahuvacanaṃ nirarthakam kuraṅgekṣaṇāyā ekasyā evopādānāt । na cālasavalitairityādivat vyāpārabhedādbahutvam vyāpārāṇāmanupāttatvāt । na ca vyāpāretra dṛkśabdo vartate । atraiva akurute a; ityātmanepadamapyanarthakam । pradhānakriyāphalasya kartrasaṃbandhe kartrabhiprāyakriyāphalābhāvāt ।। śastravyastaḥ sadanamudadhirbhūriyaṃ hantakāraḥ । baddhaspardhastava paraśunā lajjate candrahāsaḥ ।।}
atra vijeya iti kṛtyapratyayaḥ ktapratyayārthavācakaḥ ।। {atipelavamatiparimitavarṇaṃ laghutaramudāharati śaṭhaḥ । paramārthataḥ sa hṛdayaṃ vahati punaḥ kālakūṭaghaṭitamiva ।।} atra pelavaśabdaḥ ।।
snānena śāstrapariśīlanakīlanena । yo ayaṃ dṛśoḥ patati kasyacideva puṃsaḥ ।।} atra pūyaśabdaḥ ।। {vinayapraṇaaikaketanaṃ satataṃ yobhavadaṅga tādṛśaḥ ।
kathamadya sa tadvadīkṣyataāṃ tadabhipretapadaṃ samāgataḥ ।।} atha pretaśabdaḥ ।। {kasmin karmaṇi sāmarthyamasya nottapatetarām । ayaṃ sādhycarastasmādañjalirbadhyatāmiha ।।}
atra kiṃ pūrvaṃ sādhuḥ uta sādhuṣu caratīti saṃdehaḥ ।। {kimucyate asya bhūpālamaulimālāmahāmaṇeḥ । sudurlabhaṃ vacobāṇaistejo yasya vibhāvyate ।।} atra vacaḥśabdena gīḥśabdo lakṣyate । atra khalu na kevalaṃ pūrvapadam yāvaduttarapadamapi paryāyaparivartanaṃ na kṣamate । jaladhyādāvuttarapadameva vaḍavānalādau pūrvapadameva ।।
yadyapyasamarthasyaivāprayuktādayaḥ kecana bhedāḥ tathāpyanyairālaṅkārikairvibhāgena pradarśitā iti bhedapradarśanenodāhartavyā iti ca vibhajyoktāḥ ।। pratikūlavarṇamupahataluptavisargaṃ visandhi hatavṛttam । nyūnādhikakathitapadaṃ patatprakarṣaṃ samāptapunarāttam ।। ardhāntaraikavācakamabhavanmatayogamanabhihitavācyam ।
apadasthapadasamāsaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ garbhitaṃ prasiddhihatam ।। bhagnaprakramamakramamamataparārthaṃ ca vākyameva tathā । rasānuguṇatvaṃ varṇānāṃ vakṣyate । tadviparītaṃ pratikūlavarṇam । yathā śṛṅgāre {akuṇṭhotkaṇṭhayā pūrṇamākaṇṭhaṃ kalakaṇṭhi mām ।
kambukaṇṭhyāḥ kṣaṇaṃ kaṇṭhe kuru kaṇṭhārtimuddhara ।।} kṣatrādeva tathāvidhaḥ paribhavastātasya keśagrahaḥ । yadrāmeṇa kṛtaṃ tadeva kurute droṇātmajaḥ krodhanaḥ ।।} atra hi vikaṭavarṇatvaṃ dīrghasamāsatvaṃ cocitam । yathā
krodhapreritabhīmabhārgavabhujastambhāpaviddhaḥ ksaṇāt । ryenānena jagatsu khaṇḍaparaśurdevo haraḥ khyāpyate ।।} yatra tu na krodhastatra caturthapādābhidhāne tathaiva śabdaprayogaḥ ।। upahata utvaṃ prāpto lupto vā visargo yatra tat । yathā
{dhīro vinīto nipuṇo varākāro nṛpo atra saḥ । yasya bhṛtyā balotsiktā bhaktā buddhiprabhāvitāḥ ।।} visaṃdhi saṃdhervairūpyam viśleṣoślīlatvaṃ kaṣṭatvaṃ ca । tatrādyaṃ yahtā indordyutiṃ dadhati yāni rasātalentaḥ ।
ātanvatī vijayasaṃpadametya bhātaḥ ।।} {tata udita udārahārahāridyutiruccairudayācalādivenduḥ । nijavaṃśa udāttakāntakāntirbata muktāmaṇivaccakāstyanarghaḥ ।।} saṃhitāṃ na karomīti svacchayā sakṛdapi doṣaḥ pragṛhyādihetukatve tvasakṛt ।।
{vegāduḍḍīya gagane calaṇḍāmaraceṣṭitaḥ । ayamuttapate pastrī tato atraiva ruciṅkuru ।।} atra saṃdhāvaślīlatā ।। {urvyasāvatra tarvālī marvante cārvavasthitiḥ ।
mātrarju yujyate gantuṃ śiro namaya tanmanāk ।।} hataṃ lakṣaṇānusaraṇe apyaśravyam । aprāptagurubhāvāntalaghu rasānanuguṇaṃ ca vṛttaṃ yatra tat hatavṛttam । krameṇodāharaṇam madhuramadhikaṃ cūtasyāpi prasannarasaṃ phalam । vadatu yadihānyatsvādu syātpriyādaśanacchadāt ।।}
atra ayadihānyatsvādu syāt'; ityaśravyam । yathā vā {jaṃ parihariuṃ tīrai maṇaaṃpi ṇa sundarattaṇaguṇeṇa । aha ṇavaraṃ jassa doso paḍipakkhehiṃ pi paḍivaṇṇo ।।} [yat parihartuṃ tīryate manāgapi na sundaratvaguṇena ।
atha kevalaṃ yasya doṣaḥ pratipakṣairapi pratipannaḥ ।।] atra dvitīyatatīyagaṇau sakārabhakārau । {vikasitasahakāratārahāriparimalaguñjitapuñjitadvirephaḥ । navakisalayacārucāmaraśrīharati munerapi mānasaṃ vasantaḥ ।।}
atra hāriśabdaḥ । hāripramuditasaurabheti pāṭho yuktaḥ । yathā vā saṃbhārāḥ khalu tenya eva vidhinā yaireṣa sṛṣṭo yuvā । dṛṣṭe yatra patanti mūḍhamanasāmastrāṇi vastrāṇi ca ।।} atra avastrāṇyapi'; iti pāṭhe laghurapi gurutāṃ bhajate ।।
{hā nṛpa hā budha hā kavibandho viprasahasrasamāśraya deva । mugdhavidagdhasabhāntararatna kvāsi gataḥ kva vayaṃ ca tavaite ।।} vane vyādhaiḥ sārdhaṃ suciramuṣitaṃ valkaladharaiḥ । guruḥ khedaṃ khinne mayi bhajati nādyāpi kuruṣu ।।}
atrāsmābhiriti "khinna" ityasmātpūrvamitthamiti ca ।। {sphaṭikākṛtinirmalaḥ prakāmaṃ pratisaṃkrāntaniśātaśāstratattvaḥ । aviruddhasamanvitoktiyuktiḥ pratimallāstamayodayaḥ sa ko api ।।} atra ākṛtiśabdaḥ । yathā vā
{idamanucitamakramaśca puṃsāṃ yadiha jarāsvapi mānmathā vikārāḥ । yadapi ca na kṛtaṃ nitambinīnāṃ stanapatanāvadhi jīvitaṃ rataṃ vā ।।} atra kṛtamiti । kṛtaṃ pratyuta prakramabhaṅgamāvahati । tathā ca ayadapi ca na kuraṅgalocanānām'; iti pāṭhe nirākāṅkṣaiva pratītiḥ ।। parimilananimīlatpāṇḍimā gaṇḍapālī ।
smaranarapatilīlāyauvarājyābhiṣekam ।।} atra līleti ।। kaḥ kaḥ kaṃ kamalākaraṃ vikamakaṃ kartuṃ karī nodyataḥ । siṃhīsnehavilāsabaddhavasatiḥ pañcānano vartate ।।}
jhaṅkāro ratimañkarīmadhulihāṃ līlācakorīdhvaniḥ । kvāṇaḥ prema tanotu vo navavayolāsyāya veṇusvanaḥ ।।} viracaya sicayāntaṃ mūrdhni gharmaḥ kaṭhoraḥ । pathi pathikavadhūbhirvīkṣitā śikṣitā ca ।।}
abhavan mataḥ yogaḥ yatra tat । yathā rlīlāpānabhuvaśca nandanavanacchāyāsu yaiḥ kalpitāḥ । kiṃ taistvatparitoṣakāri vihitaṃ kiñcitpravādocitam ।।} atra {guṇānāṃ ca parārthatvādasaṃbandhaḥ samatvātsyāt} ityuktanayena yacchabdanidaśyānāmarthānāṃ parasparasamanvayena yair ityatra viśeṣasyāpratītiriti । {kṣapācāribhiḥ} iti pāṭhe yujyate samanvayaḥ । yathā vā
kalānāṃ sīmānaṃ paramiha yuvāmeva bhajathaḥ । ataḥ śeṣaṃ yatsyājjitamiha tadānīṃ guṇitayā ।।} atra yadityatra taditi tadānīmityatra yadeti vacanaṃ nāsti । {cetsyāt} iti yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ । yathā vā devākarṇaya yena yena sahasā yadyatsamāsāditam ।
tena tvaṃ bhavatā ca kīrtiratulā kīrtyā ca lokatrayam ।।} karmatve kodaṇḍaḥ śarā iti prāptam । na ca yacchabdārthastadviśeṣaṇaṃ vā kodaṇḍādi । na ca kena kenetyādi praśnaḥ । yathā vā śastravyastaḥ sadanamudadhirbhūriyaṃ hantakāraḥ ।
baddhasparddhastava paraśunā lajjate candrahāsaḥ" ।।} ityādau bhārgavasya nindāyāṃ tātparyam । kṛtavateti paraśau sā pratīyate । akṛtavataḥ'; iti tu pāṭhe matayogo bhavati । yathā vā saṃgrāmādhvaradīkṣito narapatiḥ patnī gṛhītavratā । rājyanyopanimantraṇāya rasati sphītaṃ hato dundubhiḥ ।।}
atrādhvaraśabdaḥsamāse guṇībhūta iti na tadarthaḥ sarvaiḥ saṃyujyate । yathā vā pratyagrālaktakābhāprasarakisalayo mañjumañjīrabhṛṅgaḥ । saṃbhūtāmbhojaśobhāṃ vidadhavabhinavo daṇḍapādo bhavānyāḥ ।।} atra daṇḍapādagatā nijatanuḥpratīyate bhavānyāḥ saṃbandhinī tu vivakṣitā ।।
avaśyavaktavyamanuktaṃ yatra । yathā ratyadbhutairapahṛtasya tathāpi nāsthā । saundaryasārasamudāyamayaḥ padārthaḥ ।।} atra aapahṛto asmi'; ityapahṛtatvasya vidhirvācyaḥ tathāpītyasya dvitīyavākyagatatvenaivopapatteḥ । yathā vā
prāptaḥ surāsuramanorathadūravartī । lakṣmīphalāmasurarājasutāṃ vidhāya ।।} atra manorathānāmapi dūravartītyapyartho vācyaḥ । yathā vā {tvayi nibaddharateḥ priyavādinaḥ praṇayabhaṅgaparāṅmukhacetasaḥ ।
kamaparādhalavaṃ mama paśyasi tyajasi mānini dāsajanaṃ yataḥ ।।} atra aaparādhasya lavamapi'; iti vācyam ।। vupāhitāṃ vakṣasi pīvarastane । vasanti hi premṇi guṇā na vastuṣu ।।}
atra akācinna vijahau'; iti vācyam । yathā vā mudrāṅkaḥ śitikandharenduśakalenāntagkappolasthalam । pronmṛṣṭaḥ karapallavena kuṭilātāmracchaviḥ pātu vaḥ ।।} atra nakhalakṣmetyataḥ pūrvaṃ akuṭilatāmra a; iti vācyam ।।
sthātuṃ vāñchati māna eṣa dhigiti krodhādivālohitaḥ । phullatkairavakośaniḥsaradaliśreṇīkṛpāṇaṃ śaśī ।।} atra kruddhasyoktau samāso na kṛtaḥ kaveruktau tu kṛtaḥ ।। saṃkīrṇam yatra vākyāntarasya padāni vākyāntaramanupraviśanti । yathā
{kimiti na paśyasi kopaṃ pādagataṃ bahuguṇaṃ gṛhāṇemam । nanu muñca hṛdayanāthaṃ kaṇṭhe manasastamorūpam ।।} atra pādagataṃ bahuguṇaṃ hṛdayanārthaṃ kimiti na paśyasi । imaṃ kaṇṭhe gṛhāṇa manasastamorūpaṃ kopaṃ muñceti । ekavākyatāyāṃ tu kliṣṭamiti bhedaḥ ।। garbhitam yatra vākyasya madhye vākyāntaramanupraviśati । yathā
{parāpakāraniratairdurjanaiḥ saha saṃgatiḥ । vadāmi bhavatastattvaṃ na vidheyā kathañcana ।।} atra tṛtīyapādo vākyāntaramadhye praviṣṭaḥ । yathā vā mātaṅgānāmapīhopari parapuruṣairyā ca dṛṣṭā patantī ।
bhṛtyebhyaḥ śrīniyogādgaditumiva gatetyambudhiṃ yasya kīrtiḥ ।।} atra {viditaṃ testu} iti etatkṛtam । pratyuta lakṣmīstatopasaratīti viruddhamatikṛt ।। {mañjīrādiṣu raṇitaprāyaṃ pakṣiṣu ca kūjitaprabhṛti । stanitamaṇitādi surate meghādiṣu garjitapramukham ।।}
iti prasiddhimatikrāntam । yathā pracaṇḍaghanagarjitapratirutānukārī muhuḥ । kuto adya samarodadherayambhūtapūrvaḥ puraḥ ।।} atra ravo maṇḍūkādiṣu prasiddho na tūktaviśeṣe siṃhanāde ।।
bhagnaḥ prakramaḥ prastāvaḥ yatra । yathā {nāthe niśāyā niyaterniyogādastaṃ gate hanta niśāpi yātā । kulāṅganānāṃ hi daśānurūpaṃ nātaḥparaṃ bhadrataraṃ samasti ।।} atra {gate} iti prakrānte {yātā} iti prakṛteḥ । {gatā niśāpi} iti tu yuktam ।
nanu {naikaṃ padaṃ dviḥ prayojyaṃ prāyeṇa} ityanyatra kathitapadaṃ duṣṭamiti cehaivoktam । tatkathamekasya padasya dviḥprayogaḥ । ucyate । uddeśyapratinirdeśyavyatirikto viṣaya ekapadaprayoganiṣedhasya । tadvati viṣaye pratyuta tasyaiva padasya sarvanāmro vā prayogaṃ vinā doṣaḥ । tathāhi {udeti savitā tāmrastāmra evāstameti ca । saṃpattau ca vipattau ca mahatāmekarūpatā ।।} atra rakta evāstametīti yadi kriyeta tadā padāntarapratipāditaḥ sa evārtho arthāntaratayeva pratibhāsamānaḥ pratītiṃ sthagayati ।। yathā vā
{yaśodhigantuṃ sukhalipsayā vā manuṣyasaṃkhyāmativartituṃ vā । nirutsukānāmabhiyogabhājāṃ samutsukevāṅkamupaiti siddhiḥ ।।} atra pratyayasya । asukhamīhituṃ vā'; iti yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ । {te himālayamāmantrya punaḥ prekṣya ca śūlinam ।
siddhaṃ cāsmai nivedyārthaṃ taddhisṛṣṭā kkhamudyayuḥ ।।} atra sarvanāmnaḥ । aanena visṛṣṭāḥ'; iti tu vācyam । {mahībhṛtaḥ putravato api dṛṣṭistasminnapatye na jagāma tṛptim । anantapuṣpasya madhorhi cūte dvirephamālā saviśeṣasaṅgā ।।}
atra paryāyasya । {mahībhṛtopatyavato api} iti yuktam । {atra satyapi putre kanyārūpe apyapatye sneho abhūt} iti kecitsamarthayante । {vipado abhibhavantyavikramaṃ rahayatyāpadupetamāyatiḥ । niyatā laghutā nirāyateragarīyānna padaṃ nṛpaśriyaḥ ।।} atropasargasya paryāyasya ca । {tadabhibhavaḥ kurute nirāyatim} । laghutāṃ bhajate nirāyatirlaghutāvānna padaṃ nṛpaśriyaḥ ।। iti yuktam ।
raśrīkāḥ kāścidantardiśa iva dadhire dāhamudbhrāntasattvāḥ । prasthāne pārthivānāmaśivamiti puro bhāvi nāryaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ ।।} atra vacanasya । akāśicitkīrṇā rajobhirdivamanuvidadhurmandavaktrenduśobhā niḥśrīkāḥ'; iti akampamānāḥ'; ityatra akampamāpuḥ'; iti ca paṭhanīyam । chāyābaddhakadambakaṃ mṛgakulaṃ romanthamabhyasyatāṃ ।
viśrāntiṃ labhatāmidaṃ ca śithilajyābandhamasmaddhanuḥ ।।} atra kārakasya । {viśrabdhā racayantu śūkaravarā mustākṣatim} ityaduṣṭam । vavitathamadādhmāte roṣānmunāvabhigacchati । sphurati rabhasātpāṇiḥ pādopasaṃgrahaṇāya ca ।।}
atra kramasya । pādopasaṃgrahaṇāyati pūrvaṃ vācyam । evamanyadapyanusartavyam ।। avidyamānaḥ kramo yatra । yathā samāgamaprārthanayā kapālinaḥ । tvamasya lokasya ca netrakaumudī ।।}
atra tvaṃśabdānantaraṃ cakāro yuktaḥ । yathā vā rvaktre pārśve tathaiṣā prativasati mahākuṭṭanī khaḍgayaṣṭiḥ । procyevetthaṃ prakopācchaśikarasitayā yasya kīrtyā prayātam ।।} atra {itthaṃ procyeva} iti nyāyyam । tathā
{lagnaṃ rāgāvṛtāṅgyā- ।।} ityadau {iti śrīniyogāt} iti vācyam ।। amataḥ prakṛtaviruddhaḥ parārtho yatra । yathā {rāmamanmathaśareṇa tāḍitā duḥsahena hṛdaye niśācarī ।
gandhavadrudhiracandanokṣitā jīviteśavasatiṃ jagāma sā ।।} atra prakṛte rase viruddhasya śṛṅgārasya vyañjakoparo arthaḥ ।। artho apuṣṭaḥ kaṣṭo vyāhatapunaruktaduṣkramagrāmyāḥ ।। saṃdigdho nirhetuḥ prasiddhividyāviruddhaśca ।
anavīkṛtaḥ saniyamāniyamaviśeṣā viśeṣaparivṛttāḥ ।। sākāṅkṣo apadayuktaḥ sahacarabhinnaḥ prakāśitaviruddhaḥ । vidhyanuvādāyuktastyaktapunaḥsvīkṛto aślīlaḥ ।। duṣṭa iti saṃbadhyate । kraṃeṇodāharaṇam
