{ativitatagaganasaraṇiprasaraṇaparimuktaviśramānandaḥ । marudullāsitasaurabhakamalākarahāsakṛdravirjayati ।।} atrātivitatatvādayo anupādāne api pratipādyamānamarthaṃ na bādhanta ityapuṣṭāḥ na tvasaṃgatāḥ punaruktā vā ।। sarasvatyuddāmā vahati bahumārgā parimalam ।
mahākāvyavyomni sphuritamadhurā yāntu rucayaḥ ।।} atra yāsāṃ kavirucīnāṃ madhye sukumāravicitramadhyamātmakatrimārgā bhāratī camatkāraṃ vahati tāḥ gambhīrakāvyaparicitāḥ kathamitarakāvyavat prasannā bhavantu । yāsāmādityaprabhāṇāṃ madhye tripathagā vahati tā meghaparicitāḥ kathaṃ prasannā bhavantīti saṃkṣepārthaḥ ।। prakṛtimadhurāḥ santyevānye mano madayanti ye । nayanaviṣayaṃ janmanyekaḥ sa eva mahotsavaḥ ।।}
atrendukalādayo yaṃ prati paspaśaprāyāḥ sa eva candrikātvam utkarṣārthamāropayatīti vyāhatatvam ।। {kṛtamanumatamityādi ।।} manujapaśubhirnirmaryādairbhavadbhirudāyudhaiḥ । mayamaha[ma]sṛṅmedomāṃsaiḥ karomi diśāṃ balim ।।]
atrārjunārjuneti bhavadbhiriti cokte sabhīmakirīṭināmiti kirīṭipadārthaḥ punaruktaḥ । yathā vā senānāthe sthitesminmama pitari gurau sarvadhanvīśvarāṇām । tāte cāpaddhitīye vahati raṇadhuraṃ ko bhayasyāvakāśaḥ ।।} atra caturthapādavākyārthaḥ punaruktaḥ ।।
{bhūpālaratna nirdainyapradānaprathitotsava । viśrāṇaya turaṅgaṃ me mātaṅgaṃ vā madālasam ।।} atra mātaṅgasya prāṅnirdeśo yuktaḥ । {svapiti yāvadayaṃ nikaṭe janaḥ svapimi tāvadahaṃ kimapaiti te ।
tadapi sāṃpratamāhara kūrparaṃ tvaritamūrumudañcaya kuñcitam ।।} eṣo avidagdhaḥ ।। {mātsaryamutsāryetyādi ।।} [mātsaryamutsārya vicārya kāryamāryāḥ samaryādamudāharantu ।
sevyā nitambāḥ kimu bhūdharāṇām uta smarasmeravilāsinīnām ।।] atra prakaraṇādyabhāve saṃdehaḥ śāntaśṛṅgāryanyatarābhidhāne tu niścayaḥ ।। prabhāvādyasyābhūnna khalu tava kaścinna viṣayaḥ । dvimokṣye śastra tvāmahamapi yataḥ svasti bhavate ।।}
atra [dvitīya]śastramocane heturnopāttaḥ ।। yadetasmin hemnaḥ kaṭakamiti dhatse khalu dhiyam । tava prītyā cakraṃ karakamalamūle vinihitam ।।} atra kāmasya cakraṃ loke aprasiddham । yathā vā
saraṇimaparo mārgastvadbhavadbhirihekṣyatām । caraṇalinanyāsodañcannavāṅkurakañcukaḥ ।।} atra pādāghātenāśokasya puṣpodgamaḥ kaviṣu prasiddho na punaraṅkurodgamaḥ । mahasi sudṛśi svairaṃ yāntyāṃ gatostamabhūdcidhuḥ ।
priyagṛhamagānmuktāśaṅkā kva nāsi śubhapradaḥ ।।} atrāmūrtāpi kīrtiḥ jyotsnāvatprakāśarūpā kathiteti lokaviruddhamapi kaviprasiddherna duṣṭam ।।) {sadā snātvā niśīthinyāṃ sakalaṃ vāsaraṃ budhaḥ । nānāvidhāni śāstrāṇi vyācaṣṭe ca śṛṇoti ca ।।}
grahoparāgādikaṃ vinā rātrau snānaṃ dharmaśāstraṇa viruddham । {ananyasadṛśaṃ yasya balaṃ bāhvoḥ samīkṣyate । ṣāḍaguṇyānusṛtistasya satyaṃ sā niṣprayojanā ।।} etat arthaśāstreṇa ।
{vidhāya dūre keyūramanaṅgāṅgaṇamaṅganā । babhāra kāntena kṛtāṃ karajollekhamālikām ।।} atra keyūrapade nakhaksaṭaṃ na vihitamiti । duḥsādhasiddhisavidhaṃ vidadhadvidūre ।
khyātiṃ samādhidhanamaulimarṇirvimuktaḥ ।।} atra vivekakhyātistataḥ saṃprajñātasamādhiḥ paścādasaṃprajñātastato muktirna tu vivekakhyātau ।। evaṃ vidyāntarairapi viruddhamudāhāryam ।। dattaṃ padaṃ śirasi vidviṣatāṃ tataḥ kim ।
kalpaṃ sthitaṃ tanubhṛtāṃ tanubhistataḥ kim ।।} atra tataḥ kimiti na navīkṛtam । tattu yathā {yadi dahatyanalotra kimadbhutaṃ yadi ca gauravamadriṣu kiṃ tataḥ । lavaṇamambu sadaiva mahodadheḥ prakṛtireva satāmaviṣāditā ।।}
utkarṣapratiyogikalpanamapi nyakkārakoṭiḥ parā । tasyābhāsamaṇīkṛtāśmasumaṇeraśmatvamevocitam ।।} atra {chāyāmātramaṇīkṛtāśmasu maṇestasyāśmataivocitā} iti saniyamatvaṃ vācyam ।। bāhuḥ kākutsthavīryasmṛtikaraṇapaṭurdakṣiṇaste samudraḥ ।
svacchentarmānasesmin kathamavanipate tembupānābhilāṣaḥ ।।} atra {śoṇa eva} iti niyamo na vācyaḥ ।। mantraṃ tantramatha prayujya harata śvetotpalānāṃ śriyam । yena draṣṭumahaṃ kṣame daśa diśastadvaktramudrāṅkitāḥ ।।}
atra ajyautsnīm'; iti śyāmāviśeṣo vācyaḥ ।। ratnānyamūni makarālaya māvamaṃsthāḥ । yā[ñc]āprasāritakaraḥ puruṣottame api ।।} atra {ekena kiṃ na vihito bhavataḥ sa nāma} iti sāmānyaṃ vācyam ।
druhyan dāśarathirviruddhacarito yuktastayā kanyayā । strīratnaṃ ca jagatpatirdaśamukho devaḥ kathaṃ mṛṣyate ।।} atra strīratnam aupeksitum'; ityākāṅkṣati । nahi parasyetyanena saṃbandho yogyaḥ ।। bhaktirbhūtapatau pinākini padaṃ laṅketi divyā purī ।
syāccedeṣa na rāvaṇaḥ kva nu punaḥ sarvatra sarve guṇāḥ ।।} atra asyāccedeṣa na rāvaṇaḥ'; ityatra eva samāpyam ।। {śrutena buddhirvyasanena mūrkhatā madena nārī salilena nimnagā । niśā śaśāṅkena dhṛtiḥsamādhinā nayena cālaṅkriyate narendratā ।।}
atra śrutādibhirutkṛṣṭaiḥ sahacaritairvyasanamūrkhatayornikṛṣṭayorbhinnatvam । {lagnaṃ rāgāvṛtāṅgyā- ।।} mātaṅgānāmapīhopari parapuruṣairyā ca dṛṣṭā patantī । bhṛtyebhyaḥ śrīniyogādgaditumiva gatetyambudhiṃ yasya kīrtiḥ ।।]
ityatra viditaṃ testvityanena śrīstasmādapasaratīti viruddhaṃ prakāśyate ।। makeśavamapāṇḍavaṃ bhuvanamadya niḥsomakam । mapaitu ripukānanātigururadya bhāro bhuvaḥ ।।} atra {śayitaḥ prayatnena bodhyase} iti vidheyam । yathā vā
te grastāḥ punarabhratoyakaṇikātīvravratairbarhibhiḥ । dambhasya sphuritaṃ vidannapi jano jālmo guṇānīhate ।।} atra vātāhārāditrayaṃ vyutkrameṇa vācyam ।। smarakrīḍāvrīḍāśamana virahiprāṇadamana ।
sakhedo ahaṃ mohaṃ ślathaya kathaya kvenduvadanā ।।} atra avihahiprāṇadamana'; iti nānuvādyam ।। {lagnaṃ rāgāvṛtāṅgyetyādi ।।} mātaṅgānāmapīhopari parapuruṣairyā ca dṛṣṭā patantī ।
bhṛtyebhyaḥ śrīniyogādgaditumiva gatetyambudhiṃ yasya kīrtiḥ ।।] atra {viditaṃ testu} ityupasaṃhṛto api tenetyādinā punarupāttaḥ ।। {hantumeva pravṛttasya stabdhasya vivaraiṣiṇaḥ । yathāsya jāyate pāto na tathā punarunnatiḥ ।।}
atra puṃvyañjanasyāpi pratītiḥ ।। yatraiko doṣaḥ pradarśitastatra doṣāntarāṇyapi santi tathāpi teṣāṃ tatrāprakṛtatvātprakāśanaṃ na kṛtam ।। karṇāvataṃsādipade karṇādidhvaninirmitiḥ । avataṃsādīni karṇādyābharaṇānyevocyante । tatra karṇādiśabdāḥ karṇādisthitipratipattaye । yathā
{asyāḥ karṇāvataṃsena jitaṃ sarvaṃ vibhūṣaṇam । tathaiva śobhatetyarthamasyāḥ śravaṇakuṇḍalam ।।} {apūrvamadhurāmodapramoditadiśastataḥ । āyayurbhṛṅgamukharāḥ śiraḥśekharaśālinaḥ ।।}
atra karṇaśravaṇaśiraḥśabdāḥ saṃnidhānapratītyarthāḥ ।। {vidīrṇābhimukhārātikarāle saṃgarāntare । dhanurjyākiṇacihnena doṣṇā visphuritaṃ tava ।।} atra dhanuḥśabda ārūṭhatvāvagataye ।।
{jyābandhaniṣpandabhujena yasya viniśvamadvaktraparaṃpareṇa । kārāgṛhe nirjitavāsavane laṅkeśvareṇoṣitamā prasādāt ।।} ityatra kevalo jyāśabdaḥ । {prāṇeśvarapariṣvaṅgavibhramapratipattibhiḥ ।
muktāhāreṇa lasatā hasatīva stanadvayam ।।} atra muktānāmanyaratnāmiśritatvabodhanāya muktāśabdaḥ । {saundaryasaṃpat tāruṇyaṃ yasyāste te ca vibhramāḥ । ṣaṭpadān puṣpamāleva kān nākarṣati sā sakhe ।।}
atrotkṛṣṭapuṣpaviṣaye puṣpaśabdaḥ । nirupapado hi mālāśabdaḥ puṣpasrajamevābhidhatte ।। sthiteṣvetatsamarthanam ।। {na khalu karṇāvataṃsādivajjaghanakāñcītyādi kriyate । jagāda madhurāṃ vācaṃ viśadākṣaraśālinīm ।।}
ityādau kriyāviśeṣaṇatve api vivakṣitārthapratītisiddhau {gatārthasyāpi viśeṣyasya viśeṣaṇadānārthaṃ kvacitprayogaḥ kāryaḥ} iti na yuktam । yuktatve vā {caraṇatraparitrāṇarahitābhyāmapi drutam । pādābhyāṃ dūramadhvānaṃ vrajanneṣa na khidyate ।।} ityudāhāryam ।।
{candraṃ gatā padmaguṇānna bhuṅkte padmāśritā cāndramasīmabhikhyām । umāmukhaṃ tu pratipadya lolā dvisaṃśrayāṃ prītimavāpa lakṣmīḥ ।।} atra rātrau padmasya saṃkocaḥ divā candramasaśca niṣprabhatvaṃ lokaprasiddhamiti ana bhuṅkte a; iti hetuṃ nāpekṣate ।। anukaraṇe tu sarveṣām ।
sarveṣāṃ śrutikaṭuprabhṛtīnāṃ doṣāṇām । yathā {mṛgacakṣuṣamadrākṣamityādi kathayatyayam । paśyaiṣa ca gavityāha sūtrāmāṇaṃ yajeta ca ।।} vaktrādyaucityavaśāddoṣo api guṇaḥ kvacitkvacinnobhau ।।
vakṛpratipādyavyaṅgavācyaprakaraṇādīnāṃ mahimnā doṣo api kvacidaguṇaḥ kvacinna doṣo na guṇaḥ । tatra vyākaraṇādau vaktari pratipādye ca raudrādau ca rase vyaṅge kaṣṭatvaṃ guṇaḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam {dīrghīṅvevīṅsamaḥ kaścidguṇavṛddhyorabhājanam । kvippratyayanibhaḥ kaścidyatra saṃnihite na te ।।} {yadā tvāmahamadrākṣaṃ padavidyāviśāradam ।
upādhyāyaṃ tadāsmārṣaṃ samasprākṣaṃ ca saṃmadam ।।} prāyapreṅkhitabhūribhūṣaṇaravairāghoṣayantyambaram । dvyālolastanabhārabhairavavapurdarpoddhataṃ dhāvati ।।} sāraṅgā mahiṣā madaṃ vrajatha kiṃ śūnyeṣu śarā na ke ।
sindhudhvānini huṅkṛte sphurati yat tadgarjitaṃ garjitam ।।} atra siṃhe vācye paruṣāḥ śabdāḥ ।। no dṛṣṭeti mudhaiva cālayasi kiṃ vātāvadhūtaṃ śiraḥ । statpādāhatimantareṇa bhavataḥ puṣpodgamo ayaṃ kutaḥ ।।}
atra śirodhūnanena kupitasya vacasi ।। kvacinnīrase na guṇo na doṣaḥ । yathā dīrghāghrātānaghaughaiḥ punarapi ghaṭayatyeka ullāghayan yaḥ । dattārghāḥ siddhasaṃghairvidadhatu ghṛṇayaḥ śīghramaṃhovighātam ।।}
aprayuktanihatārthau śleṣādāvaduṣṭau । yathā yaścoddhṛttabhujaṅgahāravalayogaṅgāṃ ca yodhārayat । pāyātsa svayamandhakakṣayakarastvāṃ sarvadomādhavaḥ ।।} atra mādhavapakṣe śaśimadandhakakṣayaśabdāprayuktanihatārthau ।।
aślīlaṃ kvacidguṇaḥ । yathā suratārambhagoṣṭhyām {dvyartheḥ {karihastena saṃbādhe praviśyāntarviloḍite । upasarpan dhvajaḥ puṃsaḥ sādhanāntarvirājate ।।} {uttānocchanamaṇḍūkapāṭitodarasaṃnibhe ।
kledini strīvraṇe saktirakṛmeḥ kasya jāyate ।।} nandantu pāṇḍutanayā saha mādhavena । svasthā bhavantu kururājasutāḥ sabhṛtyāḥ ।।} atra bhāvyamaṅgakasūcakam ।।
saṃdigdhamapi vācyamahimnā kvacinniyatārthapratītikṛttvena vyājastutiparyavasāyitve guṇaḥ । yathā {pṛthukārtasvarapātraṃ bhūṣitaniḥśeṣaparijanaṃ deva । vilasatkareṇugahanaṃ saṃprati samamāvayoḥ sadanam ।।} pratipādyapratipādakayorjñatve satyapratītaṃ guṇaḥ । yathā
jñānodrekādvighaṭitatamogranthayaḥ sattvaniṣṭhāḥ । taṃ mohāndhaḥ kathamayamamuṃ vetti devaṃ purāṇaṃ ।।} svayaṃ vā parāmarśe । yathā hṛdi vinihitarūpaḥ siddhidastaddhitāṃ yaḥ ।
sa jayati pariṇaddhaḥ śaktibhiḥ śaktināthaḥ ।।} adhamaprakṛtyuktiṣu grāmyo guṇaḥ । yathā je sindhuvāraviḍavā maha vallahā de । de kiṃ ca muddhaviaillapasūṇapuñjā ।।}
ye sindhuvāraviṭapā mama vallabhāste । stekiṃ ca mugdhavicakilaprasūnapuñjāḥ ।।] atra kalamabhaktamahiṣīdadhiśabdā grāmyā api vidūṣakoktau ।। nyūnapadaṃ kvacidguṇaḥ । yathā
sāndrasneharasātirekavigalacchrīmannitambāmbarā । suptā kiṃ nu mṛtā nu kiṃ manasi me līnā vilīnā nu kim ।।} kvacinna guṇo na doṣaḥ । yathā svargāyotpatitā bhavenmayi punarbhāvādramasyā manaḥ ।
sā cātyantamagocaraṃ nayanayoryāteti ko ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।} atra pihitā ityatonantaraṃ anaitadyataḥ'; ityetairnyūnaiḥ padairviśeṣabuddherakaraṇānna guṇaḥ । uttarā pratipattiḥ pūrvāṃ pratipattiṃ bādhate iti na doṣaḥ ।। adhikapadaṃ kvacidguṇaḥ । yathā kāryonmukhaḥ khalajanaḥ krṭakaṃ bravīti ।
kartuṃ vṛthā praṇayamasya na pārayanti ।।} atra {vidanti} iti dvitīyamanyayogavyavacchedaparam । yathā vā {vada vada jitaḥ sa śatrurna hato jalpaṃśca tava tavāsmīti । citraṃ citramarodīddhā heti paraṃ mṛte putre ।।}
ityevamādau harṣabhayādiyukte vaktari ।। kathitapadaṃ kvacidguṇaḥ lāṭānuprāse arthāntarasaṃkramitavācye vihitasyānuvādyatve ca । krameṇodāharaṇam {sitakarakararuciravibhā vibhākarākāra dharaṇidhara kīrtiḥ । pauruṣakamalā kamalā sāpi tavaivāsti nānyasya ।।}
{tālā jāanti guṇā jālā de sahiaeṃhi gheppanti । raikiraṇāṇuggahiāiṃ honti kamalāiṃ kamalāiṃ ।।} [tadā jāyante guṇāḥ yadā te sahṛdayairgṛhyante । ravikiraṇānugṛhītāni bhavanti kamalāni kamalāni ।।]
{jitendriyatvaṃ vinayasya kāraṇaṃ guṇaprakarṣo vinayādavāpyate । guṇaprakarṣeṇa janonurajyate janānurāgaprabhavā hi saṃpadaḥ ।।} {patatprakarṣamapi kvacidguṇaḥ । yathā udāhṛte prāgaprāpta-ityādau ।।} samāptapunarāttaṃ kvacinna guṇo na doṣaḥ । yatra na viśeṣaṇamātradānārthaḥ punargrahaṇam api tu vākyāntarameva kriyate । yathā
{atraiva prāgaprāpta ityādau ।।} apadasthasamāsaṃ kvacid guṇaḥ । yathā {udāhṛte raktāśokaityādau ।।} garbhitaṃ tathaiva । yathā
{humi avahatthiareho ṇiraṅkuso aha vivearahio vi । siviṇe vi tumammi puṇo pattihi bhattiṃ ṇa pasumarāmi ।।} [bhavāmyapahastitarekho niraṅguśo atha vivekarahito api । svapne api tvayi punaḥ pratīhi bhaktiṃ na prasmarāmi ।।]
atra pratīhīti madhye dṛḍhapratyayotpādanāya । evamanyadapi lakṣyāllakṣyam ।। vyabhicārirasasthāyibhāvānāṃ śabdavācyatā । kaṣṭakalpanayā vyaktiranubhāvavibhāvayoḥ ।। pratikūlavibhāvādigraho dīptiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
akāṇḍe prathanacchedāvaṅgasyāpyativistṛtiḥ ।। aṅgino ananusaṃdhānaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ viparyayaḥ । anaṅgasyābhidhānaṃ ca rase doṣāḥ syurīdṛśāḥ ।। satrāsā bhujage savismayarasā candre amṛtasyandini ।
pārvatyā navasaṃgamapraṇayinī dṛṣṭiḥ śivāyāstu vaḥ ।।} atra vrīḍādīnām । sotkampā bhujage nimeṣarahitā candremṛtasyandini । ityādi tu yuktam ।।
rasasya svaśabdena śṛṅgārādiśabdena vā vācyatvam । krameṇodāharaṇam {tāmanaṅgajayamaṅgalaśriyaṃ kiñciduccabhujamūlalokitām । netrayoḥ kṛtavato asya gocare ko apyajāyata raso nirantaraḥ ।।} vyaktānurāgasubhagāmabhirāmamūrtim ।
śṛṅgārasīmani taraṅgitamātanoti ।।} {saṃprahāre praharaṇaiḥ prahārāṇāṃ parasparam । ṭhaṇatkāraiḥ śrutigatairutsāhastasya ko apyabhūt ।।} atrotsāhasya ।।
diṅmaṇḍale śiśirarociṣi tasya yūnaḥ । vyaktastanonnatirabhūnnayanāvanau sā ।।} atroddīpanālambanarūpāḥ śṛṅgārayogyā vibhāvā anubhāvaparyavasāyinaḥ sthitā iti kaṣṭakalpanā ।। {pariharati ratiṃ matiṃ lunīte skhalati bhṛśaṃ parivartate ca bhūyaḥ ।
iti bata viṣamā daśāsya dehaṃ paribhavati prasabhaṃ kimatra kurmaḥ ।।} atra ratiparihārādīnāmanubhāvānāṃ karuṇādāvapi saṃbhavātkāminīrūpo vibhāvo yatnataḥ pratipādyaḥ ।। priye śuṣyantyaṅgānyamṛtamiva te siñcatu vacaḥ । na mugdhe pratyetuṃ prabhavati gataḥ kālahariṇaḥ ।।}
atra śṛṅgāre pratikūlasya śāntasyānityatāprakāśanarūpo vibhāvastatprakāśito nirvedaśca vyabhicārī upāttaḥ ।। {ṇihuaramaṇammi loaṇapahammi paḍie guruaṇamajjhammi । saalaparihārahiaā vaṇagamaṇaṃ evva mahai vahū ।।} [nibhṛtaramaṇe locanapathe patite gurujanamadhye ।
sakalaparihārahṛdayā vanamanamevecchati vadhūḥ ।।] atra sakalaparihāravanagamane śāntānubhāvau । indhanādyānayanavyājenopabhogārthaṃ vanagamanaṃ cet na doṣaḥ ।। dīptiḥ punaḥ punaryathā kumārasaṃbhave rativilāpe ।। akāṇḍe prathanaṃ yathā veṇīsaṃhāre dvitīyeṅkenekavīrakṣaye pravṛtte bhānumatyā saha duryodhanasya śṛṅgāravarṇanam ।
akāṇḍe chedo yathā vīracarite dvitīyeṅke rāghavabhārgavayordhārādhirūḍhe vīrarase {kaṅkaṇamocanāya gacchāmi} iti rāghavasyoktau ।। aṅgasyāpradhānasyātivistareṇa varṇanam । yathā hayagrīvavadhe hayagrīvasya ।। aṅgino ananusaṃdhānam । yathā ratnāvalyāṃ caturtheṅke bābhravyāgamane sāgarikāyā vismṛtiḥ ।। dhīrodāttadhīroddhatadhīralalitadhīrapraśāntāḥ uttamādhamamadhyamāśca । tatra ratihāsaśokādbhutāni adivyottamaprakṛtivat divyeṣvapi । kiṃ tu ratiḥ saṃbhogaśṛṅgārarūpā uttamadevatāviṣayā na varṇanīyā । tadvarṇanaṃ hi pitroḥ saṃbhogavarṇanamivātyantamanucitam ।
{krodhaṃ prabho saṃhara saṃhareti yāvad giraḥ khe marutāṃ caranti । tāvatsa vahnirbhavanetrajanmā bhasmāvaśeṣaṃ madanaṃ cakāra ।।} ityuktavat bhrukuṭyādivikāravarjitaḥ krodhaḥ sadyaḥphaladaḥ svargapātālagagasamudrollaṅghanādyutsāhaśca divyeṣyeva । adhikaṃ tu nibadhyamānamasatyapratibhāsena anāyakavadvartitavyaṃ na pratināyakavat'; ityupadeśe na paryavasyet । divyādivyeṣu ubhayathāpi । evamuktasyaucityasya divyādīnāmiva dhīrodāttādīnāmapyanyathāvarṇanaṃ viparyayaḥ । tatrabhavan bhagavannityuttamena na adhamena muniprabhṛtau na rājādau bhaṭṭāraka-iti nottamena rājādau prakṛtiviparyayāpattervācyam । evaṃ deśakālavayojātyādīnāṃ veṣavyavahārādikamucitamevopanibanddhavyam ।। anaṅgasya rasānupakārakasya varṇanam । yathā karpūramañjaryā nāyikayā svātmanā ca kṛtaṃ vasantavarṇanamanādṛtya bandivarṇitasya rājñā praśaṃsanam ।।
{īdṛśāḥ} iti । nāyikāpādaprahārādinā nāyakakopādivarṇanam । uktaṃ hi dhvanikṛtā {anaucityādṛtte nānyad rasabhaṅgasya kāraṇam । aucityopanibandhastu rasasyopaniṣatparā ।। idānīṃ kvacidadoṣā apyete ityucyante ।
na doṣaḥ svapadenoktāvapi saṃcāriṇaḥ kvacid । taistairbandhuvadhūjanasya vacanairnītābhimukhyaṃ punaḥ । saṃrohatpulakā hareṇa hasatā śliṣṭā śivāyāstu vaḥ ।।} atrautsukyaśabda iva tadanubhāvo na tathā pratītikṛt । ata eva adūrādutsukam'; ityādau vrīḍāpremādyanubhāvānāṃ । vivalitatvādīnāmivotsukatvānubhāvasya sahasā prasaraṇādirūpasya tathā pratipattikāritvābhāvādutsukamiti kṛtam ।।
saṃcāryāderviruddhasya bādhyasyoktirguṇāvahā ।। bādhyatvenoktirna paramadoṣaḥ yāvat prakṛtarasaparipoṣakṛt । yathā {'kvākāryaṃ śaśalakṣmaṇaḥ kva ca kulam'; ityādau ।।} doṣāṇāṃ praśamāya na śrutamaho kope api kāntaṃ mukham ।
cetaḥ svāsthyamupaihi kaḥ khalu yuvā dhanyo adharaṃ dhāsyati ।।] atra vitarkādiṣu udgateṣvapi cintāyāmeva viśrāntiriti prakṛtarasaparipoṣaḥ ।। {pāṇḍu kṣāmaṃ vadanaṃ hṛdayaṃ sarasaṃ tavālasaṃ ca vapuḥ । āvedayati nitāntaṃ kṣetriyarogaṃ sakhi hṛdantaḥ ।।}
ityādau sādhāraṇatvaṃ pāṇḍutādīnāmiti na viruddham ।। {satyaṃ manoramā rāmāḥ satyaṃ ramyā vibhūtayaḥ । kiṃ tu mattāṅganāpāṅgabhaṅgalolaṃ hi jīvitam ।।} ityatrādyamardhaṃ bādhyatvenaivokyam । jīvitādapi adhikamapāṅgabhaṅgasyāsthiratvamiti prasiddhabhaṅguropamānatayopāttaṃ śāntameva puṣṇāti na punaḥ śṛṅgārasyātra pratītistadaṅgāpratipatterḥ । na tu vineyonmukhīkaraṇamatra parihāraḥ śāntaśṛṅgārayornairantaryasyābhāvāt । nāpi kāvyaśobhākaraṇaṃ rasāntarādanuprāsamātrādvā tathābhāvāt ।।
āśrayaikye viruddho yaḥ sa kāryo bhinnasaṃśrayaḥ । rasāntareṇāntarito nairantaryeṇa yo rasaḥ ।। vīrabhayānakayorekāśrayatvena virodha iti pratiprakṣagatatvena bhayānako niveśayitavyaḥ । śāntaśṛṅgārayostu nairantaryeṇa virodha iti rasāntaramantare kāryam yathā nāgānande śāntasya jīmūtavāhanasya aaho gītam aho vāditram'; ityadbhūtamantarniveśya malayavatīṃ prati śṛṅgāro nibaddhaḥ । na paraṃ prabandhe yāvadekasminnapi vākye rasāntaravyavadhinā virodho nivartate । yathā
mālārajovāsitabāhumadhyā । surāṅganāśliṣṭabhujāntarālāḥ ।।} pakṣaiḥ khagānāmupavījyamānān । sugandhibhiḥ kalpalatādukūlaiḥ ।। ।।}
kutūhalāviṣṭitayā tadānīm । vīrāḥ svadehān patitānapaśyan ।।} atra bībhatsaśṛṅgārayorantarvīraraso niveśitaḥ ।। smaryamāṇo viruddho api sāmyenātha vivakṣitaḥ ।
aṅginyaṅgatvamāptau yau tau na duṣṭau parasparam ।। {ayaṃ sa raśanotkarṣī pīnastanavimardanaḥ । nābhyūrujaghanasparśī nīvīvisraṃsanaḥ karaḥ ।।} etad bhūriśravasaḥ samarabhuvi patitaṃ hastamālokya tadvadhūrabhidadhau । atra pūrvāvasthāsmaraṇaṃ śṛṅgārāṅgamapi karuṇaṃ paripoṣayati ।।
prodbhinnasāndrapulake bhavataḥ śarīre । jātaspṛhairmunibhirapyavalokitāni ।।} atra kāmukasya dantakṣatādīni yathā camatkārakārīṇi tathā jinasya । yathā vā paraḥ śṛṅgārī tadalokanātsaspṛhastadvat etaddṛśo munaya iti sāmyavivakṣā ।। pādaiḥ pātitayāvakairiva galadbāṣpāmbudhautānanā ।
dāvāgniṃ parito bhramanti punarapyudyadvivāhā iva ।।} atra cāṭuke rājaviṣayā ratiḥ pratīyate । tatra karuṇa iva śṛṅgāro apyaṅgamiti tayorna virodhaḥ । yathā {ehi gaccha patottiṣṭha vada maunaṃ samācara । evamāśāgrahagrastaiḥ krīḍanti dhanino arthibhiḥ ।।}
ityatra ehīti krīḍanti gaccheti krīḍantīti krīḍanāpekṣayoḥ āgamanagamanayorna virodhaḥ । gṛhṇan keśeṣvapāstaścaraṇanipatito nekṣitaḥ saṃbhrameṇa । kāmīvārdrāparādhaḥ sa dahatu duritaṃ śābhavo vaḥ śarāgniḥ ।।} ityatra tripuraripuprabhāvātiśayasya karuṇo aṅgam । tathāpi na karuṇe viśrāntiriti tasyāṅgataiva । athavā prāk yathā kāmuka ācarati sma tathā śarāgniriti śṛṅgārapoṣitena karuṇeṇa mukhya evārtha upodbalyate ।
{guṇaḥ kṛtātmasaṃskāraḥ pradhānaṃ pratimadyate । pradhānasyopakāre hi tathā bhūyasi vartate ।। prākpratipāditasya rasasya rasāntareṇa na virodhaḥ nāpyaṅgāṅgibhāvo bhavati iti rasaśabdenātra sthāyibhāva upalakṣyate ।। iti kāvyaprakāśe doṣadarśano nāma saptama ullāsaḥ ।।
ye rasasyāṅgino dharmāḥ śauryādaya ivātmanaḥ । utkarṣahetavaste syuracalasthitayo guṇāḥ ।। ātmana eva hi yathā śauryādayo nākārasya tathā rasasyaiva mādhuryādayo guṇā na varṇānām ।। vyavaharanti । ata eva mādhuryādayo rasadharmāḥ samucitairvarṇairvyajyante na tu
varṇamātrāśrayāḥ । yathaiṣāṃ vyañjakatvam tathodāhariṣyate ।। upakurvanti taṃ santaṃ ye aṅgadvāreṇa jātucit । hārādivadalaṅkārāste anuprāsopamādayaḥ ।। ye vācakavācyalakṣaṇāṅgātiśayamukhena mukhyaṃ rasaṃ saṃbhavinam upakurvanti te kaṇṭhādyaṅgānāmutkarṣādhānadvāreṇa śarīriṇo api upakārakā hārādaya ivālaṅkārāḥ । yatra tu nāsti rasastatroktivaicitryamātraparyavasāyinaḥ । kvacittu santamapi nopakurvanti ।
{apasāraya ghanasāraṃ kuru hāraṃ dūra eva kiṃ kamalaiḥ । alamalamāli mṛṇālairiti vadati divāniśaṃ bālā ।।} pramāthī nirdhūmaṃ jvalati vidhutaḥ pāvaka iva । na māṃ trātuṃ tātaḥ prabhavati na cāmbā na bhavatī ।।}
ityādau vācyamukhenālaṅkārau rasamupakurutaḥ ।। sejjāsu loṭṭadi visappadi dimuṃhesuṃ । jhāṇeṇa ṭuṭṭadi ciraṃ taruṇī taraṭṭī ।।} śayyāsu luṭhati visarpati diṅmukheṣu ।
dhyānena truṭyati ciraṃ taruṇī pragalbhā ।।] ityādau vācakameva । krandatsu bhramareṣu vīkṣya dayitāsannaṃ puraḥ sārasam । kaṇṭhe kevalamargaleva nihitā jīvasya nirgacchataḥ ।।}
ityādau vācyameva na tu rasam । atra bisalatā na jīvaṃ roddhuṃ kṣameti prakṛtānanuguṇopamā ।। eṣa eva ca guṇālaṅkārapravibhāgaḥ । evaṃ ca "samavāyavṛttyā śauryādayaḥ saṃyogavṛttyā tu hārādaya ityastu guṇālaṅkārāṇāṃ bhedaḥ । ojaḥprabhṛtīnāmanuprāsopamādīnāṃ cobhayeṣāmapi samavāyavṛttyā sthitiriti gaḍḍalikāpravāheṇaivaiṣāṃ bhedaḥ" ityabhidhānamasat ।। yadapyuktam {kāvyaśobhāyāḥ kartāro dharmā guṇās tadatiśayahetavastvalaṅkārāḥ} iti tadapi na yuktam । yataḥ kiṃ samastairguṇaiḥ kāvyavyavahāraḥ uta katipayaiḥ । yadi samastaiḥ tatkathamasamastaguṇā gauḍī pāñcālī ca rītiḥ kāvyasyātmā ।
{adrāvatra prajvalatyagniruccaiḥ prājyaḥ prodyannullasatyeṣa dhūmaḥ ।।} ityādāvojaḥ prabhṛtiṣu guṇeṣu satsu kāvyavyavahāraprāptiḥ । {svargaprāptiranenaiva dehena varavarṇinī । asyā radacchadaraso nyakkarotitarāṃ sudhām ।।}
ityādau viśeṣoktivyatirekau guṇanirapekṣau kāvyavyavahārasya pravartakau ।। mādhuryaujaḥprasādākhyāstrayaste na punardaśa । āhlādakatvaṃ mādhuryaṃ śṛṅgāre drutikāraṇam ।। śṛṅgāre arthāt saṃbhoge । drutirgalitatvamiva । śravyatvaṃ punarojaḥprasādayorapi ।।
karuṇe vipralambhe tacchānte cātiśayānvitam । [atiśayānvitamiti] atyantadrutihetutvāt ।। dīptyātmavistṛterheturojo vīrarasasthiti ।। cittasya vistārarūpadīptatvajanakamojaḥ ।।
bībhatsaraudrarasayostasyādhikyaṃ krameṇa ca । vīrādvībhatse tato sātiśayamojaḥ ।। śuṣkendhanāgnivat svacchajalavatsahasaiva yaḥ ।। vyāpnotyanyat prasādo asau sarvatra vihitasthitiḥ ।
anyaditi । sarvatreti । sarveṣu raseṣu sarvāsu racanāsu ca ।। guṇavṛttyā punasteṣāṃ vṛttiḥ śabdārthayormatā ।। guṇavṛttyā upacāreṇa । ākāre śaurysyeva ।। kecidantarbhavantyeṣu doṣatyāgātpare śritāḥ ।
anye bhajanti doṣatvaṃ kutracinna tato daśa ।। teṣāmojastantarbhāvaḥ । pṛthakpadatvarūpaṃ mādhuryaṃ bhaṅgyā sākṣādupāttam । prasādenārthavyaktirgṛhītā । mārgābhedarūpā samatā kvaciddoṣaḥ । tathāhi {mātaṅgāḥ kimu valgataiḥ} ityādau siṃhābhidhāne masṛṇamārgatvāyo guṇaḥ । kaṣṭatvagrāmyatvayorduṣṭābhidhānāttannirākaraṇenāpāruṣyarūpaṃ saukumāryam aujjvalyarūpā kāntiśca svīkṛtā ।। evaṃ na daśa śabdaguṇāḥ ।। {padārthe vākyaracanaṃ vākyārthe ca padābhidhā ।
prauḍhirvyāsasamāsau ca sābhiprāyatvamasya ca ।।} iti yā prauḍhiḥ oja ityuktaṃ tad vaicitryamātram na guṇaḥ । tadabhāve api kāvyavyavahārapravṛtteḥ । apuṣṭārthatvādhikapadatvānavīkṛtatvāmaṅgalarūpāślīlagrāmyāṇāṃ nirākaraṇena ca sābhiprāyatvarūpamojaḥ arthavaimalyātmā prasādaḥ uktivaicitryarūpaṃ mādhuryam apāruṣyarūpaṃ saukumāryam agrāmyatvarūpā udāratā ca svīkṛtāni । abhidhāsyamānasvabhāvoktyalaṅkāreṇa rasadhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyābhyāṃ ca vastusvabhāvasphuṭatvarūpā arthavyaktiḥ, dīptarasatvarūpā kāntiśca svīkṛtā । kramakauṭilyānulbaṇatvopapattiyogarūpaghaṭanātmā śleṣo api vicitratvamātram । avaiṣamyasvarūpā samatā doṣābhāvamātraṃ na punarguṇaḥ । kaḥ khalvanunmattonyasya prastāvenyadabhidadhyāt । arthasyāyoner'nyacchāyāyonervā yadi na bhavati darśanaṃ tatkathaṃ kāvyam ityarthadṛṣṭirūpaḥ samādhirapi na guṇaḥ ।।
na vācyāḥ na vaktavyāḥ ।। proktāḥ śabdaguṇāśca ye । varṇāḥ samāso racanā teṣāṃ vyañjakatāmitāḥ ।। murdhni vargāntyagāḥ sparśā aṭavargā raṇau laghū ।
āvṛttirmadhyavṛttirvā mādhurye ghaṭanā tathā ।। ṭaṭhaḍaḍhavarjitāḥ kādayo māntāḥ śirasi nijavargāntyayuktāḥ tathā rephaṇakārau hrasvāntaritāviti varṇāḥ samāsābhāvo madhyamaḥ samāso veti samāsaḥ tathā mādhuryavatī padāntarayogena racanā mādhuryasya vyañjikā ।। udāharaṇam bhaṅgībhraṅgīkṛtamānatāṅgyāḥ । svāntāni śāntāparacintanāni ।।}
yoga ādyatṛtīyāmyāmantyayo reṇa tulyayoḥ । ṭādiḥ śaṣau vṛttidairghyaṃ gumpha uddhṛta ojasi ।। vargaprathamatṛtīyābhyāmantyayoḥ dvitīyacaturthayoḥ repheṇa adha upari ubhayatra vā yasya kasyacit tulyayoḥ tena tasyaiva saṃbandhaḥ ṭavargo arthāt ṇakāravarjaḥ śakāraṣakārau dīrghasamāsaḥ vikaṭā saṃghaṭanā ojasaḥ । {mūrdhnāmuddhṛttakrṭtaityādi ।।}
dhauteśāṅghriprasādopanatajayajagajjātamithyāmahimnām । doṣṇāṃ caiṣāṃ kimetat phalamiha nagarīrakṣaṇe yat prayāsaḥ ।।] śrutimātreṇa śabdāttu yenārthapratyayo bhavet । sādhāraṇaḥ samagrāṇāṃ sa prasādo guṇo mataḥ ।।
samagrāṇāṃ rasānāṃ saṃghaṭanānāṃ ca । udāharaṇam tanormadhyasyāntaḥ parimilanamaprāpya haritam । kṛśāṅgyāḥ saṃtāpaṃ vadati bisinīpatraśayanam ।।} vaktṛvācyaprabandhānāmaucityena kvacitkvacit ।
racanāvṛttivarṇānāmanyathātvamapīṣyate ।। kvacidvācyaprabandhānapekṣayā vaktraucityādeva racanādayaḥ । yathā koṇāghāteṣu garjatpralayaghanaghaṭānyonyasaṃghaṭṭacaṇḍaḥ । kenāsmatsiṃhanādapratirasitasakho dundubhistāḍitosau ।।}
atra hi na vācyaṃ krodhādivyañjakam । abhineyārthaṃ ca ca kāvyamiti tatpratikūlā uddhatā racanādayaḥ । vaktā cātra bhīmasenaḥ ।। kvacidvaktṛprabandhānapekṣayā vācyaucityādeva racanādayaḥ ।। trāsākṛṣṭāśvatiryagvalitaravirathenāruṇenekṣyamāṇam । bhāṅkārairbhīmametannipatati viyataḥ kumbhakarṇottamāṅgam ।।}
kvacidvaktṛvācyānapekṣāḥ prabandhocitā eva te ।। ākhyāyikāyāṃ śṛṅgāre api na masṛṇavarṇādayaḥ । kathāyāṃ raudre api nātyantamuddhatāḥ । nāṭakādau raudre api na dīrghasamāsādayaḥ ।। evamanyadapuaucityamanusartavyam ।। iti kāvyaprakāśe guṇālaṅkārabhedaniyataguṇanirṇayo nāma aṣṭama ullāsaḥ ।।
yaduktamanyathā vākyamanyathānyena yojyate । śleṣeṇa kākvā vā jñeyā sā vaktroktistathā dvidhā ।। tatheti śleṣavakroktiḥ kākuvakroktiśca । tara padabhaṅgaśleṣeṇa yathā vāmānāṃ priyamādadhāti hitakṛnnaivābalānāṃ bhavān ।
sāmarthyaṃ bhavataḥ purandaramatacchedaṃ vidhātuṃ kutaḥ ।।} {aho kenedṛśī buddhirdāruṇā tava nirmitā । triguṇā śrūyate buddhirna tu dārumayī kvacit ।।} {gurujanaparatantratayā dūrataraṃ deśamudyato gantum ।
alikulakokilalalite naiṣyati sakhi surabhisamaye asau ।।} svaravaisādṛśye api vyañjanasadṛśatvaṃ varṇasāmyam । rasādyanugataḥ prakṛṣṭo nyāso anuprāsaḥ ।। chekavṛttigato dvidhā । chekāḥ vidagdhāḥ । vṛttirniyatavarṇagato rasaviṣayo vyāpāraḥ । gata iti chekānuprāso vṛttyanuprāsaśca ।।
anekasya arthāt vyañjanasya sakṛdekavāraṃ sādṛśyaṃ chekānuprāsaḥ । udāharaṇam {tato aruṇaparispandamandīkṛtavapuḥ śaśī । dadhre kāmaparikṣāmakāminīgaṇḍapāṇḍutām ।।} ekasyāpyasakṛtparaḥ ।।
ekasya apiśabdādanekasya vyañjanasya dvirbahukṛtvo vā sādṛśyaṃ vṛttyanuprāsaḥ ।। mādhuryavyñjakairvarṇairupanāgarikocyate । ubhayatrāpi prāgudāhṛtam । komalā paraiḥ ।।
paraiḥ śeṣaiḥ । tāmeva kecit grāmyeti vadanti । udāharaṇam {apasārasya ghanasāraṃ kuru hāraṃ dūra eva kiṃ kamalaiḥ । alamalamāli mṛṇākairiti vadati divāniśaṃ bālā ।।} ।।
keṣāṃcidetā vaidarbhīpramukhā rītayo matāḥ । etāstisro vṛttayaḥ vāmānādīnāṃ mate vaidarbhīgauḍīpāñcālyākhyā rītayo matāḥ ।। śābdastu lāṭānuprāso bhede tātparyamātrataḥ ।। śabdagato anuprāsaḥ śabdārthayorabhede apyanvayamātrabhedāt lāṭajanavallabhatvācca lāṭānuprāsaḥ । eṣa padānuprāsa ityanye ।।
sa iti lāṭānuprāsaḥ । udāharaṇam {yasya na savidhe dayitā davadahanastuhinadīdhitistasya । yasya ca savidhe dayitā davadahanastuhinadīdhitistasya ।।} apiśabdena sa iti samuccīyate । udāharaṇam
{vadanaṃ varavarṇinyāstasyāḥ satyaṃ sudhākaraḥ । sudhākaraḥ kva nu punaḥ kalaṅkavikalo bhavet ।।} vṛttāvanyatra tatra vā । ekasmin samāse bhinne vā samāse samāsāsamāsayorvā nāmnaḥ prātipadikasya na tu padasya sārūpyam । udāharaṇam
{sitakarakararuciravibhā vibhākarākāra dharaṇidhara kīrtiḥ । pauruṣakamalā kamalā sāpi tavaivāsti nānyasya ।।} tadevaṃ pañcadhā mataḥ ।। arthe satyarthabhinnānāṃ varṇānāṃ sā punaḥ śrutiḥ ।
samarasamaraso ayamityādāvekeṣāmarthavattve anyeṣāmanarthakatve bhinnārthānāmiti na yujyate vaktum iti arthe satītyuktam । seti sarorasa ityādivailakṣaṇyena tenaiva krameṇa sthitā । pādatadbhāgavṛtti tadyātyanekatām ।। prathamo dvitīyādau dvitīyastṛtīyādau tṛtīyaścaturthe prathamastriṣvapīti sapta । prathamo dvitīye tṛtīyaścaturthe prathamaścaturthe dvitīyastṛtīye, iti dve । tadevaṃ pādajaṃ navabhedam । ardhāvṛttiḥ ślokāvṛttiśceti dve । dvidhā vibhakte pāde prathamādipādādibhāgaḥ pūrvavat dvitīyādipādādibhāgeṣu antabhāgo anantabhāgeṣviti viṃśatirbhedāḥ ślokāntare hi nāsau bhāgāvṛttiḥ । trikhaṇḍe triṃśat catuḥkhaṇḍe catvāriṃśat ।
prathamapādādigatāntyārghādibhāgo dvitīyapādādigate ādyārdhādibhāge yamyate ityādyanvarthatānusaraṇenānekabhedam । ādyantikam । madhyādikam । antamadhyam । teṣāṃ samuccayaḥ । tathā tasminneva pāde ādyādibhāgānāṃ madhyādibhāge aniyate ca sthāne āvṛttiriti prabhūtatamabhedam । tadetatkāvyāntargaḍubhūtam iti nāsya bhedalakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam । diṅmātramudāhriyate । {sannārībharaṇomāyamārādhya vidhuśekharam । sannārībharaṇomāyastatastvaṃ pṛthivīṃ jaya ।।}
{vināyameno nayatāsukhādinā vinā yamenonayatā sukhādinā । mahājanodīyata mānasādaraṃ mahājanodī yatamānasādaram ।।} {sa tvārambharatovaśyamabalaṃ vitatāravam । sarvadā raṇamānaiṣīdavānalasamasthitaḥ ।।}
{sattvārambharatovaśyamavalambitatāravam । sarvadāraṇamānaiṣī davānalasamasthitaḥ ।।} {anantamahimavyāptaviśvāṃ vedhā na veda yām । yā ca māteva bhajate praṇate mānave dayām ।।}
{yadānato ayadā nato nayātyayaṃ na yātyayam । śivehitāṃ śive hitāṃ smarāmitāṃ smarāmi tām ।।} {sarasvati prasādaṃ me sthitiṃ cittasarasvati । sara svati kuru kṣetrakurukṣetrasarasvati ।।}
{sasāra sākaṃ darpaṇe kandarpeṇa sasārasā । śarannavānā bibhrāṇā nāvibhrāṇā śarannavā ।।} {madhuparājiparājitamānījanamanaḥsumanaḥsurabhi śriyam । abhṛta vāritavārijaviplavaṃ sphuṭitatāmratatāmravaṇaṃ jagat ।।}
evaṃ vaicitryasahasraiḥ sthitamanyadunneyam ।। vācyabhedena bhinnā tad yugapadbhāṣaṇaspṛśaḥ । śliṣyanti śabdāḥ śleṣo asāvakṣarādibhiraṣṭadhā ।। {arthabhedena śabdabhedaḥ} iti darśane {kāvyamārge svaro na gaṇyate} iti ca naye vācyabhedena bhinnā api śabdā yat yugapaduccāraṇena śliṣyanti bhinnaṃ svarūpamapahnuvate sa śleṣaḥ ।
sa ca varṇapadaliṅgabhāṣāprakṛtipratyayavibhaktivacanñanāṃ bhedādaṣṭadhā । krameṇodāharaṇam viśīrṇāṅgo bhṛṅgī avsu ca vṛṣa eko bahuvayāḥ । vidhau vakre mūrdhni sthitavati vayaṃ ke punaramī ।।} {pṛthukārtasvarapātraṃ bhūṣitaniḥśeṣaparijanaṃ deva ।
vilasatkareṇugahanaṃ saṃprati samamāvayoḥ sadanam ।।} dhyānālambanatāṃ samādhiniratairnītehitaprāptaye । yuṣmākaṃ kurutāṃ bhavārtiśamanaṃ netre tanurvā hareḥ ।।} eṣa vacanaśleṣo api ।
{mahadesurasaṃdhamme tamavasamāsaṃgamāgamāharaṇe । harabahusaraṇaṃ taṃ cittamohamavasaraume sahasā ।।} [mama dehi rasaṃ dharme tamoaśām āśāṃ gamāgamāt hara naḥ । haravadhu śaraṇaṃ tvaṃ cittamoho apasaratu me sahasā ।।]
{ayaṃ sarvāṇi śāstrāṇi hṛdi jñeṣu ca vakṣyati । sāmarthyakṛdamitrāṇāṃ mitrāṇāṃ ca nṛpātmajaḥ ।।} kṣaṇasamayaparāptāpūrvasaṃsahasram । ahamucitaruciḥ syānnanditā sā tathā me ।।}
{sarvasvaṃ hara sarvasya tvaṃ bhavacchedatatparaḥ । nayopakārasāṃmukhyamāyāsi tanuvartanam ।।} bhedābhāvātprakṛtyāderbhedo api navamo bhavet । navamopītyapirbhinnakramaḥ । udāharaṇam
{yosakṛtparagotrāṇāṃ pakṣacchedakṣaṇakṣamaḥ । śatakoṭidatāṃ bibhradcibudhendraḥ sa rājate ।।} atra prakaraṇādiniyamābhāvāt dvāvapyarthau vācyau ।। nanu svaritādiguṇabhedād bhinnaprayatnoccāryāṇāṃ tadabhāvādabhinnaprayatnoccāryāṇāṃ ca śabdānāṃ bandhe alaṅkārāntarapratibhotpattihetuḥ śabdaśleṣo arthaśleṣaśceti dvividho apyarthālaṅkāramadhye parigaṇito anyairiti kathamayaṃ śabdālaṅkāraḥ ।
ucyate iha doṣaguṇālaṅkārāṇāṃ śabdārthagatatvena yo vibhāgaḥ saḥ anvayavyatirekābhyāmeva vyavatiṣṭhate । tathāhi kaṣṭavādigāḍhatvādyanuprāsādayaḥ vyarthatvādiprauḍhyādyupamādayastadbhāvatadabhāvānuvidhāyitvādeva śabdārthagatatvena vyavasthāpyante । svayaṃ ca pallavātāmrabhāsvatkaravirājitā । ityabhaṅgaḥ {prabhātasaṃdhyevāsvāpaphalalubdhehitapradā ।।} na tvādyasyārthaśleṣatvam । arthaśleṣasya tu sa viṣayaḥ yatra śabdaparivartane api na śleṣatvakhaṇḍanā । yathā
{stokenonnatimāyāti stokenāyātyadhogatim । aho susadṛśī vṛttistulākoṭeḥ khalasya ca ।।} na cāyamupamāpratibhotpattihetuḥ śleṣaḥ api tu śleṣapratibhotpattiheturupamā । tathāpi yathā {kamalamiva mukhaṃ manojñametatkacatitarām} ityādau guṇasāmye kriyāsāmye ubhayasāmye vā upamā । tathā asakalakalaṃ purametajjātaṃ saṃprati sudhāṃśubimbamiva'; ityādau śabdamātrasāmye api sā yuktaiva । tathā hyuktaṃ rudraṭena
{sphuṭamarthālaṅkārāvetāvupamāsamuccayau kiṃ tu । āśritya śabdamātraṃ sśmānyamihāpi saṃbhavataḥ ।।} iti । na ca {kamalamiva mukham} ityādiḥ sādhāraṇadharmaprayogaśūnya upamāviṣaya iti vaktaṃ yuktaṃ pūrṇopamāyā nirviṣayatvāpatteḥ ।। {deva tvameva pātālamāśānāṃ tvaṃ nibandhanam ।
tvaṃ cāmaramarudbhūmireko lokatrayātmakaḥ ।।} ityādiḥ śleṣasya copamādyalaṅkāraviviktosti viṣaya iti । dvayoryoge saṃkara eva । upapattiparyālocane tu upamāyā evāyaṃ yukto viṣayaḥ । anyathā viṣayāpahāra eva pūrṇopamāyāḥ syāt । na ca aabindusundarī nityaṃ galallāvaṇyabindukā'; ityādau virodhapratibhotpattihetuḥ śleṣaḥ api tu śleṣapratibhotpattiheturvirodhaḥ । na hyatrārthadvayapratipādakaḥ śabdaśleṣaḥ dvitīyārthasya pratibhātamātrasya prarohābhāvāt । na ca virodhābhāsa iva virodhaḥ śleṣābhāsaḥ śleṣaḥ । tadevamādiṣu vākyeṣu śleṣapratibhotpattiheturalaṅkārāntarameva । tathā ca
{ sadvaṃśamuktāmaṇiḥ ।।} {nālpaḥ kaviriva svalpaśloko deva mahān bhavān ।।} {anurāgavatī saṃdhyā divasastatpuraḥsaraḥ । aho daivagatiścitrā tathāpi na samāgamaḥ ।।}
{ādāya cāpamacalaṃ kṛtvāhīnaṃ guṇaṃ viṣamadṛṣṭiḥ । yaścitramacyutaśaro lakṣyamabhāṅkṣīnnamastasmai ।।} ityādāvekadeśavivartirūpakaśleṣavyatirekasamāsoktivirodhatvamucitaṃ na tu śleṣatvam ।। śabdaśleṣa iti cocyate arthālaṅkāramadhye ca lakṣyate iti ko ayaṃ nayaḥ । kiṃ ca caicitryamalaṅkāra iti ya eva kavipratibhāsaṃrambhagocarastatreva vicitratā iti saivālaṅkārabhūmiḥ । arthamukhaprekṣitvameteṣāṃ śabdānāmiti cet anuprāsādīnāmapi tathaiveti te apyarthālaṅkārāḥ kiṃ nocyante । rasādivyañjakasvarūpavācyaviśeṣasavyapekṣatve api hyanuprāsādīnām
alaṅkāratā । śabdaguṇadoṣāṇāmapyarthāpekṣayaiva guṇadoṣatā । arthaguṇadoṣālaṅkārāṇāṃ śabdāpekṣayaiva vyavasthitiriti te api śabdagatatvenocyantām । {vidhau vakre mūrdhni} ityādau ca varṇādiśleṣe ekaprayatnoccāryatve arthaśleṣatvaṃ śabdabhede api prasajyatāmityevamādi svayaṃ vicāryam ।। taccitraṃ yatra varṇānāṃ khaḍgādyākṛtihetutā ।। saṃniveśaviśeṣeṇa yatra nyastā varṇāḥ khaḍgamurajapadmādyākāramullāsayanti taccitraṃ kāvyam । kaṣṭaṃ kāvyametaditi diṅmātraṃ pradarśyate । udāharaṇam
{mārāriśakrarāmebhamukhairāsāraraṃhasā । sārārabdhastavā nityaṃ tadārtiharaṇakṣamā ।।} {mātā natānāṃ saṃghaṭṭaḥśriyāṃ bādhitasaṃbhramā । mānyātha sīmā rāmāṇāṃ śaṃ me diśyādumādimā ।।}
{saralā bahulārambhataralālibalāravā । vāralābahulāmandakaralābahulāmalā ।।} {bhāsate pratibhāsāra rasābhātāhatāvibhā । bhāvitātmā śubhā vāde devābhā bata te sabhā ।।}
{rasāsāra rasā sārasāyatākṣakṣatāyasā । sātāvāta tavātāsā rakṣatastvastvatakṣara ।।} saṃbhavino apyanye prabhedāḥ śaktimātraprakāśakā na tu kāvyarūpatāṃ dadhatīti na pradarśyante ।। punarektavadābhāso vibhinnākāraśabdagā ।
bhinnarūpasārthakānarthakaśabdaniṣṭhamekārthatvena mukhe bhāsanaṃ punaruktavadābhāsaḥ । sa ca sabhaṅgābhaṅgarūpakevalaśabdaniṣṭhaḥ । udāharaṇam {arivadhadehaśarīraḥ sahasā rathisūtaturagapādātaḥ । bhāti sadānatyāgaḥ sthiratāyāmavanitalatilakaḥ ।।}
{cakāsatyaṅganārāmāḥ kautukānandahetavaḥ । tasya rājñaḥ sumanaso vibudhāḥ pārśvavartinaḥ ।।} tathā śabdārthayorayam ।। {tanuvapurajaghanyo asau karikuñjararudhiraraktakharanakharaḥ ।
tejodhāma mahaḥpṛthumanasāmindro harirjiṣṇuḥ ।।} atraikasmin pade parivartite nālaṅkāra iti śabdāśrayaḥ aparasmiṃstu parivartite api sa na hīyate ityarthaniṣṭha ityubhayālaṅkāro ayam ।। iti kāvyaprakāśe śabdālaṅkāranirṇayo nāma navama ullāsaḥ ।। upamānopameyayoreva na tu kāryakāraṇādikayoḥ sādharmyaṃ bhavatīti tayoreva samānena dharmeṇa saṃbandha upamā ।
upamānopameyasādhāraṇadharmopamāpratipādakānāmupādāne pūrṇā । ekasya dvayostrayāṇāṃ vā lope luptā ।। sāgrimā । śrautyārthī ca bhavedvākye samāse taddhite tathā ।। agrimā pūrṇā ।
yathevādiśabdā yatparāstasyaivopamānatāpratītiriti yadyapyupamānaviśeṣaṇānyete tathāpi śabdaśaktimahimnā śrutyaiva ṣaṣṭhīvat saṃbandhaṃ pratipādayantīti tatsadbhāve śrautī upamā । tathaiva {tatra tasyeva} ityanenevārthe vihitasya vaterupādāne ।। vihitasya vateḥ sthitau । {ivena nityasamāso vibhaktyapolaḥ pūrvapadakṛtisvaratvaṃ ca} iti nityasamāse ivaśabdayoge samāsagā ।। krameṇodāharaṇam
{svapne api samareṣu tvāṃ vijayaśrīrna muñchati । prabhāvaprabhavaṃ kāntaṃ svādhīnapatikā yathā ।।} {cakitahariṇalolalocanāyāḥ krudhi taruṇāruṇatārahārikānti । sarasijamidamānanaṃ ca tasyāḥ samamiti cetasi saṃmadaṃ vidhatte ।।}
divyaiḥ prabhābhiranapāyamayairupāyaiḥ । lakṣmīvilāsabhavanairbhuvanaṃ babhāra ।।} {avitathamanorathapathaprathaneṣu praguṇa garimagītaśrīḥ । suratarusadṛśaḥ sa bhavān abhilaṣaṇīyaḥ kṣitīśvaro na kasya ।।}
{gāmbhīryagarimā tasya satyaṅgaṅgābhujaṅgavat । durālokaḥ sa samare nidāghāmbararatnavat ।।} svādhīnapatikā kāntaṃ bhajamānā yathāṃ lokottaracamatkārabhūḥ tathā jayaśrīstvadāsevanenetyādinā pratīyamānena vinā yadyapi noktervaicitryam । vaicitryaṃ cālaṅkāraḥ । tathāpi na dhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyavyavahāraḥ । na khalu vyaṅgyasaṃsparśaparāmarśādatra cārutāpratītiḥ । api tu vācya vaicityapratibhāsādeva ।। rasādistu vyaṅgyor'rthālaṅkārāntaraṃ ca sarvatrāvyabhicārītyagaṇayitvaiva tadalaṅkārā udāhṛtāḥ । tadrahitatvena tu udāhriyamāṇā virasatāmāvahantīti pūrvāparaciruddhābhidhānamiti na codanīyam ।।
tadvad dharmasya lope syānna śrautī taddhite punaḥ । dharmaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ । taddhite kalpavādau tvārthyeva ।। {dhanyasyānanyasāmānyasaujanyotkarṣaśālinaḥ । karaṇīyaṃ vacaścetaḥ satyaṃ tasyāmṛtaṃ yathā ।।}
{ākṛṣṭakaravālo asau saṃparāye paribhraman । pratyarthisenayā dṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāntena samaḥ prabhuḥ ।।} {karavāla ivācārastasya vāgamṛtopamā । viṣakalpaṃ mano vetsi yadi jīvasi tatsakhe ।।}
upamānānupādāne vākyagātha samāsagā ।। {saalakaraṇaparavīsāmasiriviaraṇaṃ ṇa sarasakavvassa । dīsai aha vā ṇisammai sarisaṃ aṃsaṃsametteṇa ।।} [sakalakaraṇaparaciśrāmaśrīvitaraṇaṃ na sarasakāvyasya ।
dṛśyate atha vā niśamyate sadṛśamaṃśāṃśamātreṇa ।।] kavvassetryatra kavvasamamiti sarisamityatra ca ṇūṇamiti pāṭhe eṣaiva samāsagā ।। vāderlope samāse sā karmādhārakyaci kyaṅi । vāśabdaḥ upamādyotaka iti । vāderupamāpratipādakasya lope ṣaṭ samāsena karnṇo adhikaraṇāccotpannena kyacā kartuḥ kyaṅā karmakartrorupapadayorṇamulā ca bhavet ।।
{tataḥ kumudanāthena kāminīgaṇḍapāṇḍunā । netrānandena candreṇa māhendrī digalaṅkṛtā ।।} {asitabhujagabhīṣaṇāsipatro ruharuhikāhitacittatūrṇacāraḥ । pulakitatanurutkapolakāntiḥ pratibhaṭavikramadarśaneyamāsīt ।।}
vantaḥpurīyati vicitracaritracuñcuḥ । ālokya tasya caritāni sapatnasenā ।।} {mṛdhe nidāghagharmāṃśudarśaṃ paśyanti taṃ pare । sa punaḥ pārthasaṃcāraṃ saṃcaratyavanīpatiḥ ।।}
etaddvilope kvipsamāsagā ।। etayordhrmavādyoḥ । udāharaṇam {savitā vidhavati vidhurapi savitarati tathā dinanti yāminyaḥ । yāminayanti dināni ca sukhaduḥkhavaśīkṛte manasi ।।}
{paripanthimanojyaśatairapi durākramaḥ । saṃparāyapravṛttausau rājate rājakuñjaraḥ ।।} ।। dharmopamānayorlope vṛttau vākye ca dṛśyate ।
{ṭuṭuṇṇanto marihisi kaṇṭaakaliāiṃ keaivaṇāiṃ । mālaikusumasaricchaṃ bhamara bhamanto ṇa pāvihisi ।।} [ṭuṇṭuṇāyamāno mariṣyasi kaṇṭakakalitāni ketakīvanāni । mālatīkusumasadṛkṣaṃ bhramara bhraman na prāpsyasi ।।]
kusumeṇa samamiti pāṭhe vākyagā । āse nirāse । {arātivikramālokavikasvaravilocanaḥ । kṛpāṇodagradordaṇḍaḥ sa sahasrāyudhīyati ।।}
atrātmā upameyaḥ । trilope ca samāsagā ।। trayāṇāṃ vādidharmopamānānām । udāharaṇam {taruṇamani kṛtāvalokanā lalitavilāsavitīrṇavigrahā ।
smaraśaravisarācitāntarā mṛganayanā harate munermanaḥ ।।} atra saptamyupamānetyādinā yadā samāsalopau bhavataḥ ।। krūrasyācārasyāyaḥśūlatayādhyavasāyād ayaḥśūlenānvicchati {āyaḥśūlikaḥ} ityatiśayoktirna tu krūrācāropameyataikṣṇyadharmavādīnāṃ lope trilope ayamupamā । evamekonaviṃśatirluptāḥ pūrṇābhiḥ saha pañcaviṃśatiḥ ।।
{anayeneva rājyaśrīrdainyeneva manasvitā । mamlau sātha viṣādena padminīva himāmbhasā ।।} ityabhinne sādhāraṇe dharme ।। {jyotsneva nayanānandaḥ sureva madakāraṇam ।
prabhuteva samākṛṣṭasarvalokā nitambinī ।।} ity bhinne ca tasmin ekasyaiva bahūpamānopādāne mālopamā । {anavaratakanakavitaraṇajalalavabhṛtakarataraṅgitārthitateḥ । bhaṇitiriva matirmatiriva ceṣṭā ceṣṭeva kīrtirativimalā ।।}
{matiriva mūrtirmadhurā mūrtiriva sabhā prabhāvacitā । tasya sabheva jayaśrīḥ śakyā jetuṃ nṛpasya na pareṣām ।।} uktabhedānatikramācca ।। upamānopameyatve ekasyaivaikavākyage ।
upamānāntarasaṃbandhābhāvo ananvayaḥ । udāharaṇam {na kevalaṃ bhāti nitāntakāntirnitambanī saiva nitambinīva । yāvadvilāsāyudhalāsyavāsāste tadvilāsā iva tadvilāsāḥ ।।} viparyāsa upameyopamā tayoḥ ।।
tayoḥ upamānopameyayoḥ । parivṛttiḥ arthāt vākyadvaye । itaropamānavyavacchedaparā upameyenopamā iti upameyopamā । udāharaṇam {kamaleva matirmatiriva kamalā tanuriva vibhā vibheva tanuḥ । dharaṇīva dhṛtirdhṛtiriva dharaṇī satataṃ vibhāti bata yasya ।। ।।
saṃbhāvanamathotprekṣā prakṛtasya samena yat । samena upamānena । udāharaṇam indorindīvaradaladṛśā tasya saundaryadarpaḥ । lagnā manye lalitatanu te pādayoḥ padmalakṣmīḥ ।।}
{limpatīva tamo aṅgāni varṣatīvāñjanaṃ nabhaḥ । asatpuruṣaseveva dṛṣṭirviphalatāṃ gatā ।।} ityādau vyāpanādi lepanādirūpatayā saṃbhāvitam ।। sasaṃdehastu bhedoktau tadanuktau ca saṃśayaḥ ।।
kṛśānuḥ kiṃ sarvāḥ prasarati diśo naiṣa niyatam । samālokyājau tvāṃ vidadhati vikalpān pratibhaṭāḥ ।।} bhedoktāvityanena na kevalamayaṃ niścayagarbho yāvanniścayānto api saṃdehaḥ svīkrṭaḥ । {induḥ kiṃ kva kalaṅkaḥ sarasijametat kimambu kutra gatam ।
lalitasavilāsavacanairmukhamiti hariṇākṣi niścitaṃ parataḥ ।।} bhaṭṭodbhaṭena । tadanuktau yathā śṛṅgāraikarasaḥ svayaṃ nu madano māso nu puṣpākaraḥ । nirmātuṃ prabhavenmanoharamidaṃ rūpaṃ purāṇo muniḥ ।।}
।। tadrūpakamabhedo ya upamānopameyayoḥ । atisāmyād anapahnutabhedayoḥ abhedaḥ । samastavastuciṣyaṃ śrautā āropitā yadā ।।
āropaviṣayā iva āropyamāṇāḥ yadā śabdopāttāḥ tadā samastāni vastūni viṣayosyeti samastavastuviṣayam । āropitā iti bahuvacanamavivakṣitam । yathā nyantardhānavyasanarasikā rātrikāpālikīyam । nyastaṃ siddhāñjanaparimalaṃ lāñchanasyacchalena ।।} atra pādatraye, antardhānavyasanarasikatvamāropitadharma eveti rūpakaparigrahe sādhakamastītitatsaṃkarāśaṅkā na kāryā ।।
śrautā ārthaśca te yasminnekadeśavivarti tat । kevidāropyamāṇāḥ śabdo apāttāḥ kecidarthasāmarthyādavaseyāḥ ityekadeśavivartanāt ekadeśavivarti । yathā {jassa raṇanteurae kare kuṇantassa maṇḍalaggalaaṃ । rasasaṃmuhī vi sahasā paramuhī hoi riuseṇā ।।}
[yasya raṇāntaḥpure kare kurvato maṇḍalāgralatām । rasasaṃmukhyapi sahasā parāñmukhī bhavati ripusenā ।।] atra raṇasyāntaḥpuratvamāropyamāṇaṃ śabdo apāttam maṇḍalāgralatāyāḥ nāyikātvam ripusenāyāśca pratināyikātvam arthasāmarthyādavasīyate iti ekadeśe viśeṣeṇa vartanādekadeśavivarti । uktadvibhedaṃ sāvayavam ।।
sakhīṃ kāntodantaṃ śrutamapi punaḥ praśnayati yat । pravṛtto asyāḥ sektuṃ hṛdi manasijaḥ premalatikām ।।} mālā tu pūrvavat ।। mālopamāyāmivaikasmin bahava āropitāḥ । yathā
kānteḥ kārmaṇakarma narmarahasāmullāsanāvāsabhūḥ । vāṇāḥ pañcaśilīmukhasya lalanācūḍāmaṇiḥ sā priyā ।।} ।। niyatāropaṇopāyaḥ syādāropaḥ parasya yaḥ ।
tatparaṃparitaṃ śliṣṭe vācake bhedabhāji vā ।। durgāmārgaṇanīlalohita samitsvīkāravaiśvānara । sāmrājyaṃ varavīra vatsaraśataṃ vairiñcamuccaiḥ kriyāḥ ।।} atra mānasameva mānasam kamalāyāḥ saṃkoca eva kamalānāmasaṃkocaḥ durgāṇāmamārgaṇameva durgāyāḥ mārgaṇam samitāṃ svīkāra eva samidhāṃ svīkāraḥ satye pratītireva satyāmaprītiḥ vijayaḥ paraparābhava eva vijayorjunaḥ evamāropaṇanimitto haṃsāderāropaḥ ।
yadyapi śabdārthālaṅkāro ayamityuktaṃ vakṣyate ca tathāpi prasiddhyanurodhādatroktaḥ । ekadeśavivarti hīdamanyairabhidhīyate ।। pūrvādriḥ karavālacaṇḍamahaso līlopadhānaṃ śriyaḥ । rājan rājati vīravairivanitāvaidhavyadaste bhujaḥ ।।} atra jayāderbhinnaśabdavācyasya kuñjaratvādyārope bhujasya ālānatvādyāropo yujyate ।
{alaukikamahālokaprakāśitajagattrayaḥ । stūyate deva sadvaṃśamuktāratnaṃ na kairbhavān ।।} {niravadhi ca nirāśrayaṃ ca yasya sthitamanivartitakautukaprapñcam । prathama iha bhavān sa kūrmamūrtirjayati caturdaśalokavallikandaḥ ।।}
iti ca amālārūpoakamapi paraṃparitaṃ draṣṭavyam ।। {kisalayakarairlatānāṃ karakamalaiḥ kāmināṃ mano jayati । nalinīnāṃ kamalamukhaiḥ mukhendubhiryoṣitāṃ madanaḥ ।।} ityādi raśanārūpakaṃ na vaicitryavaditi na lakṣitam ।।
prakṛtaṃ yanniṣidhyānyat sādhyate sā tvapahnutiḥ । kalaṅko naivāyaṃ vilasati śaśāṅkasya vapuṣi । ratiśrāntā śete rajaniramaṇī gāḍhamurasi ।।} priyavirahakṛśesmin rāgiloke tathā hi ।
prativiśikhamanenoṭṭaṅkitaṃ kālakūṭam ।।} atra hi na sabhṛṅgāṇi sahakārāṇi api tu sakālakūṭā śarā iti pratītiḥ । evaṃ vā smaraḥ śarvapluṣṭaḥ pṛthujaghanabhāge nipatitaḥ । śikhā dhūmasyeyaṃ pariṇaṃmati romāvalivapuḥ ।।}
atra na romāvaliḥ dhūmaśikheyamiti pratipattiḥ ।। evamiyaṃ bhaṅgyantarairapyūhyā ।। śleṣaḥ sa vākya ekasmin yatrānekārthatā bhavet ।। ekārthapratipādakānāmeva śabdānāṃ yatrāneko arthaḥ sa śleṣaḥ । udāharaṇam
nayati nidhanaṃ nidrāmudrāṃ pravartayati kriyāḥ । bata bata lasattejaḥpuñjo vibhāti vibhākaraḥ ।।} atrābhidhāyā aniyantraṇāt dvāvapyarkabhūpau vācyau ।। prakṛtārthapratipādakavākyena śliṣṭaviśeṣaṇamāhātmyāt na tu viśeṣyasya sāmarthyādapi yat aprakṛtasyārthasyābhidhānam sā samāsena saṃkṣepeṇārthadvayakathanāt samāsoktiḥ । udāharaṇam
{lahiūṇa tujjha bāhupphaṃsaṃ jīe sa ko vi ullāso । jaalacchī tuba virahe ṇa hujjalā dubbalā ṇaṃ sā ।।} [labdhvā tava bāhusparśa yasyāḥ sa ko apyullāsaḥ । jayalakṣmīstava virahe na khalūjjvalā durbalā nanu sā ।।]
atra jayalakṣmīśabdasya kevalaṃ kāntāvācakatvaṃ nāsti ।। nidarśanā । abhavanvastusaṃbandha upamāparikalpakaḥ ।। nidarśanaṃ dṛṣṭāntakaraṇam । udāharaṇam
{kva sūryaprabhāvo vaṃśaḥ kva cālpaviṣayā matiḥ । titīrṣurdustaraṃ mohāduḍupenāsmi sāgaram ।।} atra uḍupena sāgarataraṇamiva manmatyā sūryavaṃśavarṇanamityupamāyāṃ paryavasyati । {udayati vitatordhvaraśmirajjāvahimarucau himadhāmni yāti cāstam ।
vahati girirayaṃ vilambighaṇṭādvayaparivāritavāraṇendralīlām ।।} atra kathmanyasya līlāmanyo vahatīti tatsadṛśīmityupamāyāṃ paryavasānam । ādātumicchati kare hariṇāṅkabimbam । yaste guṇān gaditumudyamamādadhati ।।}
ityādau mālārūpāpyeṣā draṣṭavyā ।। svasvahetvanvayasyoktiḥ kriyayaiva ca sāparā । kriyayaiva svasvarūpasvakāraṇayoḥ saṃbandho yadavagamyate sā aparā nidarśanā । yathā {unnataṃ padamavāpya yo laghuhelayaiva patediti bruvan ।
śailaśekharagato dṛṣatkaṇaścārumārutadhutaḥ patatyadhaḥ ।।} atra pātakriyayā patanasya lāghave sati unnatapadaprāptirūpasya ca saṃbandhaḥ khyāpyate ।। aprastutapraśaṃsā yā sā saiva prastutāśrayā ।। aprākaraṇikasyābhidhānena prākaraṇikasyākṣepo aprastutapraśaṃsā ।।
kārye nimitte sāmānye viśeṣe prastute sati । tadanyasya vacastulye tulyasyeti ca pañcadhā ।। tadanyasya kāraṇādeḥ । krameṇodāhyaṇam no kāryā nitarāṃ kṛśāsi kathayatyevaṃ sabāṣpe mayi ।
dṛṣṭvā māṃ hasitena bhāvimaraṇotsāhastayā sūcitaḥ ।।} atra prasthānātkimiti nivṛtto asīti kārye pṛṣṭe kāraṇamabhihitam । kubje bhojaya māṃ kumārasacivairnādyāpi kiṃ bhujyate । citrasthānavalokya śūnyavalabhāvekaikamābhāṣate ।।}
atra prasthānodyataṃ bhavantaṃ jñātvā sahasaiva tvadarayaḥ palāyya gatāḥ iti kāraṇe prastute kāryamuktam । yanmuktāmaṇirityamaṃsta sa jaḍaḥśṛṇvanyadasmādapi । kutroḍḍīya gato mametyanudinaṃ nidrāti nāntaḥśucā ।।} atrāsthāne jaḍānāṃ mamatvasaṃbhāvanā bhavatīti sāmānye prastute viśeṣaḥ kathitaḥ ।
{suhṛdvadhūbāṣpajalapramārjanaṃ karoti vairapratiyātanena yaḥ । sa eva pūjyaḥ sa pumānsa nītimānsujīvitaṃ tasya sa bhājanaṃ śriyaḥ ।।} atra akṛṣṇaṃ nihatya narakāsuravadhūnāṃ yadi duḥkham praśamayasi tat tvameva ślāghyaḥ'; iti viśeṣe prakṛte sāmānyamabhihitam । tuye prastute tulyābhidhāne trayaḥ prakārāḥ । śleṣaḥ samāsoktiḥ sādṛśyamātraṃ vā tulyāt tulyasya hyākṣepe hetuḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam yāyād yadi praṇayane na mahānapi syāt ।
kenāpi dik orakaṭitā puruṣottamena ।।} yujyeta pratikartumeva na punastasyaiva pādagrahaḥ । astvevaṃ jaḍadhāmatā tu bhavato yad vyomni visphūrjase ।।} kiṃ tāvadarjitamanena durarṇavena ।
pātālakukṣikuhare viniveśitaṃ ca ।।} iyaṃ ca kācit vācye pratīyamānārthānadhyāropeṇaiva bhavati । yathā potopāyā iha hi bahavo laṅghane api kṣamante । ko nāma syādavaṭakuharālokane apyasya kalpaḥ ।।}
kvacidadhyāropeṇaiva । yathā vairāgyādiva vakṣi sādhu viditaṃ kasmādidaṃ kathyate । na cchāyāpi paropakārakaraṇe mārgasthitasyāpi me।।} kvacidaṃśeṣvadhyāropeṇa । yathā
dṛṣṭiḥ sā madavismṛtasvaparadik kiṃ bhūyasoktena vā । antaḥśūnyakaro niṣevyata iti bhrātaḥ ka eṣa grahaḥ ।।} atra rasanāvaparyāsaḥ śūnyakartvaṃ ca bhramarasyāsevane na hetuḥ karṇacāpalaṃ tu hetuḥ madaḥ pratyuta sevate nimittam ।। nigīryādhyavasānaṃ tu prakṛtasya pareṇa yat ।
prastutasya yadanyatvaṃ yadyarthoktau ca kalpanam ।। kāryakāraṇayoryaśca paurvāparyaviparyayaḥ । upamānenāntarnigīrṇasyopameyasya yadadhyavasānaṃ saikā । yathā {kamalamanambhasi kamale ca kubalaye tāni kanakalatikāyām ।
sā ca sukumārasubhagetyutpātaparaṃparā keyam ।।} atra mukhādi kamalādirūpatayādhyavasitam । yacca tadevānyatvenādhyavasīyate sā aparā । yathā {aṇṇaṃ laḍahattaṇaaṃ aṇṇā via kā vi vattaṇacchāā । sāmā sāmaṇṇapaāvaiṇo rehaccia ṇa hoi ।।}
[anyatsaukumāryam anyaiva ca kāpi vartanacchāyā । śyāmā sāmānyaprajāpateḥ rekṣaiva ca na bhavati ।।] sā tṛtīyā । yathā {rākāyāmakalaṅkaṃ cedamṛtāṃśorbhavedvapuḥ ।
tasyā mukhaṃ tadā sāmyaparābhavamavāpnuyāt ।।} kāraṇasya śīghrakāritāṃ vaktuṃ kāryasya pūrvamuktau caturthī । yathā {hṛdayamadhiṣṭhitamādau mālatyāḥ kusumacāpabāṇena । caramaṃ ramaṇīvallabha locanaviṣayaṃ tvayā bhajatā ।।}
prativastūpamā tu sā ।। sāmānyasya dvirekasya yatra vākyadvaye sthitiḥ । sādhāraṇo dharmaḥ upameyavākye upamānavākye ca kathitapadasya duṣṭatayābhihitatvāt śabdabhedena yat upādīyate sā vastūno vākyārthasyopamānatvāt prativastūpamā । yathā {devībhāvaṃ gamitā parivārapadaṃ kathaṃ bhajatveṣā ।
na khalu paribhogayogyaṃ daivatarūpāṅkitaṃ ratnam ।।} {yadi dahatyanalo atra kimadbhutaṃ yadi ca gauravamadriṣu kiṃ tataḥ । lavaṇamambu sadaiva mahodadheḥ prakṛtireva satāmaviṣāditā ।।} ityādikā mālāprativastūpamā draṣṭavyā । evamanyatrāpyanusartavyam ।।
dṛṣṭāntaḥ punareteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratibimbanam ।। eteṣāṃ sādhāraṇadharmādīnāṃ dṛṣṭo anto niścayo yatra sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ । {tvayi dṛṣṭa eva tasyā nirvāti mano manobhavajvalitam । āloke hi himāṃśorvikasati kusumaṃ kumudvatyāḥ ।।}
eṣa sādharmyeṇa । vaidharmyeṇa tu {tavāhave sāhasakarmaśarmaṇaḥ karaṃ kṛpāṇāntikamāninīṣataḥ । bhaṭaḥ pareṣāṃ viśarārutāmaguḥ dadhatyavāte sthiratāṃ hi pāṃsavaḥ ।।} ।।
sakṛdvṛttistu dharmasya prakṛtāprakṛtātmanām । saiva kriyāsu bahvīṣu kārakasyeti dīpakam ।। prākaraṇikāprākaraṇikānām arthāt upamānopameyānāṃ dharmaḥ kriyādiḥ ekavārameva yat upādīyate tat ekasthasyaiva samastavākyadīpanād dīpakam । yathā {kivaṇāṇaṃ dhaṇaṃ ṇāgāṇaṃ phaṇamaṇī keśarāiṃ sīhāṇaṃ ।
kulabāliāṇaṃ tthaṇaā kutto chippanti amuāṇaṃ ।।} [kṛpaṇānāṃ dhanaṃ nāgānāṃ phaṇamaṇiḥ kesarā siṃhānām । kulabālikānāṃ stanāḥ kutaḥ spṛśyante amṛtānām ।।] kārakasya ca bahvīṣu kriyāsu sakṛdvṛttidīrpakam । yathā
{svidya[t]i kūṇati vellati vicalati nimiṣati vilokayati tiryak । antarnandati cumbatumicchati navapariṇayā vadhūḥ śayane ।।} ।। mālādīpakamādyaṃ cetyathottaraguṇāvaham ।
pūrveṇa pūrveṇa vastunā uttaramuttaraṃ cedupakriyate tat mālādīpakam । yathā devākraṇaya yena yena sahasā yadyatsamāsāditam । tena tvaṃ bhavatā ca kīrtiratulā kīrtyā ca lokatrayam ।।} niyatānāṃ sakṛddharmaḥ sā punastulyayogitā ।।
niyatānāṃ prākaraṇikānāmeva aprākaraṇikānāmeva vā । krameṇodāharaṇam {pāṇḍu kṣāmaṃ vadanaṃ hṛdayaṃ sarasaṃ tavālasaṃ ca vapuḥ । āvedayati nitāntaṃ kṣetriyarogaṃ sakhi hṛdantaḥ ।।} {kumudakamalanīlanīrajālirlalitavilāsajuṣordṛśoḥ puraḥ kā ।
amṛtamamṛtaraśmirambujanma pratihatamekapade tavānanasya ।।} ।। upamānādyadanyasya vyatirekaḥ sa eva saḥ । anyasyopameyasya vyatireka ādhikyam ।
{kṣīṇaḥ kṣīṇo api śaśī bhūyo bhūyo vivardhate satyam । virama prasīda sundari yauvanamanivarti yātaṃ tu ।।} tadyuktam । atra yauvanagatāstairyādhikyaṃ hi vivakṣitam ।। hetvoruktāvanuktīnāṃ traye sāmye nivedite ।।
śabdārthābhyāmathākṣipte śliṣṭe tadvattriraṣṭa tat । vyatirekasya hetuḥ upameyagatamutkarṣanimittam । upamānagatamapakarṣakāraṇam । tayordvayoruktiḥ, ekatarasya dvayorvā anuktirityanuktitrayam । etadbhedacatuṣṭayamupamānopameyabhāve śabdena pratipādite ārthena ca krameṇoktāścatvāra eva bhedāḥ । ākṣipte caupamye tāvanta eva ।। ete śleṣe api bhavantīti caturviśatirbhedāḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam {asimātrasahāyasya prabhūtāriparābhave । anyatucchajanasyeva na smayo asya mahādhṛteḥ ।।}
atraiva tuccheti mahādhṛterityanayoḥ paryāyeṇa yugapadvānapādānenyat bhedatrayam । evamanyeṣvapi draṣṭavyam । atra ivaśabdasya sadbhāvācchābdamaupamyam । {asimātrasahāyo api prabhūtāriparābhave । naivānyatucchajanavatsagarvo ayaṃ mahādhṛtiḥ ।।} atr trulyārthe vatirityārthamaupamyam ।
{iyaṃ sunayanā dāsīkṛtatāmarasaśriyā । ānanenākalaṅkena jayatīnduṃ kalaṅkinam ।।} atrevāditulyādipadaviraheṇa ākṣiptaivopamā । {jitendriyatayā samyagvidyāvṛddhaniṣeviṇaḥ ।
atigāḍhaguṇasyāsya nābjavadbhaṅgurā guṇāḥ ।।} atrevārthe vatiḥ । guṇaśabdaḥ śliṣṭaḥ । śābdamaupamyam ।। {akhaṇḍamaṇḍalaḥ śrīmān paśyaiṣa pṛthivīpatiḥ । na niśākaravajjātu kalāvaikalyamāgataḥ ।।}
atra tulyārthe vatiḥ । kalāśabdaḥ śliṣṭaḥ । mālāprativastūpamāvat mālāvyatireko api saṃbhavati । tasyāpi bhedā evamūhyāḥ । diṅmātramudāhriyate । yathā {haravanna viṣamadṛṣṭirharivanna vibho vidhūtavitatavṛṣaḥ । rativanna cātiduḥsahakaratāpitabhūḥ kadācidasi ।।}
atra tulyārthe vatiḥ । viṣamādayaśca śabdāḥ śliṣṭāḥ । {nityoditapratāpena triyāmāmīlitaorabhaḥ । bhāsvatānena bhūpena bhāsvāneṣa vinirjitaḥ ।।} atra hyākṣiptaivopamā bhāsvatetiśliṣṭaḥ । yathā vā
bimbaprabhādharamakṛtrimahṛdyagandham । tṛṣṇāṃ jahāra madhu nānanamaṅganānām ।।} atrevādīnāṃ tulyādīnāṃ ca padānāmabhāve api śliṣṭaviśeṣaṇairākṣiptaivopamā pratīyate । evañjātīyakāḥ śliṣṭoktiyogyasya padasya pṛthagpādāne anyepi bhedāḥ saṃbhavanti । te api anayaiva diśā draṣṭavyāḥ ।। niṣedho vaktumiṣṭasya yo viśeṣābhidhitsayā ।।
vakṣyamāṇoktaviṣayaḥ sa ākṣepo dvidhā mataḥ । vivakṣitasya prākaraṇikatvādanupasarjanīkāryasya aśakyavaktavyatvam atiprasiddhatvaṃ vā viśeṣaṃ vaktuṃ niṣedho niṣedha iva yaḥ sa vakṣyamāṇaviṣaya uktaviṣayaśceti dvidhā ākṣepaḥ । {e ehi kiṃapi kīevi aeṇa ṇikkiva bhaṇāmi alamaha vā । aviāriakajjārambhaāriṇī marau ṇa bhaṇissaṃ ।।}
[e ehi kimapi kasyā api kṛte niṣkṛpa bhaṇāmi alamatha vā । avicāritakāryārambhakāriṇī mriyatāṃ na bhaniṣyāmi ।।] karpūraṃ kadalī mṛṇālavalayānyambhojinīpallavāḥ । vyāpārāya bhavanti hanta kimanenoktena na brūmahe ।।}
kriyāyāḥ pratiṣedhe api phalavyaktirvibhāvanā ।। heturūpakriyāyāḥ niṣedhe api tatphalaprakāśanaṃ vibhāvanā । yathā {kusumitalatābhirahatāpyadhatta rujamalikulairadaṣṭāpi । parivartate sma nalinīlaharībhiralolitāpyaghūrṇata sā ।।}
।। viśeṣoktirakhaṇḍeṣu kāraṇeṣu phalāvacaḥ । militeṣvapi kāraṇeṣu kāryasyākathanaṃ viśeṣoktiḥ । anuktanimittā uktanimittā acintyanimittā ca । krameṇodāharaṇam {nidrānivṛttāvudite dyuratne sakhījane dvārapadaṃ parāpte ।
ślathīkṛtāśleṣarase bhujaṅge cacāla nāliṅganatoṅganā sā ।।} {karpūra iva dagdho api śaktimān yo jane jane । namo astvavāryavīryāya tasmai makaraketave ।।} {sa ekastrīṇi jayati jaganti kusumāyudhaḥ ।
haratāpi tanuṃ yasya śambhunā na balaṃ hṛtam ।।} yathāsaṃkhyaṃ krameṇaiva kramikāṇāṃ samanvayaḥ ।। deva dviṣāṃ ca viduṣāṃ ca mṛgīdṛśāṃ ca । śauryoṣmaṇā ca vinayena ca līlayā ca ।।}
।। sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā tadanyena samarthyate । yattu so arthāntaranyāsaḥ sādharmyeṇetareṇa vā ।। sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa vā sāmānyaṃ viśeṣeṇa yat samarthyate viśeṣo vā sāmānyena so arthāntaranyāsaḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam
{nijadoṣāvṛtamanasāmatisundarameva bhāti viparītam । paśyati pittopahataḥ śaśiśubhraṃ śaṅkhamapi pītam ।।} mahasi sudṛśi svairaṃ yāntyāṃ gato astamabhūdvidhuḥ । priyagṛhamagānmuktāśaṅkā kva nāsi śubhapradaḥ ।।}
{guṇānāmeva daurātmyād dhuri dhuryo niyujyate । asaṃjātakiṇaskandhaḥ sukhaṃ svapiti gaurgaliḥ ।।} {aho hi me bahvaparāddhamāyuṣā yadapriyaṃ vācyamidaṃ mayedṛśam । ta eva dhanyāḥ suhṛdaḥ parābhavaṃ jagatyadṛṣṭvaiva hi ye kṣayaṃ gatāḥ ।।}
।। virodhaḥ sovirodhe api viruddhatvena yadvacaḥ । vastuvṛttenāvirodhe api viruddhayoriva yadabhidhānaṃ sa virodhaḥ । jātiścaturbhijātyādyairviruddhā syādguṇaistribhiḥ ।।
kriyā dvābhyāmapi dravyaṃ dravyeṇaiveti te daśa । {abhinavanalinīkisalayamṛṇālavalayādi davadahanarāśiḥ । subhaga kuraṅgadṛśosyā vidhivaśatastvadviyogapavipāte ।।} {girayo apyanunnatiyujo marudapyacalobdhayo apyagambhīrāḥ ।
viśvaṃbharāpyatilaghurnaranātha tavāntike niyatam ।।} tīkṣṇaḥ so apyanurajyate ca kamapi snehaṃ parāpnoti ca । pāṃsūnāṃ paṭalaiḥ prasādhanavidhirnirvartyate kautukam ।।} {sṛjati ca jagadidamavati ca saṃharati ca helayaiva yo niyatam ।
avasaravaśataḥ śapharo janārdanaḥ so api citramidam ।।} {satataṃ musalāsaktā bahutaragṛhakarmaghaṭanayā nṛpate । dvijapatnīnāṃ kaṭhināḥ sati bhavati karāḥ sarojasukumārāḥ ।।} {peśalamapi khalavacanaṃ dahatitarāṃ mānasaṃ sattattvavidām ।
paruṣamapi sujanavākyaṃ malayajarasavat pramodayati ।।} {kauñcādriruddāmadṛṣaddṛḍhosau yanmārgaṇānargalaśātapāte । abhūnnavāmbhojadalābhijātaḥ sa bhārgavaḥ satyamapūrvasargaḥ ।।} punarjanmanyasminnanubhavapathaṃ yo na gatavān ।
vikāraḥ ko apyantarjaḍayati ca tāpaṃ ca kurute ।।} śritosmābhistṛṣṇātaralitamanobhirjalanidhiḥ । kṣaṇādenaṃ tāmyattimimakaramāpāsyati muniḥ ।।} {samadamataṅgajamadajalanisyandataraṅgiṇīpariṣvaṅgāt ।
kṣititilaka tvayi taṭajuṣi śaṅkaracūḍāpagāpi kālindī ।।} svabhāvoktistu ḍimbhādeḥ svakriyārūpavarṇanam ।। svayostadekāśrayoḥ । rūpaṃ varṇaḥ saṃsthānaṃ ca । udāharaṇam āsajyābhugnakaṇṭho mukhamurasi saṭāṃ dhūlidhūbhrāṃ vidhūya ।
mandaṃ śabdāyamāno vilikhati śayanādutthitaḥ kṣmāṃ khureṇa ।।} ।। vyājastutirmukhe nindā stutirvā rūḍhiranyathā । vyājarūpā vyājena vā stutiḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam
lajjāvarjanamantareṇa na ramāmanyatra saṃdṛśyate । prāpya tyāgakṛtāvamānanamapi tvayyeva yasyāḥ sthitiḥ ।।} nāsti tvatsadṛśaḥ paraḥ parahitādhāne gṛhītavrataḥ । bhāraprodvahane karoṣi kṛpayā sāhāyakaṃ yanmaroḥ ।।}
sā sahoktiḥ sahārthasya balādekaṃ dvivācakam ।। ekārthābhidhāyakamapi sahārthabalāt yat ubhayasyāpyavagamakaṃ sā sahoktiḥ । yathā saha maṇivalayeṃhi bāhadhārā galanti । saha a taṇuladāe dubbalā jīvidāsā ।।}
saha maṇibalayairvāṣpadhārā galanti । saha ca tanulatayā durbalā jīvitāśā ।।] śvāsadaṇḍādigataṃ dīrghatvādi śābdam divasaniśādigataṃ tu sahārthasāmarthyātpratipadyate ।। vinoktiḥ sā vinānyena yatrānyaḥ sanna netaraḥ ।
kvacidaśobhanaḥ kvacicchobhanaḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam {arucirniśayā vinā śaśī śaśinā sāpi vinā mahattamaḥ । ubhayena vinā manobhavasphuritaṃ naiva cakāsti kāminoḥ ।।} {mṛgalocanayā vinā vicitracvyavahārapratibhāprabhāpragalbhaḥ ।
amṛtadyutisundarāśayo ayaṃ suhṛdā tena vinā narendrasūnuḥ ।।} parivṛttirvinimayo yo arthānāṃ syātsamāsamaiḥ ।। parivṛttiralaṅkāraḥ । udāharaṇam mataṃ lāsyaṃ dattvā śrayati bhṛśamāmodamasamam ।
dadatyādhivyādhibhramiruditamohavyatikaram ।।} atra prathamerghe samena samasya dvitīye uttamene nyūnasya । svīkṛtya dāruṇaninādavataḥ prahārān । nirvipralambhaparirambhavidhirvitīrṇā ।।}
atra nyūnenottamasya ।। pratyakṣā iva yadbhāvāḥ kriyante bhūtabhāvinaḥ । bhūtāśca bhāvinaśceti dvandvaḥ । bhāvaḥ kaverabhiprāyo atrāstīti bhāvikam । udāharaṇam {āsīdañjanamatreti paśyāmi tava locane ।
bhāvibhūṣaṇasaṃbhārāṃ sākṣātkurve tavākṛtim ।।} ādye bhūtasya dvitīye bhāvino darśanam ।। kāvyaliṅgaṃ hetorvākyapadārthatā ।। purāre na prāyaḥ kvacidapi bhavantaṃ praṇatavān ।
maheśa kṣantavyaṃ tadidamaparādhadvayamapi ।।} lalitaśirīṣapuṣpahananairapi tāmyati yat । patatu śirasyakāṇḍayamadaṇḍa ivaiṣa bhujaḥ ।।} hā sopānaparaṃparāṃ girisutākāntālayālaṅkṛtiṃ ।
lokocchedini mokṣanāmani mahāmohe nidhīyāmahe ।।} eṣu aparādhadvaye pūrvāparajanmanoranamanam bhujapāte śastropakṣepaḥ mahāmohe sukhāvalokoccheditvaṃ ca yathākramamuktarūpo hetuḥ ।। paryāyoktaṃ vinā vācyavācakatvena yadvacaḥ । vācyavācakabhāvavyatiriktenāvagamanavyāpāreṇa yat pratipādanaṃ tat paryāyeṇa bhaṅgyantareṇa kathanāt paryāyoktam । udāharaṇam
{yaṃ prekṣya cirarūḍhāpi nivāsaprītirujjhatā । madenairāvaṇamukhe mānena hṛdaye hareḥ ।।} atra airāvaṇaśakrau madamānamuktau jātāviti vyaṅgyamapi śabdenocyate । tena yadevocyate tadeva vyaṅgyam । yathā tu vyaṅgyaṃ na tathocyate । yathā gavi śukle calati dṛṣṭe {gauḥ śuklaścalati} iti vikalpaḥ । yadeva dṛṣṭaṃ tadeva vikalpayati na tu yathā dṛṣṭaṃ tathā । yato abhinnāsaṃsṛṣṭatvena dṛṣṭam bhedasaṃsargābhyāṃ vikalpayati ।।
saṃpat samṛddhiyogaḥ । yathā prātaḥ prāṅgaṇasīmni mantharacaladbālāṅghrilākṣāruṇāḥ । yadvidvadbhavaneṣu bhojanṛpatestat tyāgalīlāyitam ।।} mahatāṃ copalakṣaṇam ।।
upalakṣaṇamaṅgabhāvaḥ arthādupalakṣaṇīye arthe । udāharaṇam {tadidamaraṇyaṃ yasmin daśarathavacanānupālanavyasanī । nivasan bāhusahāyaścakāra rakṣaḥkṣayaṃ rāmaḥ ।।} na cātra vīro rasaḥ tasyehāṅgatvāt ।।
tatsiddhihetāvekasmin yatrānyattatkaraṃ bhavet । tasya prastutasya kāryasya ekasmin sādhake sthite sādhakāntarāṇi yatra saṃbhavanti sa samuccayaḥ । udāharaṇam gāḍhaṃ prema navaṃ vayotikaṭhināḥ prāṇāḥ kulaṃ nirmalam । no sakhyaścaturāḥ kathaṃ nu virahaḥ soḍhavya itthaṃ śaṭhaḥ ।।}
atra virahāsahatvaṃ smaramārgaṇā eva kurvanti । tadupari priyatamadūrasthityādi upāttam ।। eṣa eva samuccayaḥ sadyoge asadyoge sadasadyoge ca paryavasyatīti na pṛthak lakṣyate । tathāhi bhujabalamalaṃ sphītā lakṣmīḥ prabhutvamakhaṇḍitam । vrajati sutarāṃ darpaṃ rājan ta eva tavāṅkuśāḥ ।।}
atra satāṃ yogaḥ । uktodāharaṇe tvasatāṃ yogaḥ । saro vigatavārikaṃ mukhamanakṣaraṃ svākṛteḥ । nṛpāṅgaṇagataḥ khalo manasi sapta śalyāni me ।।} atra śaśini dhūsare śalye śalyāntarāṇīti śobhanāśobhanayogaḥ ।।
sa tvanyo yugapad yā guṇakriyāḥ ।। guṇau ca kriye ca guṇakriye ca guṇakriyāḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam {vidalitasakalārikulaṃ tava balamidamabhavadā‘u vimalaṃ ca । prakhalamukhāni narādhipa malināni ca tāni jātāni ।।}
{ayamekapade tayā viyogaḥ prayayā copanataḥ suduḥsaho me । navavāridharodayādahobhirbhavitavyaṃ ca nirātapatvaramyaiḥ ।।} {kaluṣaṃ ca tavāhiteṣvakasmātsitapaṅkeruhasodaraśri cakṣuḥ । patitaṃ ca mahīpatīndra teṣāṃ vapuṣi prasphuṭamāpadāṃ kaṭākṣaiḥ ।।}
{dhunoti cāsiṃ tanute ca kīrtim} ityādeḥ {kṛpāṇapāṇiśca bhavān raṇakṣitau sasādhuvādāśca surāḥ surālaye} ityādeśca darśanāt {vyadhikaraṇe} iti {ekasmin deśe} iti ca na vācyam ।। ekaṃ vastu krameṇānekasmin bhavati kriyate vā sa paryāyaḥ । krameṇodāharaṇam kenottarottaraviśiṣṭapadopadiṣṭā । kaṇṭhedhunā vasasi vāci punaḥ khalānām ।।}
{bimboṣṭa eva rāgaste tanvi pūrvamadṛśyata । adhunā hṛdaye apyeṣa mṛgaśāvākṣi lakṣyate ।।} rāgasya vastuto bhede apyekatayādhyavasitatvādekatvamaviruddham । {taṃ tāṇa sirisahoararaaṇāharaṇammi hiaamekkarasaṃ ।
bimbāhare piāṇaṃ ṇivesiaṃ kusumabāṇeṇa ।।} [tatteṣāṃ śrīsahodararatnābharaṇe hṛdayamekarasam । vimbādhare priyāṇāṃ niveśitaṃ kusumabāṇena ।।] anyastato anyathā ।
anekamekasmin krameṇa bhavati kriyate vā so anyaḥ ।। {madhurimaruciraṃ vacaḥ khalānāmamṛtamaho prathamaṃ pṛthu vyanakti । atha kathayati mohahetumantargatamiva hālahalaṃ viṣaṃ tadeva ।।} sā dhenurjaratī nadamti kariṇāmetā ghanābhā ghaṭāḥ ।
āścaryaṃ divasairdvijoyamiyatīṃ bhūmiṃ samāropitaḥ ।।} atra ekasyaiva hānopādānayoravivakṣitatvāt na parivṛttiḥ ।। anumānaṃ taduktaṃ yat sādhyasādhanayorvacaḥ ।। pakṣadharmānvayavyatirekitvena trirūpo hetuḥ sādhanam । dharmiṇi ayogavyavacchedo vyāpakasya sādhyatvam । yathā
yat tatraiva patanti saṃtatamamī marmaspṛśo mārgaṇāḥ । dhāvatyagrata eva śāsanadharaḥ satyaṃ sadāsāṃ smaraḥ ।।} sādhyasādhanyoḥ paurvāparyavikalpe ne kiñcidvaicitryamiti na tathā darśitam ।। viśeṣaṇairyatsākūtairuktiḥ parikarastu saḥ ।
arthādviśeṣyasya । udāharaṇam dhanurbhṛtaḥ saṃyati labdhakīrtayaḥ । priyāṇi vāñchantyasubhiḥ samīhitum ।।} yadyapyuṣṭārthasya doṣatābhidhānāttannirākaraṇena puṣṭārthasvīkāraḥ kṛtaḥ tathāpyekaniṣṭhatvena bahunāṃ viśeṣaṇānāmevamupanyāse vaicitryam ityalaṅkāramadhye gaṇitaḥ ।।
vyājoktiśchadmanodbhinnavasturūpanigūhanam ।। nigūḍhamapi vastuno rūpaṃ kathamapi prabhinnaṃ kenāpi vyapadeśena yadapahnūyate sā vyājoktiḥ । na caiṣāpahnutiḥ prakṛtāprakṛto abhayaniṣṭhasya sāmyasyehāsaṃbhavāt । udāharaṇam romāñcādivisaṃṣṭhulākhilavidhivyāsaṅgabhaṅgākulaḥ ।
śailāntaḥpuramātṛmaṇḍalagaṇairdṛṣṭo avatādvaḥ śivaḥ ।।} kiñcit pṛṣṭamapṛṣṭaṃ vā kathitaṃ yat prakalpate । tādṛganyavyapohāya parisaṃkhyā tu sā smṛtā ।। pramānāntarāvagatamapi vastu śabdena pratipāditaṃ prayojanāntarābhāvāt sadṛśavastvanataravyavacchedāya yat paryavasyati sā bhavetparisaṃkhyā । atra ca kathanaṃ praśnapūrvakaṃ tadanyathā ca paridṛṣṭam ।
tathā ubhayatra vyapohyamānasya pratīyamānatā vācyatvaṃ ceti catvāro bhedāḥ ।। krameṇodāharaṇam kimekānte dhyeyaṃ caraṇayugalaṃ kaustubhabhṛtaḥ । yadāsaktyā ceto niravadhivimuktyai prabha[v]ati ।।} kiṃ kāryamāryacaritaṃ sukṛtaṃ na doṣaḥ ।
jānāti kastvadadaparaḥ sadasadvivekam ।।} {kauṭilyaṃ kacanicaye karacaraṇādharadaleṣu rāgaste । kāṭhinyaṃ kucayugale taralatvaṃ nayanayorvasati ।।} {bhaktirbhave na vibhave vyasanaṃ śāstre na yuvatikāmāstre ।
cintā yaśasi na vapuṣi prāyaḥ paridṛśyate mahatām ।।} ।। yathottaraṃ cet pūrvasya pūrvasyārthasya hetutā । uttaramuttaraṃ prati yathottaram । udāharaṇam
{jitendriyatvaṃ vinayasya kāraṇaṃ guṇaprakarṣo vinayādavāpyate । guṇaprakarṣeṇa jano anurajyate janānurāgaprabhavā hi saṃpadaḥ ।।} {hetumatā saha hetoravhidhānamabhedayo hetuḥ ।} iti hetvalaṅkāro na lakṣitaḥ । āyurdhṛtamityādirūpo hyeṣa na bhūṣaṇatāṃ kadācidarhati vaicitryābhāvāt ।
{aviralakamalavikāsaḥ sakalālimadaśca kokilānandaḥ । ramyo ayameti saṃprati lokotkaṇṭhākaraḥ kālaḥ ।।} ityatra kāvyarūpatāṃ komalānuprāsamahimnaiva samāmnāsiṣurna punarhetvalaṅkārakalpanayeti pūrvoktakāvyaliṅgameva hetuḥ ।। kriyayā tu parasparam ।।
arthayorekakriyāmukhena parasparaṃ kāraṇatve sati anyonyanāmā alaṅkāraḥ । udāharaṇam {haṃsāṇaṃ sarehiṃ sirī sārijjai aha sarāṇa haṃsehiṃ । aṇṇoṇṇaṃ via ee appāṇṇaṃ ṇavara garuanti ।।} [haṃsānāṃ sarobhiḥ śrīḥ sāryate atha sarasāṃ haṃsaiḥ ।
anyonyameva ete ātmānaṃ kevalaṃ garayanti ।।] atrobhayeṣānapi parasparajanakatā mithaḥ śrīsāratāsaṃpādanadvāreṇa ।। uttaraśrutimātrataḥ । praśnasyonnayanaṃ yatra kriyate tatra vā sati ।।
asakṛd yadasaṃbhāvyamuttaraṃ syāt taduttaram । prativacanopalambhādeva pūrvavākyaṃ yatra kalpyate tadekaṃ tāvaduttaram । udāharaṇam {vāṇiaa hatthidantā kutto amhāṇa vagdhakittī a । jāva luliālaamuhī dharammi parisakkae soṇhā ।।}
[vāṇijaka hastidantāḥ kuto asmākaṃ vyāghrakṛtayaśca । yāvat lulitālakamukhī gṛhe pariṣvakkate snuṣā ।।] hastidantavyāghrakṛttīnāmahamarthī tāḥ mūlyena prayaccheti kreturvacanam amunā vākyena samunnīyata ।। na caitat kāvyaliṅgam uttarasya tādrūpyānupapatteḥ । nahi praśnasya prativacanaṃ janako hetuḥ । nāpīdamanumānam ekadharminiṣṭhatayā sādyasādhanayoranirdeśādityalaṅkārāntaramevottaraṃ sādhīyaḥ ।
praśnādanantaraṃ lokātikrāntagocaratayā yat asaṃbhāvyarūpaṃ prativacanaṃ syāt tat aparamuttaram । anayośca sakṛdupādāne na cārutāpratītirityasakṛdityuktam । udāharaṇam {kā visamā devvagari kiṃ labdhaṃ jaṃ jaṇo guṇggāhī । kiṃ sokkhaṃ sukalattaṃ kiṃ dukkhaṃ jaṃ khalo loo ।।} [kā viṣamā daivagatiḥ kiṃ labdhavyaṃ yat jano guṇagrāhī ।
kiṃ saukhyaṃ sukalatraṃ kiṃ duḥkhaṃ yat khalo lokaḥ ।।] praśnaparisaṃkhyāyāmanyavyapohe eva tātparyam । iha tu vācye eva viśrāntirityanayorvivekaḥ ।। kuto api lakṣitaḥ sūkṣmo apyartho anyasmai prakāśyate ।। dharmeṇa kenacid yatra tat sūkṣmaṃ paricakṣate ।
kuto api ākārādiṅgitādvā sūkṣmastīkṣṇamatisaṃvedyaḥ ।। {vaktrasyandisvedabinduprabandhairdṛṣṭvā bhinnaṃ kuṅkumaṃ kāpi kaṇṭhe । puṃstvaṃ tanvyā vyañjayantī vayasyā smitvā pāṇau khaḍgalekhāṃ lilekha ।।} atra ākṛtimavalokya kayāpi vitarkitaṃ puruṣāyitam asilatālekhanena vaidagdhyādabhivyaktimupanītam puṃsāmeva kṛpāṇapāṇitā yogyatvāt ।।
{saṃketakālamanasaṃ viṭam jñātvā vidagdhayā । īṣannetrārpitākūtaṃ līlāpadmaṃ nimīlitam ।।} atra jijñāsitaḥ saṃketakālaḥ kayācidiṅgitamātreṇa vidito niśāsamayaśaṃsinā kamalanimīlanena līlayā pratipāditaḥ ।। uttarottaramutkarṣo bhavetsāraḥ parāvadhiḥ ।।
paraḥ paryantabhāgaḥ avadhiryasya dhārādhirohitayā tatraivotkarṣasya viśrānteḥ । udāharaṇam {rājye sāraṃ vasudhā vasudhāyāṃ puraṃ pure saudham । saudhe talpaṃ talpe varāṅganānaṅgasarvasvam ।।} ।।
bhinnadeśatayātyantaṃ kāryakāraṇabhūtayoḥ । yugapaddharmayoryatra khyātiḥ sā syādasaṃgatiḥ ।। iha yaddeśaṃ karaṇaṃ taddeśameva kāryamutpadyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam yathā dhūmādi । yatra tu hetuphalarūpayorapi dharmayoḥ kenāpyatiśayena nānādeśatayā yugapadavabhāsanaṃ sā tayoḥ svabhāvotpannaparasparasaṃgatityāgāt asaṃgatiḥ । udāharaṇam {jassea vaṇo tassea veaṇā bhaṇai taṃ jaṇo aliaṃ ।
dantakkhaaṃ kavole bahue veaṇā savattīṇaṃ ।।} [yasyaiva vraṇastasyaiva vedanā bhaṇati tajjano alīkam । dantakṣataṃ kapole vadhvāḥ vedanā sapatnīnām ।।] eṣā ca virodhabādhinī na virodhaḥ bhinnādharatayaiva dvayoriha virodhitāyāḥ pratibhāsāt । virodhe tu virodhitvam ekāśrayaniṣṭamanuktamapi paryavasitam apavādaviṣayaparihāreṇotsargasya vyavasthiteḥ । tathā caivaṃ nidarśitam ।।
samādhiḥ sukaraṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇāntarayogataḥ । sādhanāntaropakṛtena kartrā yat akleśena kāryamārabdhaṃ samādhīyate sa samādhirnāma । udāharaṇam {mānamasyā nirākartuṃ pādayorme patiṣyataḥ । upakārāya diṣṭyedamudīrṇaṃ ghanagarjitam ।।}
samaṃ yogyatayā yogo yadi saṃbhāvitaḥ kvacit ।। idamanayoḥ ślāghyamiti yogyatayā saṃbandhasya niyataviṣayamadhyavasānaṃ cettadā samam tat sadyoge asadyoge ca ।। rūpe devo apyayamanupamo dattapatraḥ smarasya । cchṛṅgārasyopanatamadhunā rājyamekātapatram ।।}
jāto daivāducitaracanāsaṃvidhātā vidhātā । yaccaitasyāḥ kavalanakalākovidaḥ kākalokaḥ ।।} kvacidyadativaidharmyānna śleṣo ghaṭanāmiyāt । kartuḥ kriyāphalāvāptirnaivānarthaśca yadbhavet ।।
guṇakriyābhyāṃ kāryasya kāraṇasya guṇakriye । krameṇa ca viruddhe yat sa eṣa viṣamo mataḥ ।। dvayoratyantavilakṣaṇatayā yat anupapadyamānatayaiva yogaḥ pratīyate yacca kiñcidārabhamāṇaḥ kartā kriyāyāḥ praṇāśāt na kevalamabhīṣṭaṃ yat phalaṃ na labhet yāvadaprārthitamapyanarthaṃ viṣayamāsādayet tathā satyapi kāryasya kāraṇarūpānukāre tat tayorguṇau kriye ca parasparaṃ viruddhatāṃ vrajataḥ sa samaviparyayātmā catūrūpo viṣamaḥ ।। {śirīṣādapi mṛdvaṅgī kveyamāyatalocanā ।
ayaṃ kva ca kukūlāgnikarkaśo madanānalaḥ ।।} {siṃhikāsutasaṃtrastaḥ śaśaḥ śītāṃśumāśritaḥ । jagrase sāśrayaṃ tatra tamanyaḥ siṃhikāsutaḥ ।।} {sadyaḥkarasparśamavāpya citraṃ raṇe raṇe yasya kṛpāṇalekhā ।
tamālanīlā śaradindupāṇḍu yaśastrilokyābharaṇaṃ prasūte ।।} {ānandamamandamimaṃ kuvalayadalalocane dadāsi tvam । virahastvayaiva janitastāpayatitarāṃ śarīraṃ me ।।} atrānandadānaṃ śarīratāpena virudhyate ।
{vipulena sāgaraśayasya kukṣiṇā bhuvanāni yasya papire yugakṣaye । madavibhramāsakalayā pape punaḥ sa purastriyaikatamayaikayā dṛśā ।।} ityādāvapi viṣamatvaṃ yathāyogabhavagantavyam ।। mahatoryanmahīyāṃsāvāśritāśrayayoḥ kramāt ।
āśrayāśrayiṇau syātāṃ tanutve apyadhikaṃ tu tat ।। āśritam ādheyam āśrayastadādhāraḥ । tayormahatorapi viṣaye tadapekṣayā tanū apyāśrayāśrayiṇau prastutavastuprakarṣaviavkṣayā yathākramaṃ yat adhikataratāṃ vrajataḥ । tadidaṃ dvividham adhikaṃ nāma । {aho viśālaṃ bhūpāla bhuvanatritayodaram । māti mātumaśakyo api yaśorāśiryadatra te ।।}
{yugāntakālapratisaṃhṛtātmano jaganti yasyāṃ savikāśamāsata । tanau manustatra na kaiṭabhadviṣastapodhanābhyāgamasaṃbhavā mudaḥ ।।} ।। pratipakṣamaśaktena pratikartuṃ tiraskriyā ।
yā tadīyasya tatstutyai pratyanīkaṃ taducyate ।। nyakkṛtiparamapi vipakṣaṃ sākṣānnirasitumaśaktena kenāpi yat tameva pratipakṣamutkarṣayituṃ tadāśritasya tiraskaraṇam tat anīkapratinidhitulyatvāt pratyanīkamabhidhīyate । yathā anīke abhiyojye tatpratinidhībhūtamaparaṃ mūḍhatayā kenacidabhiyujyate tatheha pratiyogini vijeye tadīyonyo vijīyate ityarthaḥ । udāharaṇam {tvaṃ vinirjitamanobhavarūpaḥ sā ca sundara bhavatyanuraktā । pañcabhiryugapadeva śaraistāṃ tāpayatyanuśayādiva kāmaḥ ।।}
{yasya kiñcidapakartumakṣamaḥ kāyanigrahagṛhītavigrahaḥ । kāntavaktrasadṛśākṛtiṃ kṛtī rāhurindumadhunāpi bādhate ।।} indoratra tadīyatā saṃbandhisaṃbandhāt ।। samena lakṣmaṇā vastu vastunā yannigūhyate ।
nijenāgantunā vāpi tanmīlitamiti smṛtam ।। sahajam āgantukaṃ vā kimapi sādhāraṇaṃ yat lakṣaṇam taddvāreṇa yat kiñcit kenacidvastu vastusthityaiva valīyastayā tirodhīyate tat mīlitamiti dvidhā smaranti ।। vilāsabharamantharā gatiratīva kāntaṃ mukham । tadatra na madodayaḥ kṛtapado api saṃlakṣyate ।।}
atra dṛktaralatādikamaṅgasya liṅgaṃ svābhāvikaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ ca mahodayena tatrāpyetasya darśanāt । tvatpātaśaṅkitadhiyo vivaśā dviṣaste । teṣāmaho bata bhiyāṃ na budho apyabhijñaḥ ।।} atra tu sāmarthyādavasitasya śaityasya āgantukatvāttatprabhavayorapi kampapulakayostādrūpyaṃ samānatā ca bhayeṣvapi tayorupalakṣitatvāt ।।
sthāpyatepohyate vāpi yathāpūrvaṃ paraṃ param । viśeṣaṇatayā yatra vastu saikāvalī dvidhā ।। pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ prati yathottarasya vastuno vīpsayā viśeṣaṇabhāvena yat sthāpanaṃ niṣedho vā saṃbhavati sā dvidhā budhairekāvalī bhaṇyate । krameṇodāharaṇam {purāṇi yasyāṃ savarāṅganāni varāṅganā rūpapuraskṛtāṅgyaḥ ।
rūpaṃ samunmīlitasadvilāsamastraṃ vilāsaḥ kusumāyudhasya ।।} napaṅkajaṃ tad yadalīnaṣaṭpadam । na guñjitaṃ tanna jahāra yanmanaḥ ।।} pūrvatra purāṇāṃ varāṅganāḥ tāsāmaṅgaviśeṣaṇamukhena rūpam tasya vilāsāḥ teṣāmapyastramityamunā krameṇa viśeṣaṇaṃ vidhīyate । uttaratra pratiṣedhe apyevaṃ yojyam ।।
yathānubhavamarthasya dṛṣṭe tatsadṛśe smṛtiḥ । yaḥ padārthaḥ kenacidākāreṇa niyataḥ yadā kadācit anubhūto abhūt sa kālāntare smṛtipratibodhādhāyini tatsamāne vastuni dṛṣṭe sati yat tathaiva smaryate tat bhavet smaraṇam । udāharaṇam {nimnanābhikuhareṣu yadambhaḥ plāvitaṃ caladṛśāṃ laharībhiḥ । tadbhavaiḥ kuharutaiḥ suranāryaḥ smāritā suratakaṇṭharutānām ।।}
{karajuagahiajasoātthaṇamuhaviṇivesiāharapuḍassa । samariapañcajaṇṇassa ṇamaha kaṇhassa romāñcaṃ ।।} [karayugagṛhītayaśodāstanamukhaviniveśitādharapuṭasya । saṃsmṛtapāñcajanyasya namata kṛṣṇasya romāñcam ।।]
bhrāntimānanyasaṃvittattulyadarśane ।। taditi anyat aprākaraṇikaṃ nirdiśyate । tena samānam arthādiha prākaraṇikam āśrīyate । tasya tathāvidhasya dṛṣṭau satyāṃ yat aprākaraṇikatayā saṃvedanaṃ sa bhrāntimān । na caiṣa rūpakaṃ prathamātiśayoktirvā tatra vastuto bhramasyābhāvāt iha ca, arthānugamanena saṃjñāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tasya spaṣṭameva pratipannatvāt । udāharaṇam tarucchidraprotān bisamiti karī saṃkalayati ।
prabhāmattaścandro jagadidamaho viplavayati ।।} ākṣepa upamānasya pratīpamupameyatā । tasyaiva yadi vā kalpyā tiraskāranibandhanam ।। asya dhuraṃ sutarāmupameyameva voḍhuṃ prauḍhamiti kaimarthyena yat upamānamākṣipyate yadapi tasyaivopamānatayā prasiddhasya upamānāntaravivakṣayānādarārthamupameyabhāvaḥ kalpyate tat upameyasyopamānapratikūlavartitvāt ubhyarūpaṃ pratīpam । krameṇodāharaṇam
deva tvayyavanībharakṣamabhuje niṣpādite vedhasā । cintāratnamado mudhaiva kimamī sṛṣṭāḥ kulakṣmābhṛtaḥ ।।} {e ehi dāva sundari kaṇṇaṃ dāūṇa suṇasu vaaṇijjaṃ । tujjha muheṇa kisoari cando uamijjai jaṇeṇa ।।}
[ayi ehi tāvat sundari karṇandattvā śṛṇuṣva vacanīyam । tava mukhena kṛśodari candra upamīyate janena ।।] atra mukhenopamīyamānasya śaśinaḥ svalpataraguṇatvāt upamityaniṣpattyā avaaṇijjaṃ'; iti vacanīyapadābhivyaṅgyastiraskāraḥ । kkacittu niṣpannaivopamitikriyā anādaranibandhanam । yathā
{garvamasaṃvāhyamimaṃ locranayugalena kiṃ vahasi mugdhe । santīdṛśāni diśi diśi sarassu nanu nīlanalināni ।।} ihopameyīkaraṇamevotpalānāmanādaraḥ । anayaiva rītyā yat asāmānyaguṇayogāt nopamānabhāvamapi anubhūtapūrvi tasya tatkalpanāyāmapi bhavati pratīpamiti pratyetavyam । yathā
iti hālāhala tāta mā sma dṛpyaḥ । bhuvanesmin vacanāni durjanānām ।।} atra hālāhalasyopamānatvamasaṃbhāvyamevopanibaddham ।। prastutasya yadanyena guṇasāmyavivakṣayā ।
aikātmyaṃ badhyate yogāttatsāmānyamiti smṛtam ।। atādṛśamapi tādṛśatayā vivakṣituṃ yat aprastutārthena saṃpṛktamaparityaktanijaguṇameva tadekātmatayā nibadhyate tat samānaguṇanibandhanāt sāmānyam । udāharaṇam sitataradantapatra kṛtavaktraruco rucirāmalāṃśukāḥ । śaśabhṛti vitatadhāmni dhavalayati dharāmavibhāvyatāṃ gatāḥ ।
priyavasatiṃ prayānti sukhameva nirastabhiyo abhisārikāḥ ।।} atra prastutatadanyayoranyūnānatiriktatayā nibaddhaṃ dhavalatvamekātmatāhetuḥ । ata eva pṛthagbhāvena na tayorupalakṣaṇam । yathā vā {vetratvacā tulyarucāṃ cadhūnāṃ karṇāgrato gaṇḍatalāgatāni । bhṛṅgā sahelaṃ yadi nāpatiṣyan kovedayiṣyannavacampakāni ।।}
atra nimittāntarajanitāpi nānātvapratītiḥ prathamapratipannamabhedaṃ na vyudsitumutsahate pratītatvāttasya pratīteśca bādhāyogāt ।। vinā prasiddhamādhāramādheyasya vyavasthitiḥ । ekātmā yagapaddṛttirekasyānekagocarā ।। anyat prakurvataḥ kāryamaśakyasyānyavastunaḥ ।
tathaiva karaṇaṃ ceti viśeṣastrividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। prasiddhārdhaparihāreṇa yat ādheyasya viśiṣṭā sthitirabhidhīyate sa prathamo viśeṣaḥ । {divamapyupayātānāmākalpamanalpaguṇagaṇā yeṣām । ramayanti jaganti giraḥ kathamiha kavayo na te vandyāḥ ।।}
evamapi vastu yat ekenaiva svabhāvena yugapadanekatra vartate sa dvitīyaḥ । udāharaṇam {sā vasai tujjha hiae sā ccia acchīsu sā a vaaṇesu । ahmārisāṇa sundara osāso kattha pāvāṇaṃ ।।} [sā vasati tava hṛdaye saivākṣiṣu sā ca vacaneṣu ।
asmādṛśīnāṃ sundara avakāśaḥ kutra pāpānām ।।] yadyapi kiñcidrabhasena ārabhamāṇastenaiva yatnenāśakyamapi kāryāntaramārabhate soparo viśeṣaḥ । udāharaṇam {sphuradadbhutarūpamutpratāpajvalanaṃ tvāṃ sṛjatānavadyavidyam । vidhinā sasṛje navo manobhūrbhuvisatyaṃ savitā vṛhaspatiśca ।।}
{gṛhiṇī sacivaḥ sakhī mithaḥ priyaśiṣyā lalite kalāvidhau । karuṇāvimukhena mṛtyunā haratā tvāṃ bata kiṃ na me hṛtam ।।} sarvatra evaṃvidhaviṣaye atiśayoktireva prāṇatvenāvatiṣṭhate tāṃ vinā prāueṇālaṅkāratvāyogāt । ata evoktam {saiṣā sarvatra vakroktiranayārtho vibhāvyate ।
yatnosyāṃ kavinā kāryaḥ ko alaṅkāro anayā vinā ।। svamutsṛjya guṇaṃ yogādatyujjvalaguṇasya yat । vastu tadguṇatāmeti bhaṇyate sa tu tadguṇaḥ ।। vastu tiraskṛtanijarūpaṃ kenāpi samīpagatena praguṇayā svaguṇasaṃpadoparaktaṃ tatpratibhāsameva yatsamāsādayati sa tadguṇaḥ । tasyāprakṛtasya guṇotrāstīti । udāharaṇam
{vibhinnavarṇā garuḍāgrajena sūryasya rathyāḥ paritaḥ sphurantyā । ratnaiḥ punaryatra rucā rucaṃ svāmāninyire vaṃśakarīranīlaiḥ ।।} atra ravituragāpekṣayā garuḍāgrajasya tadapekṣayā ca harinmaṇīnāṃ praguṇavarṇatā ।। tadrūpānanuhāraścedasya tat syādatadguṇaḥ ।
yadi tu tadīyaṃ varṇaṃ saṃbhavantyāmapi yogyatāyām idaṃ nyūnaguṇaṃ na gṛhaṇīyāt tadā bhavedatadguṇo nāma । udāharaṇam {dhavalosi jahavi sundara taha vi tue majjha rañjiaṃ hiaaṃ । rāabharievi hiae suhaa ṇihitto ṇa rattosi ।।} [dhvalo asi yadyapi sundara tathāpi tvayā mama rañjitaṃ hṛdayam ।
rāgabharite api hṛdaye subhaga nihito na rakto asi ।।] atrātiraktenāpi manasā saṃyukto na raktatāmupagata ityatadguṇaḥ । kiñca taditi aprakṛtam asyeti ca prakṛtamatra nirdiśyate । tena yat aprakṛtasya rūpaṃ prakṛtena kutp'pi nimittāt nānuvidhīyate so atadaguṇa ityapi pratipattavyam । yathā {gāṅgamambu sitamambu yāmunaṃ kajjalābhamubhayatra majjataḥ ।
rājahaṃsa tava saiva śubhratā cīyate na ca na cāpacīyate ।।} yadyathā sādhitaṃ kenāpyapareṇa tadanyathā ।। tathaiva yadvidhīyeta sa vyāghāta iti smṛtiḥ । yenopāyena yat ekenopakalpitam tasyānyena jigīṣutayā tadupāyakameva yat anyathākaraṇam sa sādhitavastuvyāhatitetutvāt vyāghātaḥ । udāharaṇam
{dṛśā dagdhaṃ manasijaṃ jīvayanti dṛśaiva yāḥ । virūpākṣasya jayinīstāḥ stuve vāmalocanāḥ ।।} seṣṭā saṃsṛṣṭireteṣāṃ bhedena yadiha sthitiḥ ।। eteṣāṃ samanantaramevoktasvarūpāṇāṃ yathāsaṃbhavananyonyanirapekṣatayā yat ekatra śabdabhāge eva arthaviṣaye eva ubhayatrāpi vā avasthānam sā ekārthasamavāyasvabhāvā saṃsṛṣṭiḥ ।
{vadanasaurabhalobhaparibhramadbhramarasaṃbhramasaṃbhṛtaśobhayā । calitayā vidadhe kalamekhalākalakalolakaloladṛśānyayā ।।} {limpatīva tamoṅgāni varṣatīvāñjanaṃ nabhaḥ । asatpuruṣaseveva dṛṣṭirviphalatāṃ gatā ।।}
pūrvatra parasparanirapekṣau yamakānuprāsau saṃsṛṣṭiṃ prayojayataḥ uttaratra tu tathāvidhe upamotprekṣe । śabdārthālaṅkārayostu saṃsṛṣṭiḥ । {so ṇatthi ettha gāme jo eaṃ mahamahantalāaṇṇaṃ । taruṇāṇa hiaalūḍiṃ parisakkantīṃ ṇivārei ।।}
[sa nāstyatra grāme ya enāṃ mahamahāyamānalāvaṇyām । taruṇānāṃ hṛdayaluṇṭhākiṃ pariṣvakkamāṇāṃ nivārayati ।] atrānuprāso rūpakaṃ cānyonyānapekṣe । saṃsargaśca tayorekatra vākye chandasi vā samavetatvāt ।। aviśrāntijuṣāmātmanyaṅgāṅgitvaṃ tu saṃkaraḥ ।
ete eva yatrātmani anāsāditasvatantrabhāvāḥ prasparam anugrāhyānugrāhakatāṃ dadhati sa eṣāṃ saṃkīryamāṇasvarūpatvāt saṃkaraḥ । udāharaṇam luptāyāṃ mekhalāyāṃ jhaṭiti maṇitulākoṭiyugme gṛhīte । rājan guñjāphalānāṃ sraja iti śabarā naiva hāraṃ haranti ।।} atra tadguṇamapekṣya bhrāntimatā prādurbhūtam tadāśrayeṇa ca tadguṇaḥ sacetasāṃ prabhūtacamatkṛtinimittamityanayoraṅgāṅgibhāvaḥ । yathā vā
viyogivyāpatteriva kalitavairāgyaviśadaḥ । śaśī bhasmāpāṇḍuḥ pitṛvana iva vyomni carati ।।} upamā rūpakam utprekṣā śleṣaśceti catvāro atra pūrvavat aṅgāṅgitayā pratīyante । kalaṅka evākṣavalayamiti rūpakaparigrahe karadhṛtatvameva sādhakapramāṇatāṃ pratipadyate । asya hi rūpakatve tirohitakalaṅkarūpam akṣavalayameva mukhyatayāvagamyate tasyaiva ca karagrahaṇayogyatāyāṃ sārvatrikī prasiddhiḥ । śleṣacchāyayā tu kalaṅgasya kalaṅkasya mūrtyaiva udvahanāt । kalaṅko akṣavalayamiveti tu, upamāyāṃ
kalaṅkasya, utkaṭatayā pratipattiḥ । na cāsya karadhṛtatvaṃ tattvatostīti mukhye apyupacāra eva śaraṇaṃ syāt । evaṃrūpaśca saṃkaraḥ śabdālaṅkārayorapi paridṛśyate । yathā {rājati taṭīyamabhihatadānavarāsātipātisārāvanadā । gajatā ca yūthamviratadānavarā sātipāti sārā vanadā ।।}
atra yamakāmanulomapratilomaśca citrabhedaḥ pādadvayagate parasparāpekṣe । ekasya ca grahe nyāyadoṣābhāvādaniścayaḥ ।। dvitīyaḥ saṃkaraḥ samuccayena saṃkarasyaivākṣepāt । udāharaṇam {jaha gahiro jaha raaṇaṇivbharo jaha a ṇimmalacchāo ।
